Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa

# Khuddakanikāye

## Therāpadānapāḷi

#### (Dutiyo bhāgo)

### 43. Sakiṃsammajjakavaggo

#### 1. Sakiṃsammajjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassino <pb ed="T" n="2.0024" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0001" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0001" /> bhagavato, pāṭaliṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Disvāva taṃ pādapaggaṃ, tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Sammajjaniṃ gahetvāna, bodhiṃ sammajji tāvade;
```

```
Sammajjitvāna taṃ bodhiṃ, avandiṃ pāṭaliṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Namassamāno taṃ bodhiṃ, gañchiṃ paṭikuṭiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Tādimaggena <pb ed="V" n="2.0002" /> gacchāmi, saranto bodhimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Ajagaro maṃ pīḷesi, ghorarūpo mahabbalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Āsanne <pb ed="P" n="2.0379" /> me kataṃ kammaṃ, phalena tosayī mamaṃ;
```

```
Kaḷevaraṃ me gilati, devaloke ramāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Anāvilaṃ mama cittaṃ, visuddhaṃ paṇḍaraṃ sadā;
```

```
Sokasallaṃ na jānāmi, cittasantāpanaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Kuṭṭhaṃ gaṇḍo kilāso ca, apamāro vitacchikā;
```

```
Daddu kaṇḍu ca me natthi, phalaṃ sammajjanāyidaṃ <note>sammajjane idaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Soko <pb ed="M" n="2.0002" /> ca paridevo ca, hadaye me na vijjati;
```

```
Abhantaṃ ujukaṃ cittaṃ, phalaṃ sammajjanāyidaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Samādhīsu <pb ed="T" n="2.0025" /> na majjāmi <note>samādhīsu na sajjāmi (sī.), samādhiṃ puna pajjāmi (syā)</note>, visadaṃ hoti mānasaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ yaṃ samādhimicchāmi, so so sampajjate mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Rajanīye na rajjāmi, atho dussaniyesu <note>dosaniyesu (sī. syā. ka.)</note> ca;
```

```
Mohanīye na muyhāmi, phalaṃ sammajjanāyidaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <note>ekanavute ito (sī. syā.)</note> kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phalaṃ sammajjanāyidaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sakiṃsammajjako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sakiṃsammajjakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Ekadussadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="V" n="2.0003" /> haṃsavatiyā, ahosiṃ tiṇahārako;
```

```
Tiṇahārena jīvāmi, tena posemi dārake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Tamandhakāraṃ nāsetvā, uppajji lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Sake <pb ed="T" n="2.0026" /> ghare nisīditvā, evaṃ cintesi tāvade;
```

```
‘Buddho loke samuppanno, deyyadhammo na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0003" /> me sāṭakaṃ ekaṃ, natthi me koci dāyako;
```

```
Dukkho nirayasamphasso, ropayissāmi dakkhiṇaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
```

```
Ekaṃ dussaṃ gahetvāna, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Ekaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0380" /> dussaṃ daditvāna, ukkuṭṭhiṃ sampavattayiṃ;
```

```
‘Yadi buddho tuvaṃ vīra, tārehi maṃ mahāmuni’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mama dānaṃ pakittento, akā me anumodanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā ekadussena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Kappasatasahassāni, vinipātaṃ na gacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘‘Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissasi;
```

```
Tettiṃsakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī <note>cakkavatti (syā.)</note> bhavissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ <note>asaṅkayaṃ (syā. ka.) evamuparipi</note>;
```

```
Devaloke manusse vā, saṃsaranto tuvaṃ bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rūpavā guṇasampanno, anavakkantadehavā <note>anuvattanta… (syā)</note>;
```

```
Akkhobhaṃ amitaṃ dussaṃ, labhissasi yadicchakaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
```

```
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī vīro <note>dhīro (sī. syā.)</note>, haṃsarājāva ambare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0027" /> yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, ekadussassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Paduddhāre <pb ed="V" n="2.0004" /> paduddhāre, dussaṃ nibbattate mamaṃ;
```

```
Heṭṭhā dussamhi tiṭṭhāmi, uparicchadanaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkavāḷaṃ upādāya, sakānanaṃ sapabbataṃ;
```

```
Icchamāno cahaṃ ajja, dussehacchādayeyya taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Teneva ekadussena, saṃsaranto bhavābhave;
```

```
Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo hutvāna, saṃsarāmi bhavābhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Vipākaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0004" /> viekadussassa, nājjhagaṃ katthacikkhayaṃ;
```

```
Ayaṃ me antimā jāti, vipaccati idhāpi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dussamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekadussassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekadussadāyako thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Ekadussadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Ekāsanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="T" n="2.0028" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0381" />, gosito nāma pabbato;
```

```
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Nārado nāma nāmena, kassapo iti maṃ vidū;
```

```
Suddhimaggaṃ gavesanto, vasāmi gosite tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, agañchi anilañjasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Vanagge gacchamānassa, disvā raṃsiṃ mahesino;
```

```
Kaṭṭhamañcaṃ paññāpetvā, ajinañca apatthariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Āsanaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0005" /> paññāpetvāna, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Somanassaṃ paveditvā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sallakatto mahāvīra, āturānaṃ tikicchako;
```

```
Mamaṃ rogaparetassa <note>rāga… (syā.)</note>, tikicchaṃ dehi nāyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kallatthikā ye passanti, buddhaseṭṭha tuvaṃ mune;
```

```
Dhuvatthasiddhiṃ papponti, etesaṃ ajaro <note>jajjaro (sī. pī. ka.)</note> bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na <pb ed="M" n="2.0005" /> me deyyadhammo atthi, pavattaphalabhojihaṃ;
```

```
Idaṃ me āsanaṃ atthi <note>na me deyyaṃ tava atthi (sī. syā.)</note>, nisīda kaṭṭhamañcake’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Nisīdi tattha bhagavā, asambhītova <note>acchambhitova (syā. ka.)</note> kesarī;
```

```
Muhuttaṃ vītināmetvā, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘‘Visaṭṭho <pb ed="T" n="2.0029" /> <note>vissattho (sī. pī), vissaṭṭho (syā. ka.)</note> hohi mā bhāyi, laddho jotiraso tayā;
```

```
Yaṃ tuyhaṃ patthitaṃ sabbaṃ, paripūrissatināgate <note>paripūrissatāsanaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na moghaṃ taṃ kataṃ tuyhaṃ, puññakkhette anuttare;
```

```
Sakkā uddharituṃ attā, yassa cittaṃ paṇīhitaṃ <note>sunīhitaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘‘Imināsanadānena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Kappasatasahassāni, vinipātaṃ na gacchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissasi;
```

```
Asītikkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padesarajjaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0382" /> vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhito hutvā, saṃsāre saṃsarissasi’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
```

```
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī vīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, sarathaṃ sandamānikaṃ;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Kānanaṃ pavisitvāpi, yadā icchāmi āsanaṃ;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, pallaṅko upatiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Vārimajjhagato santo, yadā icchāmi āsanaṃ;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, pallaṅko upatiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0006" /> yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Pallaṅkasatasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Duve <pb ed="T" n="2.0030" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0006" /> bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Duve kule pajāyāmi, khattiye atha brāhmaṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Ekāsanaṃ daditvāna, puññakkhette anuttare;
```

```
Dhammapallaṅkamādāya <note>dhammapallaṅkamaññāya (syā. ka.)</note>, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekāsanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ekāsanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Sattakadambapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre, kukkuṭo <note>kadambo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nāma pabbato;
```

```
Tamhi pabbatapādamhi, satta buddhā vasiṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Kadambaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā, paggahetvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Satta mālā gahetvāna, puññacittena <note>puṇṇacittena (ka.)</note> okiriṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0031" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <pb ed="P" n="2.0383" /> kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0007" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0007" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sattakadambapupphiyo thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sattakadambapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Koraṇḍapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Vanakammiko pure āsiṃ, pitumātumatenahaṃ <note>pitupitāmahenahaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pasumārena jīvāmi, kusalaṃ me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Mama āsayasāmantā, tisso lokagganāyako;
```

```
Padāni tīṇi dassesi, anukampāya cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Akkante ca pade disvā, tissanāmassa satthuno;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, pade cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Koraṇḍaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0032" /> pupphitaṃ disvā, pādapaṃ dharaṇīruhaṃ;
```

```
Sakosakaṃ gahetvāna, padaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Koraṇḍavaṇṇakoyeva, suppabhāso bhavāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, padapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koraṇḍapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Koraṇḍapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Ghatamaṇḍadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Sucintitaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0008" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0008" /> bhagavantaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Upaviṭṭhaṃ mahāraññaṃ, vātābādhena pīḷitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā <pb ed="T" n="2.0033" /> cittaṃ pasādetvā, ghatamaṇḍamupānayiṃ;
```

```
Katattā <pb ed="P" n="2.0384" /> ācitattā ca, gaṅgā bhāgīrathī ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāsamuddā cattāro, ghataṃ sampajjare mama;
```

```
Ayañca pathavī ghorā, appamāṇā asaṅkhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, bhavate madhusakkarā;
```

```
Cātuddīpā <note>catuddisā (syā.)</note> ime rukkhā, pādapā dharaṇīruhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, kapparukkhā bhavanti te;
```

```
Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ghatamaṇḍassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ghatamaṇḍadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ghatamaṇḍadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Ekadhammassavaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0034" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Catusaccaṃ pakāsento, santāresi bahuṃ janaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0009" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0009" /> tena samayena, jaṭilo uggatāpano;
```

```
Dhunanto vākacīrāni, gacchāmi ambare tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhaseṭṭhassa upari, gantuṃ na visahāmahaṃ;
```

```
Pakkhīva selamāsajja, gamanaṃ na labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Udake vokkamitvāna, evaṃ gacchāmi ambare;
```

```
Na me idaṃ bhūtapubbaṃ, iriyāpathavikopanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Handa metaṃ gavesissaṃ, appevatthaṃ labheyyahaṃ;
```

```
Orohanto antalikkhā, saddamassosi satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Sarena rajanīyena, savanīyena vaggunā;
```

```
Aniccataṃ kathentassa, taññeva uggahiṃ tadā;
```

```
Aniccasaññamuggayha<pb ed="P" n="2.0385" />, agamāsiṃ mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatāyuṃ vasitvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ;
```

```
Carime vattamānamhi, saddhammassavanaṃ sariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassāni, devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca<pb ed="T" n="2.0035" />, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Ekavīsatikkhattuñca <note>ekatiṃsati… (syā.)</note>, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Anubhomi sakaṃ puññaṃ, sukhitohaṃ bhavābhave;
```

```
Anussarāmi taṃ saññaṃ, saṃsaranto bhavābhave;
```

```
Na koṭiṃ paṭivijjhāmi, nibbānaṃ accutaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Pitugehe nisīditvā, samaṇo bhāvitindriyo;
```

```
Kathaṃsa <note>kathayaṃ (sī. pī. ka.)</note> paridīpento, aniccatamudāhari.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aniccā vata saṅkhārā, uppādavayadhammino;
```

```
Uppajjitvā nirujjhanti, tesaṃ vūpasamo sukho’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Saha <pb ed="M" n="2.0010" /> gāthaṃ suṇitvāna, pubbasaññamanussariṃ;
```

```
Ekāsane nisīditvā, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā <pb ed="V" n="2.0010" /> sattavassena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ;
```

```
Upasampādayī buddho, dhammassavanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dhammamasuṇiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, dhammassavanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0036" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekadhammassavaniyo thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ekadhammassavaniyattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Sucintitattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, ahosiṃ kassako tadā;
```

```
Kasikammena jīvāmi, tena posemi dārake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Susampannaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0386" /> tadā khettaṃ, dhaññaṃ me phalinaṃ <note>phalitaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> ahu;
```

```
Pākakāle ca sampatte, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Nacchannaṃ nappatirūpaṃ, jānantassa guṇāguṇaṃ;
```

```
Yohaṃ saṅghe adatvāna, aggaṃ bhuñjeyya ce tadā <note>mattanā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ buddho asamasamo, dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
```

```
Tato pabhāvito saṅgho, puññakkhetto anuttaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha dassāmahaṃ dānaṃ, navasassaṃ pure pure;
```

```
Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, haṭṭho pīṇitamānaso <note>pītika… (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Khettato <pb ed="M" n="2.0011" /> dhaññamāhatvā, sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ;
```

```
Upasaṅkamma sambuddhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘‘Navasassañca sampannaṃ, āyāgosi <note>idha hosi (syā.)</note> ca tvaṃ mune;
```

```
Anukampamupādāya<pb ed="T" n="2.0037" />, adhivāsehi cakkhuma’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="V" n="2.0011" /> lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cattāro ca paṭipannā, cattāro ca phale ṭhitā;
```

```
Esa saṅgho ujubhūto, paññāsīlasamāhito;
```

```
Yajantānaṃ manussānaṃ, puññapekkhāna pāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘‘Karotopadhikaṃ puññaṃ, saṅghe dinnaṃ mahapphalaṃ;
```

```
Tasmiṃ saṅgheva <note>saṃghe ca (syā. pī.)</note> dātabbaṃ, tava sassaṃ tathetaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṅghato uddisitvāna, bhikkhū netvāna saṃgharaṃ;
```

```
Paṭiyattaṃ ghare santaṃ, bhikkhusaṅghassa dehi tvaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅghato uddisitvāna, bhikkhū netvāna saṃgharaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ ghare paṭiyattaṃ me, bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ sappabhassaraṃ;
```

```
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
```

Ekūnavīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Ākiṇṇaṃ bhavanaṃ mayhaṃ, nārīgaṇasamākulaṃ;
```

```
Tattha bhutvā pivitvā ca, vasāmi tidase ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Satānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0038" /> tīṇikkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavābhave <pb ed="M" n="2.0012" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0387" /> saṃsaranto, labhāmi amitaṃ dhanaṃ;
```

```
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, sivikaṃ sandamānikaṃ;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ <note>sabbametampi (ka.)</note>, navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Navavatthaṃ navaphalaṃ, navaggarasabhojanaṃ;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Koseyyakambaliyāni<pb ed="V" n="2.0012" />, khomakappāsikāni ca;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Dāsīgaṇaṃ dāsagaṇaṃ, nāriyo ca alaṅkatā;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Na maṃ sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā, pariḷāho na vijjati;
```

```
Atho cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ, hadaye me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ khāda idaṃ bhuñja, imamhi sayane saya;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ pacchimako dāni, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Ajjāpi deyyadhammo me, phalaṃ tosesi sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Navasassaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0039" /> daditvāna, saṅghe gaṇavaruttame;
```

```
Aṭṭhānisaṃse anubhomi, kammānucchavike mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Vaṇṇavā yasavā homi, mahābhogo anītiko;
```

```
Mahāpakkho <note>mahābhakkho (syā. ka.)</note> sadā homi, abhejjapariso sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe maṃ apacāyanti, ye keci pathavissitā;
```

```
Deyyadhammā ca ye keci, pure pure labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhusaṅghassa vā majjhe, buddhaseṭṭhassa sammukhā;
```

```
Sabbepi samatikkamma, denti mameva dāyakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭhamaṃ navasassañhi, datvā saṅghe gaṇuttame;
```

```
Imānisaṃse anubhomi, navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="M" n="2.0013" /> kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, navasassassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sucintito thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sucintitattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Sovaṇṇakiṅkaṇiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhāya <pb ed="T" n="2.0040" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0013" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0388" /> abhinikkhamma, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Vākacīradharo āsiṃ, tapokammamapassito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassī tu bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Uppajji tamhi samaye, tārayanto mahājanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Balañca vata me khīṇaṃ, byādhinā paramena taṃ;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna, puline thūpamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Karitvā haṭṭhacittohaṃ, sahatthena <note>pasādena (ka.)</note> samokiriṃ;
```

```
Soṇṇakiṅkaṇipupphāni, udaggamanaso ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, thūpaṃ paricariṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tena cetopasādena, atthadassissa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘Devalokaṃ gato santo, labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ;
```

```
Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo tatthāsiṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Asītikoṭiyo mayhaṃ, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Sadā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhanti, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni <note>saṭṭhitūriya… (ka.)</note>, bheriyo paṇavāni ca;
```

```
Saṅkhā ca ḍiṇḍimā tattha, vaggū vajjanti <note>nadanti (sī.), vadanti (pī.)</note> dundubhī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni<pb ed="M" n="2.0014" />, hatthino samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Tidhāpabhinnamātaṅgā, kuñjarā saṭṭhihāyanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘Hemajālābhisañchannā<pb ed="T" n="2.0041" />, upaṭṭhānaṃ karonti me;
```

```
Balakāye gaje ceva, ūnatā me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘Soṇṇakiṅkaṇipupphānaṃ, vipākaṃ anubhomahaṃ;
```

```
Aṭṭhapaññāsakkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘Ekasattatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Pathabyā rajjaṃ ekasataṃ, mahiyā kārayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘So dāni amataṃ patto, asaṅkhataṃ sududdasaṃ <note>gambhīraṃ duddasaṃ padaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Saṃyojanaparikkhīṇo, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase <pb ed="V" n="2.0014" /> kappasate, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0389" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sovaṇṇakiṅkaṇiyo thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sovaṇṇakiṅkaṇiyattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Soṇṇakontarikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘Manobhāvaniyaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0042" /> buddhaṃ, attadantaṃ samāhitaṃ;
```

```
Iriyamānaṃ brahmapathe, cittavūpasame rataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘Nittiṇṇaoghaṃ sambuddhaṃ, jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ muniṃ;
```

```
Upatitthaṃ samāpannaṃ, indivaradalappabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘Alābunodakaṃ gayha, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upāgamiṃ;
```

```
Buddhassa pāde dhovitvā, alābukamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘Āṇāpesi <pb ed="M" n="2.0015" /> ca sambuddho, padumuttaranāmako;
```

```
‘Iminā dakamāhatvā, pādamūle ṭhapehi me’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Sādhūtihaṃ paṭissutvā, satthugāravatāya ca;
```

```
Dakaṃ alābunāhatvā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ upāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Anumodi mahāvīro, cittaṃ nibbāpayaṃ mama;
```

```
‘Iminālābudānena, saṅkappo te samijjhatu’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Pannarasesu kappesu, devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tiṃsatikkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Divā vā yadi vā rattiṃ, caṅkamantassa tiṭṭhato;
```

```
Sovaṇṇaṃ kontaraṃ gayha, tiṭṭhate purato mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa <pb ed="V" n="2.0015" /> datvānalābuṃ, labhāmi soṇṇakontaraṃ;
```

```
Appakampi kataṃ kāraṃ, vipulaṃ hoti tādisu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="T" n="2.0043" /> kappe, yaṃlābumadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, alābussa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā soṇṇakontariko thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Soṇṇakontarikattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Sakiṃsammajjakavaggo tecattālīsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sakiṃsammajjako <pb ed="P" n="2.0390" /> thero, ekadussī ekāsanī;
```

```
Kadambakoraṇḍakado, ghatassavanikopi ca.
```

```
Sucintiko kiṅkaṇiko, soṇṇakontarikopi ca;
```

```
Ekagāthāsatañcettha, ekasattatimeva ca.
```

### 44. Ekavihārivaggo

#### 1. Ekavihārikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi <pb ed="T" n="2.0044" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0016" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0016" /> bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Nippapañco nirālambo, ākāsasamamānaso;
```

```
Suññatābahulo tādī, animittarato vasī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṅgacitto nikleso <note>nillepo (syā. ka.)</note>, asaṃsaṭṭho kule gaṇe;
```

```
Mahākāruṇiko vīro, vinayopāyakovido.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Uyyutto parakiccesu, vinayanto sadevake;
```

```
Nibbānagamanaṃ maggaṃ, gatiṃ paṅkavisosanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Amataṃ paramassādaṃ, jarāmaccunivāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Mahāparisamajjhe so, nisinno lokatārako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Karavīkaruto <note>karavīkarudo (syā. pī. ka.)</note> nātho, brahmaghoso tathāgato;
```

```
Uddharanto mahāduggā, vippanaṭṭhe anāyake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Desento virajaṃ dhammaṃ, diṭṭho me lokanāyako;
```

```
Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvā tadāpāhaṃ, cintento jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ekakova vane ramme, vasiṃ saṃsaggapīḷito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Sakkāyavūpakāso <pb ed="T" n="2.0045" /> me, hetubhūto mamābhavī <note>mamāgamī (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Manaso vūpakāsassa, saṃsaggabhayadassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0391" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0017" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0017" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekavihāriko thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ekavihārikattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Ekasaṅkhiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassino bhagavato, mahābodhimaho ahu;
```

```
Mahājanā samāgamma, pūjenti bodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Na hi taṃ orakaṃ maññe, buddhaseṭṭho bhavissati;
```

```
Yassāyaṃ īdisā bodhi, pūjanīyā <note>īdiso bodhi, pūjanīyo (syā.)</note> ca satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Tato saṅkhaṃ gahetvāna, bodhirukkhamupaṭṭhahiṃ;
```

```
Dhamanto sabbadivasaṃ, avandiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Āsannake kataṃ kammaṃ, devalokaṃ apāpayī;
```

```
Kaḷevaraṃ me patitaṃ, devaloke ramāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni<pb ed="T" n="2.0046" />, tuṭṭhahaṭṭhā pamoditā;
```

```
Sadā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhanti, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Ekasattatime kappe, rājā āsiṃ sudassano;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambumaṇḍassa issaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Tato aṅgasatā turiyā <note>tūrā (sī. ka.)</note>, parivārenti maṃ sadā;
```

```
Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ, upaṭṭhānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Mātukucchigatassāpi, vajjare bheriyo sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhitvāna sambuddhaṃ, anubhutvāna sampadā;
```

```
Sivaṃ sukhemaṃ amataṃ, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0018" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0018" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekasaṅkhiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ekasaṅkhiyattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Pāṭihīrasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0047" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0392" /> nāma jino, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi, nagaraṃ pāvisī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Nagaraṃ pavisantassa, upasantassa tādino;
```

```
Ratanāni pajjotiṃsu <note>panādiṃsu (pī.)</note>, nigghoso āsi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa ānubhāvena, bherī vajjumaghaṭṭitā;
```

```
Sayaṃ vīṇā pavajjanti, buddhassa pavisato puraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ namassāmi <note>na passāmi (sī.)</note>, padumuttaramahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Pāṭihīrañca passitvā, tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Aho buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthusampadā;
```

```
Acetanāpi turiyā, sayameva pavajjare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0048" /> sudaṃ āyasmā pāṭihīrasaññako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Pāṭihīrasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Ñāṇatthavikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva <pb ed="M" n="2.0019" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0019" /> jalitaṃ, dīparukkhaṃva jotitaṃ;
```

```
Kañcanaṃva virocantaṃ, addasaṃ dvipaduttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Kamaṇḍaluṃ ṭhapetvāna, vākacīrañca kuṇḍikaṃ;
```

```
Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ thaviṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tamandhakāraṃ vidhamaṃ, mohajālasamākulaṃ;
```

```
Ñāṇālokaṃ dassetvāna, nittiṇṇosi mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘‘Samuddharasimaṃ lokaṃ, sabbāvantamanuttaraṃ;
```

```
Ñāṇe te upamā natthi, yāvatājagatogati <note>yāvatā ca gatogati (pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tena ñāṇena sabbaññū, iti buddho pavuccati;
```

```
Vandāmi taṃ mahāvīraṃ, sabbaññutamanāvaraṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="P" n="2.0393" /> kappe, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ thaviṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ñāṇatthavāyidaṃ phalaṃ;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0049" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ñāṇatthaviko thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ñāṇatthavikattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Ucchukhaṇḍikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare bandhumatiyā, dvārapālo ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Ucchukhaṇḍikamādāya, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, vipassissa mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="M" n="2.0020" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0020" /> kappe, yaṃ ucchumadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ucchukhaṇḍassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ucchukhaṇḍiko thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ucchukhaṇḍikattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Kaḷambadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Romaso <pb ed="T" n="2.0050" /> nāma sambuddho, vasate pabbatantare;
```

```
Kaḷambaṃ tassa pādāsiṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kaḷambassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kaḷambadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Kaḷambadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Ambāṭakadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Vipine <pb ed="P" n="2.0394" /> buddhaṃ disvāna, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ;
```

```
Ambāṭakaṃ gahetvāna, sayambhussa adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse <pb ed="V" n="2.0021" /> ito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0051" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0021" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambāṭakadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ambāṭakadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Harītakadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Harītakaṃ āmalakaṃ, ambajambuvibhītakaṃ;
```

```
Kolaṃ bhallātakaṃ billaṃ, sayameva harāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Disvāna pabbhāragataṃ, jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ muniṃ;
```

```
Ābādhena āpīḷentaṃ, adutīyaṃ mahāmuniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Harītakaṃ gahetvāna, sayambhussa adāsahaṃ;
```

```
Khādamattamhi bhesajje, byādhi passambhi <note>passaddhi (ka.)</note> tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Pahīnadaratho buddho, anumodamakāsi me;
```

```
‘Bhesajjadāneniminā, byādhivūpasamena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devabhūto manusso vā, jāto vā aññajātiyā;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhito hotu, mā ca te byādhimāgamā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0052" /> vatvāna sambuddho, sayambhū aparājito;
```

```
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī dhīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Yato harītakaṃ dinnaṃ, sayambhussa mahesino;
```

```
Imaṃ jātiṃ upādāya, byādhi me nupapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Tisso vijjā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, bhesajjamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bhesajjassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0022" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0022" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0395" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā harītakadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Harītakadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Ambapiṇḍiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthirājā tadā āsiṃ, īsādanto uruḷhavā;
```

```
Vicaranto brahāraññe, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Ambapiṇḍaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0053" /> gahetvāna, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ;
```

```
Paṭiggaṇhi mahāvīro, siddhattho lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Mama nijjhāyamānassa, paribhuñji tadā jino;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Tato ahaṃ cavitvāna, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Eteneva upāyena, anubhutvāna sampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Padhānapahitattohaṃ, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambapiṇḍiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ambapiṇḍiyattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Ambaphaliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa<pb ed="T" n="2.0054" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0023" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0023" />, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Piṇḍāya vicarantassa, dhārato uttamaṃ yasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Aggaphalaṃ gahetvāna, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Dakkhiṇeyyassa vīrassa, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena dvipadinda <note>dipadinda (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
```

```
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="P" n="2.0396" /> kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, aggadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

```
Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ambaphaliyo thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti;
```

Ambaphaliyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Ekavihārivaggo catucattālīsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Thero <pb ed="T" n="2.0055" /> ekavihārī ca, saṅkhiyo pāṭihīrako;
```

```
Thaviko ucchukhaṇḍī ca, kaḷambaambāṭakado.
```

```
Harītakambapiṇḍī ca, ambado dasamo yati;
```

```
Chaḷasīti ca gāthāyo, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
```

### 45. Vibhītakavaggo

#### 1. Vibhītakamiñjiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Kakusandho <pb ed="T" n="2.0056" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0024" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0024" /> mahāvīro, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Gaṇamhā vūpakaṭṭho so, agamāsi vanantaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Bījamiñjaṃ gahetvāna, latāya āvuṇiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Bhagavā tamhi samaye, jhāyate pabbatantare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Disvānahaṃ devadevaṃ, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Dakkhiṇeyyassa vīrassa, bījamiñjamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappamhi, yaṃ miñjamadadiṃ <note>phalamadadiṃ (sī. pī.), bījamadadiṃ (syā.)</note> tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bījamiñjassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vibhītakamiñjiyo <note>vibhedaka… (syā. ka.)</note> thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Vibhītakamiñjiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Koladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Ajinena <pb ed="T" n="2.0057" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0025" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0397" /> nivatthohaṃ, vākacīradharo tadā;
```

```
Khāriyā pūrayitvāna, kolaṃhāsiṃ mamassamaṃ <note>khāribhāraṃ haritvāna, kolamāharimassamaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Tamhi <pb ed="M" n="2.0025" /> kāle sikhī buddho, eko adutiyo ahu;
```

```
Mamassamaṃ upāgacchi, jānanto sabbakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, vanditvāna ca subbataṃ;
```

```
Ubho hatthehi paggayha, kolaṃ buddhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, koladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koladāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Koladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Billiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre<pb ed="T" n="2.0058" />, assamo sukato mama;
```

```
Billarukkhehi <note>beluvarukkhehi (syā.)</note> ākiṇṇo, nānādumanisevito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Sugandhaṃ beluvaṃ disvā, buddhaseṭṭhamanussariṃ;
```

```
Khāribhāraṃ pūrayitvā, tuṭṭho saṃviggamānaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Kakusandhaṃ upāgamma, billapakkamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Puññakkhettassa vīrassa, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappasmiṃ, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0026" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0026" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā billiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Billiyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Bhallātadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0059" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0398" /> sambuddhaṃ, dvattiṃsavaralakkhaṇaṃ;
```

```
Vipinaggena <note>pavanaggena (sī. syā. pī.)</note> gacchantaṃ, sālarājaṃva phullitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṇattharaṃ paññāpetvā, buddhaseṭṭhaṃ ayācahaṃ;
```

```
‘Anukampatu maṃ buddho, bhikkhaṃ icchāmi dātave’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako kāruṇiko, atthadassī mahāyaso;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, orūhi mama assame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Orohitvāna sambuddho, nisīdi paṇṇasanthare;
```

```
Bhallātakaṃ gahetvāna, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Mama nijjhāyamānassa, paribhuñji tadā jino;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, abhivandiṃ tadā jinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, yaṃ phalamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0060" /> sudaṃ āyasmā bhallātadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto <pb ed="T" n="2.0061" /> sumano, ambāṭakamapūjayiṃ;
```

```
Puññakkhettaṃ anuttaraṃ <note>mahāvīraṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

#### 7. Sīhāsanikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarassa <pb ed="M" n="2.0028" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0028" /> bhagavato, sabbabhūtahitesino;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, sīhāsanamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Devaloke manusse vā, yattha yattha vasāmahaṃ;
```

```
Labhāmi vipulaṃ byamhaṃ, sīhāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Soṇṇamayā rūpimayā, lohitaṅgamayā <note>lohitaṅkamayā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> bahū;
```

```
Maṇimayā ca pallaṅkā, nibbattanti mamaṃ sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Bodhiyā <pb ed="T" n="2.0062" /> āsanaṃ katvā, jalajuttamanāmino;
```

```
Ucce kule pajāyāmi, aho dhammasudhammatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, sīhāsanamakāsahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, sīhāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sīhāsaniko thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sīhāsanikattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Pādapīṭhiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho <pb ed="P" n="2.0400" /> nāma sambuddho, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
```

```
Tārayitvā bahū satte, nibbuto so mahāyaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhāsanassa sāmantā, sumedhassa mahesino;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, pādapīṭhamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Katvāna kusalaṃ kammaṃ, sukhapākaṃ sukhudrayaṃ;
```

```
Puññakammena saṃyutto, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha <pb ed="T" n="2.0063" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0029" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0029" /> me vasamānassa, puññakammasamaṅgino;
```

```
Padāni uddharantassa, soṇṇapīṭhā bhavanti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhā tesaṃ suladdhaṃ vo, ye labhanti upassutiṃ;
```

```
Nibbute kāraṃ katvāna, labhanti vipulaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Mayāpi sukataṃ kammaṃ, vāṇijjaṃ suppayojitaṃ;
```

```
Pādapīṭhaṃ karitvāna, soṇṇapīṭhaṃ labhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ disaṃ pakkamāmi, kenaci kiccayenahaṃ <note>paccayenahaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Soṇṇapīṭhe akkamāmi <note>soṇṇapīṭhena kamāmi (ka.)</note>, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pādapīṭhassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pādapīṭhiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Pādapīṭhiyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Vedikārakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarassa <pb ed="T" n="2.0064" /> bhagavato, bodhiyā pādaputtame;
```

```
Vedikaṃ sukataṃ katvā, sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Atoḷārāni <note>athoḷārāni (sī. pī.), aggoḷārāni (syā.)</note> bhaṇḍāni, katāni akatāni ca;
```

```
Antalikkhā pavassanti, vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Ubhato byūḷhasaṅgāme, pakkhandanto bhayānake;
```

```
Bhayabheravaṃ na passāmi, vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Mama <pb ed="M" n="2.0030" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0401" /> saṅkappamaññāya, byamhaṃ nibbattate subhaṃ;
```

```
Sayanāni mahagghāni, vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="V" n="2.0030" /> kappe, yaṃ vedikamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, vedikāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vedikārako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Vedikārakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Bodhigharadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhatthassa <pb ed="T" n="2.0065" /> bhagavato, dvipadindassa tādino;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, bodhigharamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Tusitaṃ upapannomhi, vasāmi ratane ghare;
```

```
Na me sītaṃ vā uṇhaṃ vā, vāto gatte na samphuse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcasaṭṭhimhito kappe, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Kāsikaṃ nāma nagaraṃ, vissakammena <note>visukammena (syā. ka.)</note> māpitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Dasayojanaāyāmaṃ, aṭṭhayojanavitthataṃ;
```

```
Na tamhi nagare atthi, kaṭṭhaṃ vallī ca mattikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Tiriyaṃ yojanaṃ āsi, addhayojanavitthataṃ;
```

```
Maṅgalo nāma pāsādo, vissakammena māpito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni, thambhā soṇṇamayā ahuṃ;
```

```
Maṇimayā ca niyyūhā, chadanaṃ rūpiyaṃ ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbasoṇṇamayaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0031" /> gharaṃ, vissakammena māpitaṃ;
```

```
Ajjhāvutthaṃ mayā etaṃ, gharadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Te sabbe anubhotvāna, devamānusake bhave;
```

```
Ajjhapattomhi nibbānaṃ, santipadamanuttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, bodhigharamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0066" /> nābhijānāmi, gharadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0031" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="P" n="2.0402" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhigharadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Bodhigharadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Vibhītakavaggo pañcacattālīsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Vibhītakī kolaphalī, billabhallātakappado;
```

```
Uttalambaṭakī ceva, āsanī pādapīṭhako.
```

```
Vediko bodhighariko, gāthāyo gaṇitāpi ca;
```

```
Ekūnāsītikā sabbā, asmiṃ vagge pakittitā.
```

### 46. Jagatidāyakavaggo

#### 1. Jagatidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammadassissa <pb ed="T" n="2.0067" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0032" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0032" /> munino, bodhiyā pādaputtame;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, jagatiṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Darito pabbatato vā, rukkhato patito ahaṃ;
```

```
Cuto patiṭṭhaṃ vindāmi, jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Na me corā vihesanti, nātimaññanti khattiyā <note>pasahanti, nātimaññati khattiyo (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbāmittetikkamāmi, jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha pūjito homi, jagatiyā idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, jagatiṃ kārayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, jagatidānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0068" /> sudaṃ āyasmā jagatidāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Jagatidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Morahatthiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Morahatthaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0033" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0403" /> gahetvāna, upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, morahatthamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Iminā <pb ed="M" n="2.0033" /> morahatthena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Nibbāyiṃsu tayo aggī, labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Aho buddho aho dhammo, aho no satthusampadā;
```

```
Datvānahaṃ morahatthaṃ, labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Tiyaggī <note>tidhaggī (syā. ka.), tivaggī (pī.)</note> nibbutā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, morahatthassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0069" /> sudaṃ āyasmā morahatthiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Morahatthiyattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Sīhāsanabījiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Tissassāhaṃ bhagavato, bodhirukkhamavandiyaṃ;
```

```
Paggayha bījaniṃ tattha, sīhāsanamabījahaṃ <note>mabījayiṃ (sī.), mavijjahaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, sīhāsanamabījahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bījanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0034" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sīhāsanabījiyo thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sīhāsanabījiyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 7. Ekachattiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Aṅgārajātā <pb ed="T" n="2.0072" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0405" /> pathavī, kukkuḷānugatā mahī;
```

```
Padumuttaro bhagavā, abbhokāsamhi caṅkami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Paṇḍaraṃ chattamādāya, addhānaṃ paṭipajjahaṃ;
```

```
Tattha disvāna sambuddhaṃ, vitti me upapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Marīciyotthaṭā <pb ed="V" n="2.0036" /> <note>maricimophunā (syā.), marīcivophuṭā (pī.)</note> bhūmi, aṅgārāva mahī ayaṃ;
```

```
Upahanti <note>upavāyanti (sī. pī.)</note> mahāvātā, sarīrassāsukhepanā <note>sarīrakāyukhepanā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Sītaṃ uṇhaṃ vihanantaṃ <note>vihanati (syā. ka.)</note>, vātātapanivāraṇaṃ;
```

```
Paṭiggaṇha imaṃ chattaṃ, phassayissāmi <note>passayissāmi (ka.)</note> nibbutiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako kāruṇiko, padumuttaro mahāyaso;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, paṭiggaṇhi tadā jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappāni devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Anubhomi sakaṃ kammaṃ, pubbe sukatamattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0036" /> me pacchimā jāti, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Ajjāpi setacchattaṃ me, sabbakālaṃ dharīyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ chattamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, chattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0073" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

#### 8. Jātipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Parinibbute bhagavati, padumuttare mahāyase;
```

```
Pupphavaṭaṃsake katvā <note>pupphacaṅkoṭake gahetvā (syā.)</note>, sarīramabhiropayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, nimmānaṃ agamāsahaṃ;
```

```
Devalokagato santo, puññakammaṃ sarāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Ambarā <pb ed="V" n="2.0037" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0406" /> pupphavasso me, sabbakālaṃ pavassati;
```

```
Saṃsarāmi manusse ce <note>ve (syā.)</note>, rājā homi mahāyaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Tahiṃ kusumavasso me, abhivassati sabbadā;
```

```
Tasseva <note>kāyesu (syā.), kāyeva (pī.)</note> pupphapūjāya, vāhasā sabbadassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Ajjāpi pupphavasso me, abhivassati sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="T" n="2.0074" /> kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>


Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Jagatī <pb ed="T" n="2.0076" /> morahatthī ca, āsanī ukkadhārako;
```

```
Akkami vanakoraṇḍi, chattado jātipūjako.
```

```
Paṭṭipupphī ca yo thero, dasamo gandhapūjako;
```

```
Sattasaṭṭhi ca gāthāyo, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
```

### 47. Sālakusumiyavaggo

#### 1. Sālakusumiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Parinibbute <pb ed="T" n="2.0077" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0039" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0039" /> bhagavati, jalajuttamanāmake;
```

```
Āropitamhi citake, sālapupphamapūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhiropayiṃ <note>pupphamabhipujayiṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, citapūjāyidaṃ <note>buddhapūjāyidaṃ (syā.)</note> phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sālakusumiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sālakusumiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 7. Labujaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>


<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Adhigañchiṃ tadā pītiṃ, vipulaṃ sukhamuttamaṃ;
```


<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Labujaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Pilakkhaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Vanantare <pb ed="V" n="2.0043" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0410" /> buddhaṃ disvā <note>vanante buddhaṃ disvāna (sī. pī.)</note>, atthadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, pilakkhassa <note>pilakkhussa (pī.)</note> phalaṃ adā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0083" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0043" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pilakkhaphaladāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pilakkhaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Sayaṃpaṭibhāniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Kakudhaṃ vilasantaṃva, devadevaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Tamandhakāraṃ nāsetvā, santāretvā bahuṃ janaṃ;
```

```
Ñāṇālokena jotantaṃ, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Vasīsatasahassehi, nīyantaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Uddharantaṃ bahū satte, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Āhanantaṃ <note>āhanitvā (syā. ka.)</note> dhammabheriṃ, maddantaṃ titthiye gaṇe;
```

```
Sīhanādaṃ vinadantaṃ, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā brahmalokato, āgantvāna sabrahmakā;
```

```
Pucchanti nipuṇe pañhe, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Yassañjaliṃ karitvāna, āyācanti sadevakā;
```

```
Tena puññaṃ anubhonti, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe <pb ed="V" n="2.0044" /> janā samāgantvā, sampavārenti cakkhumaṃ;
```

```
Na vikampati ajjhiṭṭho, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Nagaraṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0084" /> pavisato yassa, ravanti bheriyo bahū;
```

```
Vinadanti gajā mattā, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Vīthiyā <note>rathiyā (sī.)</note> gacchato yassa, sabbābhā jotate sadā;
```

```
Abbhunnatā samā honti, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Byāharantassa <pb ed="P" n="2.0411" /> buddhassa, cakkavāḷampi suyyati;
```

```
Sabbe satte viññāpeti, ko disvā na pasīdati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="M" n="2.0044" /> kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhikittayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sayaṃpaṭibhāniyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sayaṃpaṭibhāniyattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Nimittabyākaraṇiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā himavaṃ, mante vāce mahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Catupaññāsasahassāni, sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Adhitā <pb ed="T" n="2.0085" /> vedagū sabbe, chaḷaṅge pāramiṃ gatā;
```

```
Sakavijjāhupatthaddhā, himavante vasanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Cavitvā tusitā kāyā, devaputto mahāyaso;
```

```
Uppajji mātukucchismiṃ, sampajāno patissato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Sambuddhe upapajjante, dasasahassi kampatha;
```

```
Andhā cakkhuṃ alabhiṃsu, uppajjantamhi nāyake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbākāraṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0045" /> pakampittha, kevalā vasudhā ayaṃ;
```

```
Nigghosasaddaṃ sutvāna, ubbijjiṃsu <note>vimhayiṃsu (syā. ka.)</note> mahājanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe janā samāgamma, āgacchuṃ mama santikaṃ;
```

```
Vasudhāyaṃ pakampittha, kiṃ vipāko bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Avacāsiṃ <note>vidassāmi (syā.)</note> tadā tesaṃ, mā bhetha <note>mā roda (ka.), mābhāyittha (syā.)</note> natthi vo bhayaṃ;
```

```
Visaṭṭhā hotha sabbepi, uppādoyaṃ suvatthiko <note>sukhatthiko (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhahetūhi <pb ed="M" n="2.0045" /> samphussa <note>aṭṭhahetūhi samphassa (syā. pī.), atthahetu nisaṃsayaṃ (ka.)</note>, vasudhāyaṃ pakampati;
```

```
Tathā nimittā dissanti, obhāso vipulo mahā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṃsayaṃ buddhaseṭṭho, uppajjissati cakkhumā;
```

```
Saññāpetvāna janataṃ, pañcasīle kathesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvāna <pb ed="P" n="2.0412" /> pañca sīlāni, buddhuppādañca dullabhaṃ;
```

```
Ubbegajātā sumanā, tuṭṭhahaṭṭhā ahaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ nimittaṃ viyākariṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, byākaraṇassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0086" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nimittabyākaraṇiyo thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Nimittabyākaraṇiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Sālakusumiyavaggo sattacattālīsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sālakusumiyo thero, pūjā nibbāpakopi ca;
```

```
Setudo tālavaṇṭī ca, avaṭalabujappado.
```

```
Pilakkhapaṭibhānī ca, veyyākaraṇiyo dijo;
```

```
Dvesattati ca gāthāyo, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
```

### 48. Naḷamālivaggo

#### 1. Naḷamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0087" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0046" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0046" /> sambuddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
```

```
Vipinaggena gacchantaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Naḷamālaṃ gahetvāna, nikkhamanto ca tāvade;
```

```
Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, naḷamālamapūjayiṃ;
```

```
Dakkhiṇeyyaṃ mahāvīraṃ, sabbalokānukampakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ mālamabhiropayiṃ <note>pupphamabhiropayiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā naḷamāliyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Naḷamāliyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Maṇipūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0088" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0047" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0413" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, gacchate anilañjase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Avidūre himavantassa, mahājātassaro ahu;
```

```
Tattha me bhavanaṃ āsi, puññakammena saṃyutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavanā <pb ed="M" n="2.0047" /> abhinikkhamma, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Indīvaraṃva jalitaṃ, ādittaṃva hutāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Vicinaṃ naddasaṃ pupphaṃ, pūjayissanti nāyakaṃ;
```

```
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, avandiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Mama sīse maṇiṃ gayha, pūjayiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Imāya maṇipūjāya, vipāko hotu bhaddako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Antalikkhe ṭhito satthā, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘So te ijjhatu saṅkappo, labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ;
```

```
Imāya maṇipūjāya, anubhohi mahāyasaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna bhagavā, jalajuttamanāmako;
```

```
Agamāsi buddhaseṭṭho, yattha cittaṃ paṇīhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhikappāni devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Anekasatakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbakammaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0089" /> sarantassa, devabhūtassa me sato;
```

```
Maṇi nibbattate mayhaṃ, ālokakaraṇo mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Chaḷasītisahassāni, nāriyo me pariggahā;
```

```
Vicittavatthābharaṇā, āmukkamaṇikuṇḍalā <note>āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Aḷārapamhā hasulā, susaññā tanumajjhimā;
```

```
Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ, maṇipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Soṇṇamayā maṇimayā, lohitaṅgamayā tathā;
```

```
Bhaṇḍā me sukatā honti, yadicchasi <note>yadicchāya (sī. pī.)</note> piḷandhanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgārā <pb ed="V" n="2.0048" /> gahārammā, sayanañca mahārahaṃ;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, nibbattanti yadicchakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhā tesaṃ suladdhañca, ye labhanti upassutiṃ;
```

```
Puññakkhettaṃ manussānaṃ, osadhaṃ sabbapāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Mayhampi <pb ed="M" n="2.0048" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0414" /> sukataṃ kammaṃ, yohaṃ adakkhi nāyakaṃ;
```

```
Vinipātā pamuttomhi, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Divasañceva rattiñca <note>samantā sattaratanā (sī. pī. ka.)</note>, āloko hoti me sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Tāyeva maṇipūjāya, anubhotvāna sampadā;
```

```
Ñāṇāloko mayā diṭṭho, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ maṇiṃ abhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, maṇipūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0090" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā maṇipūjako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Maṇipūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Ukkāsatikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Kosiko nāma bhagavā, cittakūṭe vasī tadā;
```

```
Jhāyī jhānarato buddho, vivekābhirato muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā <note>ajjhogahetvā (sī. syā. pī.)</note> himavantaṃ, nārīgaṇapurakkhato;
```

```
Addasaṃ kosikaṃ buddhaṃ, puṇṇamāyeva candimaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Ukkāsate gahetvāna, parivāresahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Sattarattindivaṃ ṭhatvā <note>buddho (syā. ka.)</note>, aṭṭhamena agacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Vuṭṭhitaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0049" /> kosikaṃ buddhaṃ, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto vanditvā, ekaṃ bhikkhaṃ adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena dvipadinda, lokajeṭṭha narāsabha;
```

```
Uppajjiṃ tusite kāye, ekabhikkhāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Divasañceva <pb ed="T" n="2.0091" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0049" /> rattiñca, āloko hoti me sadā;
```

```
Samantā yojanasataṃ, obhāsena pharāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcapaññāsakappamhi, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Cāturanto vijitāvī, jambumaṇḍassa <note>jambusaṇḍassa (pī.)</note> issaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā me nagaraṃ āsi, iddhaṃ phītaṃ sunimmitaṃ;
```

```
Tiṃsayojanamāyāmaṃ, vitthārena ca vīsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Sobhaṇaṃ nāma nagaraṃ, vissakammena māpitaṃ;
```

```
Dasasaddāvivittaṃ taṃ, sammatāḷasamāhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="P" n="2.0415" /> tamhi nagare atthi, vallikaṭṭhañca mattikā;
```

```
Sabbasoṇṇamayaṃyeva, jotate niccakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Catupākāraparikkhittaṃ, tayo āsuṃ maṇimayā;
```

```
Vemajjhe tālapantī ca, vissakammena māpitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Dasasahassapokkharañño, padumuppalachāditā;
```

```
Puṇḍarīkehi <note>puṇḍarīkādi (syā.)</note> sañchannā, nānāgandhasamīritā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ ukkaṃ dhārayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ukkadhārassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0092" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ukkāsatiko thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ukkāsatikattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Sumanabījaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassino <pb ed="V" n="2.0050" /> bhagavato, bodhiyā pādaputtame;
```

```
Sumano bījaniṃ gayha, abījiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="M" n="2.0050" /> kappe, abījiṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bījanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sumanabījaniyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sumanabījaniyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Kummāsadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Esanāya <pb ed="T" n="2.0093" /> carantassa, vipassissa mahesino;
```

```
Rittakaṃ pattaṃ disvāna, kummāsaṃ pūrayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ bhikkhaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kummāsassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kummāsadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Kummāsadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Kusaṭṭhakadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Kassapassa <pb ed="V" n="2.0051" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0416" /> bhagavato, brāhmaṇassa vusīmato;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, kusaṭṭhakamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappasmiṃ, kusaṭṭhakamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kusaṭṭhakassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0094" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0051" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kusaṭṭhakadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Kusaṭṭhakadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Giripunnāgiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Sobhito nāma sambuddho, cittakūṭe vasī tadā;
```

```
Gahetvā giripunnāgaṃ, sayambhuṃ abhipūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0095" /> sudaṃ āyasmā giripunnāgiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Giripunnāgiyattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Vallikāraphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Sumano <pb ed="V" n="2.0052" /> nāma sambuddho, takkarāyaṃ vasī tadā;
```

```
Vallikāraphalaṃ gayha, sayambhussa adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0052" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vallikāraphaladāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Vallikāraphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Pānadhidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī <pb ed="P" n="2.0417" /> bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Divāvihārā nikkhamma, pathamāruhi <note>pītimāruyhi (syā.)</note> cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Pānadhiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0096" /> sukataṃ gayha, addhānaṃ paṭipajjahaṃ;
```

```
Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, pattikaṃ cārudassanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, nīharitvāna pānadhiṃ;
```

```
Pādamūle ṭhapetvāna, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘‘Abhirūha mahāvīra, sugatinda vināyaka;
```

```
Ito phalaṃ labhissāmi, so me attho samijjhatu’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Anomadassī bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Pānadhiṃ abhirūhitvā, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo pānadhiṃ me adāsi, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa <pb ed="V" n="2.0053" /> giramaññāya, sabbe devā samāgatā;
```

```
Udaggacittā sumanā, vedajātā katañjalī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Pānadhīnaṃ padānena, sukhitoyaṃ bhavissati;
```

```
Pañcapaññāsakkhattuñca, devarajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassakkhattuṃ rājā ca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena <note>nāmena (sabbattha)</note>, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="M" n="2.0053" /> dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Devaloke <pb ed="T" n="2.0097" /> manusse vā, nibbattissati puññavā;
```

```
Devayānapaṭibhāgaṃ, yānaṃ paṭilabhissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Pāsādā sivikā vayhaṃ, hatthino samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Rathā vājaññasaṃyuttā, sadā pātubhavanti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Agārā nikkhamantopi, rathena nikkhamiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Kesesu chijjamānesu, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhā mayhaṃ suladdhaṃ me, vāṇijjaṃ suppayojitaṃ;
```

```
Datvāna pānadhiṃ ekaṃ, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, yaṃ pānadhimadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pānadhissa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0418" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pānadhidāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Pānadhidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Pulinacaṅkamiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo <pb ed="T" n="2.0098" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0054" /> pure āsiṃ, araññe kānane ahaṃ;
```

```
Vātamigaṃ gavesanto, caṅkamaṃ addasaṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Ucchaṅgena pulinaṃ <note>puḷinaṃ (sī. syā. pī. ka.)</note> gayha, caṅkame okiriṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, sugatassa sirīmato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, pulinaṃ okiriṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pulinassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0054" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pulinacaṅkamiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Pulinacaṅkamiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Naḷamālivaggo aṭṭhacattālīsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Naḷamālī maṇidado, ukkāsatikabījanī;
```

```
Kummāso ca kusaṭṭho ca, giripunnāgiyopi ca.
```

```
Vallikāro <pb ed="T" n="2.0099" /> pānadhido, atho pulinacaṅkamo;
```

```
Gāthāyo pañcanavuti, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi.
```

### 49. Paṃsukūlavaggo

#### 1. Paṃsukūlasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

