‘‘Tisso <pb ed="M" n="2.0055" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0055" /> nāmāsi bhagavā, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
```

```
Paṃsukūlaṃ ṭhapetvāna, vihāraṃ pāvisī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Vinataṃ <note>sajjitaṃ (syā.), tiyantaṃ (pī.)</note> dhanumādāya, bhakkhatthāya cariṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Maṇḍalaggaṃ gahetvāna, kānanaṃ pāvisiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthaddasaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0419" /> paṃsukūlaṃ, dumagge laggitaṃ tadā;
```

```
Cāpaṃ tattheva nikkhippa, sire katvāna añjaliṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, vipulāya ca pītiyā;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna, paṃsukūlaṃ avandahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, paṃsukūlamavandahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, vandanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0100" /> vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paṃsukūlasaññako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Paṃsukūlasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Buddhasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhāyako <pb ed="V" n="2.0056" /> mantadharo, tiṇṇaṃ vedāna pāragū;
```

```
Lakkhaṇe itihāse ca, sanighaṇḍusakeṭubhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Nadīsotapaṭibhāgā<pb ed="M" n="2.0056" />, sissā āyanti me tadā;
```

```
Tesāhaṃ mante <note>mantaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> vācemi, rattindivamatandito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Siddhattho nāma sambuddho, loke uppajji tāvade;
```

```
Tamandhakāraṃ nāsetvā, ñāṇālokaṃ pavattayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Mama aññataro sisso, sissānaṃ so kathesi me;
```

```
Sutvāna te etamatthaṃ, ārocesuṃ mamaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho loke samuppanno, sabbaññū lokanāyako;
```

```
Tassānuvattati jano, lābho amhaṃ na vijjati <note>na hessati (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Adhiccuppattikā buddhā, cakkhumanto mahāyasā;
```

```
Yaṃnūnāhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhaṃ, passeyyaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Ajinaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0101" /> me gahetvāna, vākacīraṃ kamaṇḍaluṃ;
```

```
Assamā abhinikkhamma, sisse āmantayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Odumbarikapupphaṃva, candamhi sasakaṃ yathā;
```

```
Vāyasānaṃ yathā khīraṃ, dullabho lokanāyako <note>dullabhā lokanāyakā (sī.), dullabhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ (syā. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho lokamhi uppanno, manussattampi dullabhaṃ;
```

```
Ubhosu vijjamānesu, savanañca sudullabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho loke samuppanno, cakkhuṃ lacchāma no bhavaṃ;
```

```
Etha sabbe gamissāma, sammāsambuddhasantikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Kamaṇḍaludharā <pb ed="P" n="2.0420" /> sabbe, kharājinanivāsino;
```

```
Te jaṭā bhārabharitā, nikkhamuṃ vipinā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Yugamattaṃ pekkhamānā, uttamatthaṃ gavesino;
```

```
Āsattidosarahitā, asambhītāva kesarī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Appakiccā aloluppā, nipakā santavuttino;
```

```
Uñchāya caramānā te, buddhaseṭṭhamupāgamuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Diyaḍḍhayojane <pb ed="V" n="2.0057" /> sese, byādhi me upapajjatha;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <pb ed="M" n="2.0057" /> kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0102" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā buddhasaññako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Buddhasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Bhisadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Ogayha yaṃ <note>ogayhāhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> pokkharaṇiṃ, nānākuñjarasevitaṃ;
```

```
Uddharāmi bhisaṃ tattha, ghāsahetu <note>asanahetu (syā.)</note> ahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, padumuttarasavhayo;
```

```
Rattambaradharo <note>rattakambaladharo (syā.)</note> buddho, gacchati anilañjase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Dhunanto paṃsukūlāni, saddamassosahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Uddhaṃ nijjhāyamānohaṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Tattheva ṭhitako santo, āyāciṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Madhuṃ bhisehi savati, khīraṃ sappiṃ muḷālibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggaṇhātu me buddho, anukampāya cakkhumā;
```

```
Tato kāruṇiko satthā, oruhitvā mahāyaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggaṇhi mamaṃ bhikkhaṃ, anukampāya cakkhumā;
```

```
Paṭiggahetvā sambuddho, akā me anumodanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sukhī <pb ed="T" n="2.0103" /> hotu <note>hohi (sī. syā. pī. ka.)</note> mahāpuñña, gati tuyhaṃ samijjhatu;
```

```
Iminā bhisadānena, labhassu vipulaṃ sukhaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0058" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0421" /> vatvāna sambuddho, jalajuttamanāmako;
```

```
Bhikkhamādāya sambuddho, ambarenāgamā jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="M" n="2.0058" /> bhisaṃ gahetvāna, āgacchiṃ mama assamaṃ;
```

```
Bhisaṃ rukkhe lagetvāna <note>laggitvāna (syā. ka.)</note>, mama dānamanussariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāvāto vuṭṭhahitvā, sañcālesi vanaṃ tadā;
```

```
Ākāso abhinādittha, asaniyā phalantiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me asanipāto, matthake nipatī tadā;
```

```
Sohaṃ nisinnako santo, tattha kālaṅkato ahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Puññakammena saṃyutto, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ;
```

```
Kaḷevaraṃ me patitaṃ, devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Chaḷasītisahassāni, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Sāyapātaṃ <note>sāyaṃ pātaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> upaṭṭhanti, bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Manussayonimāgantvā, sukhito homahaṃ sadā;
```

```
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampitako tena, devadevena tādinā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ bhisaṃ <note>bhikkhaṃ (sabbattha)</note> adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bhisadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0104" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bhisadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Bhisadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Ñāṇathavikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Dakkhiṇe <pb ed="V" n="2.0059" /> himavantassa, sukato assamo mama;
```

```
Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto, vasāmi vipine tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhālābhena <pb ed="M" n="2.0059" /> santuṭṭho, mūlena ca phalena ca;
```

```
Anvesanto ācariyaṃ, vasāmi ekako ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho nāma sambuddho, loke uppajji tāvade;
```

```
Catusaccaṃ pakāseti, uddharanto mahājanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Nāhaṃ suṇomi sambuddhaṃ, napi me koci saṃsati <note>bhāsati (sī.), sāsati (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Aṭṭhavasse atikkante, assosiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Aggidāruṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0422" /> nīharitvā, sammajjitvāna assamaṃ;
```

```
Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna, nikkhamiṃ vipinā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Ekarattiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0105" /> vasantohaṃ, gāmesu nigamesu ca;
```

```
Anupubbena candavatiṃ, tadāhaṃ upasaṅkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā tamhi samaye, sumedho lokanāyako;
```

```
Uddharanto bahū satte, deseti amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Janakāyamatikkamma, vanditvā jinasāgaraṃ;
```

```
Ekaṃsaṃ ajinaṃ katvā, santhaviṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tuvaṃ satthā ca ketu ca, dhajo yūpo ca pāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Parāyano <note>parāyaṇo (sī. pī.)</note> patiṭṭhā ca, dīpo ca dvipaduttamo.
```

Ekavīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nepuñño dassane vīro, tāresi janataṃ tuvaṃ;
```

```
Natthañño tārako loke, tavuttaritaro mune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sakkā theve <note>have (sī. pī.) bhave (syā. ka.)</note> kusaggena, pametuṃ sāgaruttame <note>sāgaruttamo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Natveva tava sabbaññu, ñāṇaṃ sakkā pametave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tuladaṇḍe <pb ed="V" n="2.0060" /> <note>tulamaṇḍale (sī. pī.)</note> ṭhapetvāna, mahiṃ <note>mahī (syā. pī.)</note> sakkā dharetave;
```

```
Natveva tava paññāya, pamāṇamatthi cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ākāso minituṃ sakkā, rajjuyā aṅgulena vā;
```

```
Natveva tava sabbaññu, sīlaṃ sakkā pametave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahāsamudde <pb ed="M" n="2.0060" /> udakaṃ, ākāso ca vasundharā;
```

```
Parimeyyāni etāni, appameyyosi cakkhuma’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Chahi <pb ed="T" n="2.0106" /> gāthāhi sabbaññuṃ, kittayitvā mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, tuṇhī aṭṭhāsahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ vadanti sumedhoti, bhūripaññaṃ sumedhasaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo me ñāṇaṃ pakittesi, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattasattati kappāni, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Sahassakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjaṃ karissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anekasatakkhattuñca, cakkavattī bhavissati;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devabhūto <pb ed="P" n="2.0423" /> manusso vā, puññakammasamāhito;
```

```
Anūnamanasaṅkappo, tikkhapañño bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Agārā abhinikkhamma, pabbajissati kiñcano;
```

```
Jātiyā sattavassena, arahattaṃ phusissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Etthantare na jānāmi, cetanaṃ amanoramaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃsaritvā bhave sabbe, sampattānubhaviṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Bhoge <pb ed="T" n="2.0107" /> me ūnatā natthi, phalaṃ ñāṇassa thomane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Tiyaggī nibbutā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā parikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi<pb ed="V" n="2.0061" />, yaṃ ñāṇamathaviṃ ahaṃ <note>mabhithomayiṃ (sī. pī.), mabhithomahaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phalaṃ ñāṇassa thomane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0061" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ñāṇathaviko thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ñāṇathavikattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Candanamāliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā, piyarūpe manorame;
```

```
Asītikoṭiyo hitvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvāna kāyena, pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ;
```

```
Vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā, nadīkūle vasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Ekakaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0108" /> maṃ viharantaṃ, buddhaseṭṭho upāgami;
```

```
Nāhaṃ jānāmi buddhoti, akāsiṃ paṭisantharaṃ <note>paṭisandhāraṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Karitvā paṭisanthāraṃ, nāmagottamapucchahaṃ;
```

```
‘Devatānusi gandhabbo, adu sakko purindado.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, mahābrahmā idhāgato;
```

```
Virocesi disā sabbā, udayaṃ sūriyo yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sahassārāni <pb ed="P" n="2.0424" /> cakkāni, pāde dissanti mārisa;
```

```
Ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto, kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ;
```

```
Nāmagottaṃ pavedehi, saṃsayaṃ apanehi me’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘‘Namhi devo na gandhabbo, namhi <note>nāpi (sī.)</note> sakko purindado;
```

```
Brahmabhāvo ca me natthi, etesaṃ uttamo ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atīto visayaṃ tesaṃ, dālayiṃ kāmabandhanaṃ;
```

```
Sabbe kilese jhāpetvā, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="M" n="2.0062" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0062" /> vācaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ;
```

```
‘Yadi buddhoti sabbaññū, nisīda tvaṃ mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘Tamahaṃ pūjayissāmi, dukkhassantakaro tuvaṃ’;
```

```
‘‘Pattharitvā jinacammaṃ, adāsi satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Nisīdi tattha bhagavā, sīhova girigabbhare;
```

```
Khippaṃ pabbatamāruyha, ambassa phalamaggahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Sālakalyāṇikaṃ pupphaṃ, candanañca mahārahaṃ;
```

```
Khippaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0109" /> paggayha taṃ sabbaṃ, upetvā lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Phalaṃ buddhassa datvāna, sālapupphamapūjayiṃ;
```

```
Candanaṃ anulimpitvā, avandiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, vipulāya ca pītiyā;
```

```
Ajinamhi nisīditvā, sumedho lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Mama kammaṃ pakittesi, hāsayanto mamaṃ tadā;
```

```
‘Iminā phaladānena, gandhamālehi cūbhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcavīse kappasate, devaloke ramissati;
```

```
Anūnamanasaṅkappo, vasavattī bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘‘Chabbīsatikappasate, manussattaṃ gamissati;
```

```
Bhavissati cakkavattī, cāturanto mahiddhiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vebhāraṃ nāma nagaraṃ, vissakammena māpitaṃ;
```

```
Hessati sabbasovaṇṇaṃ, nānāratanabhūsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘‘Eteneva upāyena, saṃsarissati so bhave <note>yoniso (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sabbattha pūjito hutvā, devatte atha mānuse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, brahmabandhu bhavissati;
```

```
Agārā abhinikkhamma, anagārī bhavissati;
```

```
Abhiññāpāragū hutvā, nibbāyissatināsavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0425" /> vatvāna sambuddho, sumedho lokanāyako;
```

```
Mama nijjhāyamānassa, pakkāmi anilañjase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0110" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0063" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Tusitato <pb ed="V" n="2.0063" /> cavitvāna, nibbattiṃ mātukucchiyaṃ;
```

```
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, yamhi gabbhe vasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Mātukucchigate mayi, annapānañca bhojanaṃ;
```

```
Mātuyā mama chandena, nibbattati yadicchakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā pañcavassena, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Oropitamhi kesamhi, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbakammaṃ gavesanto, orena nāddasaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, mama kammamanussariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Namo te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
```

```
Tava sāsanamāgamma, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0111" /> sudaṃ āyasmā candanamāliyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Candanamāliyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Dhātupūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbute lokanāthamhi, siddhatthe lokanāyake;
```

```
Mama ñātī samānetvā, dhātupūjaṃ akāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ dhātumabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, dhātupūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0064" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhātupūjako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Dhātupūjakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Pulinuppādakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbate <pb ed="V" n="2.0064" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0426" /> himavantamhi, devalo nāma tāpaso;
```

```
Tattha me caṅkamo āsi, amanussehi māpito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Jaṭābhārena <pb ed="T" n="2.0112" /> <note>jaṭābhārassa (syā. ka.)</note> bharito, kamaṇḍaludharo sadā;
```

```
Uttamatthaṃ gavesanto, vipinā nikkhamiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni, sissā mayhaṃ upaṭṭhahuṃ;
```

```
Sakakammābhipasutā, vasanti vipine tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Assamā abhinikkhamma, akaṃ pulinacetiyaṃ;
```

```
Nānāpupphaṃ samānetvā, taṃ cetiyamapūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, assamaṃ pavisāmahaṃ;
```

```
Sabbe sissā samāgantvā, etamatthaṃ pucchiṃsu maṃ <note>etamatthamapucchu maṃ (sī.), etamattaṃ apucchiṃsu (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pulinena kato thūpo <note>kato thūpe (sī.)</note>, yaṃ tvaṃ deva <note>devaṃ (sī. pī.)</note> massati;
```

```
Mayampi ñātumicchāma, puṭṭho ācikkha no tuvaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘‘Niddiṭṭhā nu <note>niddiṭṭhā no (sī. pī.), diṭṭhāno vo (syā.)</note> mantapade, cakkhumanto mahāyasā;
```

```
Te kho ahaṃ namassāmi, buddhaseṭṭhe mahāyase’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kīdisā te mahāvīrā, sabbaññū lokanāyakā;
```

```
Kathaṃvaṇṇā kathaṃsīlā, kīdisā te mahāyasā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bāttiṃsalakkhaṇā <pb ed="M" n="2.0065" /> buddhā, cattālīsadijāpi ca;
```

```
Nettā gopakhumā tesaṃ, jiñjukā phalasannibhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘‘Gacchamānā ca te buddhā, yugamattañca pekkhare;
```

```
Na tesaṃ jāṇu nadati, sandhisaddo na suyyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘‘Gacchamānā ca sugatā, uddharantāva gacchare;
```

```
Paṭhamaṃ dakkhiṇaṃ pādaṃ, buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘‘Asambhītā <pb ed="T" n="2.0113" /> ca te buddhā, migarājāva kesarī;
```

```
Nevukkaṃsenti attānaṃ, no ca vambhenti pāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mānāvamānato muttā, samā sabbesu pāṇisu;
```

```
Anattukkaṃsakā buddhā, buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘‘Uppajjantā <pb ed="V" n="2.0065" /> ca sambuddhā, ālokaṃ dassayanti te;
```

```
Chappakāraṃ pakampenti, kevalaṃ vasudhaṃ imaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘‘Passanti <pb ed="P" n="2.0427" /> nirayañcete, nibbāti nirayo tadā;
```

```
Pavassati mahāmegho, buddhānaṃ esa dhammatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘‘Īdisā te mahānāgā, atulā ca <note>te (syā. ka.)</note> mahāyasā;
```

```
Vaṇṇato anatikkantā, appameyyā tathāgatā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anumodiṃsu me vākyaṃ, sabbe sissā sagāravā;
```

```
Tathā ca paṭipajjiṃsu, yathāsatti yathābalaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭipūjenti pulinaṃ, sakakammābhilāsino;
```

```
Saddahantā mama vākyaṃ, buddhasakkatamānasā <note>buddhattagatamānasā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā cavitvā tusitā, devaputto mahāyaso;
```

```
Uppajji mātukucchimhi, dasasahassi kampatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Assamassāvidūramhi, caṅkamamhi ṭhito ahaṃ;
```

```
Sabbe sissā samāgantvā, āgacchuṃ mama santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Usabhova mahī nadati, migarājāva kūjati;
```

```
Susumārova <note>suṃsumārova (sī. syā. pī.)</note> saḷati, kiṃ vipāko bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0114" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0066" /> pakittemi sambuddhaṃ, sikatāthūpasantike;
```

```
So dāni bhagavā satthā, mātukucchimupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘Tesaṃ dhammakathaṃ vatvā, kittayitvā mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Uyyojetvā sake sisse, pallaṅkamābhujiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘Balañca vata me khīṇaṃ, byādhinā <note>byādhito (sī. syā. pī. ka.)</note> paramena taṃ;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna, tattha kālaṅkato <note>kālakato (sī. pī.)</note> ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbe sissā samāgantvā, akaṃsu citakaṃ tadā;
```

```
Kaḷevarañca me gayha, citakaṃ abhiropayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘Citakaṃ parivāretvā, sīse katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Sokasallaparetā te, vikkandiṃsu samāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘Tesaṃ lālappamānānaṃ, agamaṃ citakaṃ tadā;
```

```
‘Ahaṃ ācariyo tumhaṃ, mā socittha sumedhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sadatthe <pb ed="V" n="2.0066" /> vāyameyyātha, rattindivamatanditā;
```

```
Mā vo pamattā ahuttha <note>ahuvattha (sī.)</note>, khaṇo vo paṭipādito’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Sake sissenusāsitvā, devalokaṃ punāgamiṃ;
```

```
Aṭṭhārasa ca kappāni, devaloke ramāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Satānaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0428" /> pañcakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Anekasatakkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Avasesesu kappesu, vokiṇṇo <note>vokiṇṇaṃ (sī. syā. ka.)</note> saṃsariṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, uppādassa idaṃ phalaṃ <note>pulinapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Yathā <pb ed="T" n="2.0115" /> komudike māse, bahū pupphanti pādapā;
```

```
Tathevāhampi samaye, pupphitomhi mahesinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Vīriyaṃ me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhikittayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, kittanāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0067" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pulinuppādako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Pulinuppādakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Taraṇiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadassī tu bhagavā, sayambhū lokanāyako;
```

```
Vinatā nadiyā tīraṃ <note>tīre (syā. pī. ka.)</note>, upāgacchi tathāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘Udakā abhinikkhamma, kacchapo vārigocaro;
```

```
Buddhaṃ tāretukāmohaṃ, upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘‘Abhirūhatu <pb ed="T" n="2.0116" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0067" /> maṃ buddho, atthadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Ahaṃ taṃ tārayissāmi, dukkhassantakaro tuvaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, atthadassī mahāyaso;
```

```
Abhirūhitvā me piṭṭhiṃ, aṭṭhāsi lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘Yato sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi viññutaṃ;
```

```
Sukhaṃ me tādisaṃ natthi, phuṭṭhe pādatale yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘Uttaritvāna sambuddho, atthadassī mahāyaso;
```

```
Nadītīramhi ṭhatvāna, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yāvatā <pb ed="P" n="2.0429" /> vattate cittaṃ, gaṅgāsotaṃ tarāmahaṃ;
```

```
Ayañca kacchapo rājā, tāresi mama paññavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā buddhataraṇena, mettacittavatāya ca;
```

```
Aṭṭhārase kappasate, devaloke ramissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devalokā idhāgantvā, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Ekāsane nisīditvā, kaṅkhāsotaṃ tarissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yathāpi <pb ed="M" n="2.0068" /> bhaddake khette, bījaṃ appampi ropitaṃ;
```

```
Sammādhāre pavacchante, phalaṃ toseti kassakaṃ <note>kassake (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tathevidaṃ buddhakhettaṃ, sammāsambuddhadesitaṃ;
```

```
Sammādhāre pavacchante, phalaṃ maṃ tosayissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘Padhānapahitattomhi, upasanto nirūpadhi;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase <pb ed="T" n="2.0117" /> kappasate, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, taraṇāya idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā taraṇiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Taraṇiyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Dhammaruciyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="V" n="2.0068" /> dīpaṅkaro buddho, sumedhaṃ byākarī jino;
```

```
‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, ayaṃ buddho bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘‘Imassa janikā mātā, māyā nāma bhavissati;
```

```
Pitā suddhodano nāma, ayaṃ hessati gotamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘‘Padhānaṃ padahitvāna, katvā dukkarakārikaṃ;
```

```
Assatthamūle sambuddho, bujjhissati mahāyaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘‘Upatisso kolito ca, aggā hessanti sāvakā;
```

```
Ānando nāma nāmena <note>ānando nāmupaṭṭhāko (syā.)</note>, upaṭṭhissatimaṃ jinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘‘Khemā <pb ed="T" n="2.0118" /> uppalavaṇṇā ca, aggā hessanti sāvikā;
```

```
Citto āḷavako ceva, aggā hessantupāsakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘‘Khujjuttarā <pb ed="M" n="2.0069" /> nandamātā, aggā hessantupāsikā;
```

```
Bodhi imassa vīrassa, assatthoti pavuccati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0430" /> sutvāna vacanaṃ, asamassa mahesino;
```

```
Āmoditā naramarū, namassanti katañjalī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ māṇavo āsiṃ, megho nāma susikkhito;
```

```
Sutvā byākaraṇaṃ seṭṭhaṃ, sumedhassa mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃvisaṭṭho bhavitvāna, sumedhe karuṇāsaye <note>karuṇālaye (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Pabbajantañca taṃ vīraṃ, sahāva anupabbajiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃvuto pātimokkhasmiṃ, indriyesu ca pañcasu;
```

```
Suddhājīvo sato vīro, jinasāsanakārako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ viharamānohaṃ, pāpamittena kenaci;
```

```
Niyojito anācāre, sumaggā paridhaṃsito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Vitakkavasiko hutvā, sāsanato apakkamiṃ;
```

```
Pacchā tena kumittena, payutto mātughātanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘Akariṃ ānantariyaṃ <note>akariṃ nantariyañca (syā. ka.)</note>, ghātayiṃ duṭṭhamānaso;
```

```
Tato cuto mahāvīciṃ, upapanno sudāruṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘Vinipātagato <pb ed="V" n="2.0069" /> santo, saṃsariṃ dukkhito ciraṃ;
```

```
Na puno addasaṃ vīraṃ, sumedhaṃ narapuṅgavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘Asmiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0119" /> kappe samuddamhi, maccho āsiṃ timiṅgalo;
```

```
Disvāhaṃ sāgare nāvaṃ, gocaratthamupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā maṃ vāṇijā bhītā, buddhaseṭṭhamanussaruṃ;
```

```
Gotamoti mahāghosaṃ, sutvā tehi udīritaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbasaññaṃ saritvāna, tato kālaṅkato ahaṃ;
```

```
Sāvatthiyaṃ kule iddhe, jāto brāhmaṇajātiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Āsiṃ dhammaruci nāma, sabbapāpajigucchako;
```

```
Disvāhaṃ lokapajjotaṃ, jātiyā sattavassiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Mahājetavanaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0070" /> gantvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Upemi buddhaṃ tikkhattuṃ, rattiyā divasassa ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā disvā muni āha, ciraṃ dhammarucīti maṃ;
```

```
Tatohaṃ avacaṃ buddhaṃ, pubbakammapabhāvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Suciraṃ satapuññalakkhaṇaṃ, patipubbena visuddhapaccayaṃ;
```

```
Ahamajjasupekkhanaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0431" /> vata, tava passāmi nirupamaṃ viggahaṃ <note>nirūpamaggahaṃ (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Suciraṃ vihatattamo mayā, sucirakkhena nadī visositā;
```

```
Suciraṃ amalaṃ visodhitaṃ, nayanaṃ ñāṇamayaṃ mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Cirakālasamaṅgito <pb ed="T" n="2.0120" /> <note>cirakālaṃ samāgato (pī.)</note> tayā, avinaṭṭho punarantaraṃ ciraṃ;
```

```
Punarajjasamāgato tayā, na hi nassanti katāni gotama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dhammaruciyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Dhammaruciyattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Sālamaṇḍapiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhogāhetvā <pb ed="V" n="2.0070" /> sālavanaṃ, sukato assamo mama;
```

```
Sālapupphehi sañchanno, vasāmi vipine tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
‘‘Piyadassī ca bhagavā, sayambhū aggapuggalo;
```

```
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, sālavanamupāgami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘Assamā abhinikkhamma, pavanaṃ agamāsahaṃ;
```

```
Mūlaphalaṃ gavesanto, āhiṇḍāmi vane tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘Tatthaddasāsiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0121" /> sambuddhaṃ, piyadassiṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Sunisinnaṃ samāpannaṃ, virocantaṃ mahāvane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Catudaṇḍe <pb ed="M" n="2.0071" /> ṭhapetvāna, buddhassa uparī ahaṃ;
```

```
Maṇḍapaṃ sukataṃ katvā, sālapupphehi chādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
‘‘Sattāhaṃ dhārayitvāna, maṇḍapaṃ sālachāditaṃ;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, buddhaseṭṭhamavandahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
‘‘Bhagavā <pb ed="P" n="2.0432" /> tamhi samaye, vuṭṭhahitvā samādhito;
```

```
Yugamattaṃ pekkhamāno, nisīdi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvako varuṇo nāma, piyadassissa satthuno;
```

```
Vasīsatasahassehi, upagacchi vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
‘‘Piyadassī ca bhagavā, lokajeṭṭho narāsabho;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghe nisīditvā, sitaṃ pātukarī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘Anuruddho upaṭṭhāko, piyadassissa satthuno;
```

```
Ekaṃsaṃ cīvaraṃ katvā, apucchittha mahāmuniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ko nu kho bhagavā hetu, sitakammassa satthuno;
```

```
Kāraṇe vijjamānamhi, satthā pātukare sitaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattāhaṃ sālacchadanaṃ <note>pupphachadanaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, yo me dhāresi māṇavo;
```

```
Tassa kammaṃ saritvāna, sitaṃ pātukariṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anokāsaṃ na passāmi, yattha <note>yaṃ taṃ (syā. pī. ka.)</note> puññaṃ vipaccati;
```

```
Devaloke <pb ed="T" n="2.0122" /> manusse vā, okāsova na sammati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devaloke <pb ed="V" n="2.0071" /> vasantassa, puññakammasamaṅgino;
```

```
Yāvatā parisā tassa, sālacchannā bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tattha dibbehi naccehi, gītehi vāditehi ca;
```

```
Ramissati sadā santo, puññakammasamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yāvatā parisā tassa, gandhagandhī bhavissati;
```

```
Sālassa pupphavasso ca, pavassissati tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tato cutoyaṃ manujo, mānusaṃ āgamissati;
```

```
Idhāpi sālacchadanaṃ, sabbakālaṃ dharissati <note>dhariyati (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘‘Idha <pb ed="M" n="2.0072" /> naccañca gītañca, sammatāḷasamāhitaṃ;
```

```
Parivāressanti maṃ niccaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘‘Uggacchante ca sūriye, sālavassaṃ pavassati;
```

```
Puññakammena saṃyuttaṃ, vassate sabbakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārase kappasate, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissatināsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhammaṃ abhisamentassa, sālacchannaṃ bhavissati;
```

```
Citake jhāyamānassa, chadanaṃ tattha hessati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘Vipākaṃ kittayitvāna, piyadassī mahāmuni;
```

```
Parisāya dhammaṃ desesi, tappento dhammavuṭṭhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappāni <pb ed="T" n="2.0123" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0433" /> devesu, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Saṭṭhi ca sattakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘Devalokā idhāgantvā, labhāmi vipulaṃ sukhaṃ;
```

```
Idhāpi sālacchadanaṃ, maṇḍapassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Idhāpi sālacchadanaṃ, hessati sabbakālikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāmuniṃ tosayitvā, gotamaṃ sakyapuṅgavaṃ;
```

```
Pattomhi acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, hitvā jayaparājayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārase <pb ed="V" n="2.0072" /> kappasate, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0073" /> sudaṃ āyasmā sālamaṇḍapiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sālamaṇḍapiyattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Paṃsukūlavaggo ekūnapaññāsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Paṃsukūlaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0124" /> buddhasaññī, bhisado ñāṇakittako;
```

```
Candanī dhātupūjī ca, pulinuppādakopi ca.
```

```
Taraṇo dhammaruciko, sālamaṇḍapiyo tathā;
```

```
Satāni dve honti gāthā, ūnavīsatimeva ca.
```

### 50. Kiṅkaṇipupphavaggo

#### 1. Tikiṅkaṇipupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva <pb ed="T" n="2.0125" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0074" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0073" /> jotantaṃ, nisinnaṃ pabbatantare;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Tīṇi kiṅkaṇipupphāni, paggayha abhiropayiṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhamabhipūjetvā, gacchāmi dakkhiṇāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0434" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tikiṅkaṇipupphiyo thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Tikiṅkaṇipupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Paṃsukūlapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="T" n="2.0126" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0074" />, udaṅgaṇo nāma pabbato;
```

```
Tatthaddasaṃ paṃsukūlaṃ, dumaggamhi vilambitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Tīṇi kiṅkaṇipupphāni, ocinitvānahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, paṃsukūlamapūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="M" n="2.0075" /> kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pūjitvā arahaddhajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā paṃsukūlapūjako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Paṃsukūlapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Koraṇḍapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Vanakammiko <pb ed="T" n="2.0127" /> pure āsiṃ, pitumātumatenahaṃ <note>pitupetāmahenahaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Pasumārena jīvāmi, kusalaṃ me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Mama āsayasāmantā, tisso lokagganāyako;
```

```
Padāni tīṇi dassesi, anukampāya cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Akkante ca pade disvā, tissanāmassa satthuno;
```

```
Haṭṭho haṭṭhena cittena, pade cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Koraṇḍaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā, pādapaṃ dharaṇīruhaṃ;
```

```
Sakosakaṃ gahetvāna, padaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ <note>padaseṭṭhe apūjayiṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="2.0075" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0435" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Koraṇḍakachavi homi, suppabhāso <note>sapabhāso (sī. syā. pī. ka.)</note> bhavāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, padapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0076" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0128" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā koraṇḍapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Koraṇḍapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Kiṃsukapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃsukaṃ pupphitaṃ disvā, paggahetvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Buddhaseṭṭhaṃ saritvāna, ākāse abhipūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kiṃsukapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Kiṃsukapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Upaḍḍhadussadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabhagavato<pb ed="T" n="2.0129" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0076" />, sujāto nāma sāvako;
```

```
Paṃsukūlaṃ gavesanto, saṅkāre carate <note>caratī (sī. ka.)</note> tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, paresaṃ bhatako ahaṃ;
```

```
Upaḍḍhadussaṃ datvāna, sirasā abhivādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="2.0077" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Tettiṃsakkhattuṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0436" /> devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Sattasattatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Upaḍḍhadussadānena, modāmi akutobhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Icchamāno cahaṃ ajja, sakānanaṃ sapabbataṃ;
```

```
Khomadussehi chādeyyaṃ, aḍḍhadussassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, aḍḍhadussassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0130" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā upaḍḍhadussadāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Upaḍḍhadussadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Ghatamaṇḍadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Sucintitaṃ bhagavantaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Upaviṭṭhaṃ mahāraññaṃ, vātābādhena pīḷitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā <pb ed="V" n="2.0077" /> cittaṃ pasādetvā, ghatamaṇḍamupānayiṃ;
```

```
Katattā ācitattā <note>upacitattā (syā. ka.)</note> ca, gaṅgā bhāgīrathī ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāsamuddā cattāro, ghataṃ sampajjare mama;
```

```
Ayañca pathavī ghorā, appamāṇā asaṅkhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Mama saṅkappamaññāya, bhavate madhusakkarā <note>madhusakkharā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Cātuddīpā ime rukkhā, pādapā dharaṇīruhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Mama <pb ed="M" n="2.0078" /> saṅkappamaññāya, kapparukkhā bhavanti te;
```

```
Paññāsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Ekapaññāsakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <note>chanavute ito (sī.)</note> kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ghatamaṇḍassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0131" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ghatamaṇḍadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ghatamaṇḍadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Udakadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa<pb ed="P" n="2.0437" />, bhikkhusaṅghe anuttare;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, pānīghaṭamapūrayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbatagge dumagge vā, ākāse vātha bhūmiyaṃ;
```

```
Yadā pānīyamicchāmi, khippaṃ nibbattate mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, dakadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0078" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0132" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā udakadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Udakadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Pulinathūpiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="M" n="2.0079" />, yamako nāma pabbato;
```

```
Assamo sukato mayhaṃ, paṇṇasālā sumāpitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Nārado nāma nāmena, jaṭilo uggatāpano;
```

```
Catuddasasahassāni, sissā paricaranti maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisallīnako santo, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
```

```
‘Sabbo jano maṃ pūjeti, nāhaṃ pūjemi kiñcanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na me ovādako atthi, vattā koci na vijjati;
```

```
Anācariyupajjhāyo, vane vāsaṃ upemahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘‘Upāsamāno yamahaṃ, garucittaṃ upaṭṭhahe;
```

```
So me ācariyo natthi, vanavāso niratthako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āyāgaṃ me gavesissaṃ, garuṃ bhāvaniyaṃ tathā;
```

```
Sāvassayo vasissāmi, na koci garahissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Uttānakūlā nadikā, supatitthā manoramā;
```

```
Saṃsuddhapulinākiṇṇā, avidūre mamassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Nadiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0133" /> amarikaṃ nāma, upagantvānahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Saṃvaḍḍhayitvā pulinaṃ, akaṃ pulinacetiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Ye <pb ed="P" n="2.0438" /> te ahesuṃ sambuddhā, bhavantakaraṇā munī;
```

```
Tesaṃ etādiso thūpo, taṃ nimittaṃ karomahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Karitvā <pb ed="V" n="2.0079" /> pulinaṃ <note>puḷine (sī. syā. pī.)</note> thūpaṃ, sovaṇṇaṃ māpayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Soṇṇakiṅkaṇipupphāni, sahasse tīṇi pūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Sāyapātaṃ namassāmi, vedajāto katañjalī;
```

```
Sammukhā viya sambuddhaṃ, vandiṃ pulinacetiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā kilesā jāyanti, vitakkā gehanissitā;
```

```
Sarāmi sukataṃ thūpaṃ, paccavekkhāmi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Upanissāya viharaṃ, satthavāhaṃ vināyakaṃ;
```

```
Kilese saṃvaseyyāsi, na yuttaṃ tava mārisa.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Saha <pb ed="M" n="2.0080" /> āvajjite thūpe, gāravaṃ hoti me tadā;
```

```
Kuvitakke vinodesiṃ, nāgo tuttaṭṭito yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ viharamānaṃ maṃ, maccurājābhimaddatha;
```

```
Tattha kālaṅkato santo, brahmalokamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatāyuṃ vasitvāna, tidive <note>tidase (sī. pī.)</note> upapajjahaṃ;
```

```
Asītikkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Soṇṇakiṅkaṇipupphānaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0134" /> <note>tesaṃ kiṅkaṇipupphānaṃ (sī.)</note>, vipākaṃ anubhomahaṃ;
```

```
Dhātīsatasahassāni, parivārenti maṃ <note>me (ka.)</note> bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Thūpassa pariciṇṇattā, rajojallaṃ na limpati;
```

```
Gatte sedā na muccanti, suppabhāso bhavāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Aho me sukato thūpo, sudiṭṭhāmarikā nadī;
```

```
Thūpaṃ katvāna pulinaṃ, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Kusalaṃ kattukāmena, jantunā sāragāhinā;
```

```
Natthi khettaṃ akhettaṃ vā, paṭipattīva sādhakā <note>sārikā (pī.), sārakā (syā.), sāratā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi balavā poso, aṇṇavaṃ taritussahe;
```

```
Parittaṃ kaṭṭhamādāya, pakkhandeyya mahāsaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Imāhaṃ kaṭṭhaṃ nissāya, tarissāmi mahodadhiṃ;
```

```
Ussāhena vīriyena, tareyya udadhiṃ naro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva <pb ed="V" n="2.0080" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0439" /> me kataṃ kammaṃ, parittaṃ thokakañca yaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ kammaṃ upanissāya, saṃsāraṃ samatikkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto, mahāsāle suaḍḍhake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhā mātā pitā mayhaṃ, buddhassa saraṇaṃ gatā;
```

```
Ubho diṭṭhapadā ete, anuvattanti sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Bodhipapaṭikaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0081" /> gayha, soṇṇathūpamakārayuṃ;
```

```
Sāyapātaṃ <note>sāyaṃ pātaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> namassanti, sakyaputtassa sammukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Uposathamhi <pb ed="T" n="2.0135" /> divase, soṇṇathūpaṃ vinīharuṃ;
```

```
Buddhassa vaṇṇaṃ kittentā, tiyāmaṃ vītināmayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Saha disvānahaṃ <note>pasādetvānahaṃ (ka.)</note> thūpaṃ, sariṃ pulinacetiyaṃ;
```

```
Ekāsane nisīditvā, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

Dvāvīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Gavesamāno taṃ vīraṃ, dhammasenāpatiddasaṃ;
```

```
Agārā nikkhamitvāna, pabbajiṃ tassa santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ;
```

```
Upasampādayī buddho, guṇamaññāya cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Dārakeneva santena, kiriyaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ mayā;
```

```
Kataṃ me karaṇīyajja, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbaverabhayātīto, sabbasaṅgātigo <note>sabbasaṅkātito (ka.)</note> isi;
```

```
Sāvako te mahāvīra, soṇṇathūpassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0136" /> sudaṃ āyasmā pulinathūpiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Pulinathūpiyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Naḷakuṭidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="V" n="2.0081" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0440" />, hārito nāma pabbato;
```

```
Sayambhū nārado nāma, rukkhamūle vasī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Naḷāgāraṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0082" /> karitvāna, tiṇena chādayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Caṅkamaṃ sodhayitvāna, sayambhussa adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, naḷakuṭikanimmitaṃ;
```

```
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Catuddasesu kappesu, devaloke ramiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Ekasattatikkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Catutiṃsatikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammapāsādamāruyha, sabbākāravarūpamaṃ;
```

```
Yadicchakāhaṃ vihare, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, naḷakuṭiyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0137" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā naḷakuṭidāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Naḷakuṭidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Piyālaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo <pb ed="V" n="2.0082" /> pure āsiṃ, vipine vicaraṃ tadā;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Piyālaphalamādāya, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Puññakkhettassa vīrassa, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse <pb ed="M" n="2.0083" /> ito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0441" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0138" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā piyālaphaladāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Piyālaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

Kiṅkaṇipupphavaggo paññāsamo.

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kiṅkaṇī paṃsukūlañca, koraṇḍamatha kiṃsukaṃ;
```

```
Upaḍḍhadussī ghatado, udakaṃ thūpakārako.
```

```
Naḷakārī ca navamo, piyālaphaladāyako;
```

```
Satamekañca gāthānaṃ, navakañca taduttari.
```

Atha vagguddānaṃ –

```
Metteyyavaggo bhaddāli, sakiṃsammajjakopi ca;
```

```
Ekavihārī vibhītakī, jagatī sālapupphiyo.
```

```
Naḷāgāraṃ paṃsukūlaṃ, kiṅkaṇipupphiyo tathā;
```

```
Asīti dve ca gāthāyo, catuddasasatāni ca.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Metteyyavaggadasakaṃ.</trailer>

Pañcamasatakaṃ samattaṃ.

### 51. Kaṇikāravaggo

#### 1. Tikaṇikārapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Sumedho <pb ed="T" n="2.0139" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0084" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0083" /> nāma sambuddho, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
```

```
Vivekakāmo sambuddho, himavantamupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjhogayha himavantaṃ, aggo kāruṇiko muni;
```

```
Pallaṅkamābhujitvāna, nisīdi purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Vijjādharo tadā āsiṃ, antalikkhacaro ahaṃ;
```

```
Tisūlaṃ sukataṃ gayha, gacchāmi ambare tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbatagge yathā aggi, puṇṇamāyeva candimā;
```

```
Vane obhāsate buddho, sālarājāva phullito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Vanaggā <pb ed="P" n="2.0442" /> nikkhamitvāna, buddharaṃsībhidhāvare;
```

```
Naḷaggivaṇṇasaṅkāsā, disvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Vicinaṃ addasaṃ pupphaṃ, kaṇikāraṃ devagandhikaṃ;
```

```
Tīṇi pupphāni ādāya, buddhaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa ānubhāvena, tīṇi pupphāni me tadā;
```

```
Uddhaṃvaṇṭā adhopattā, chāyaṃ kubbanti satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha <pb ed="T" n="2.0140" /> me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, kaṇikārīti ñāyati;
```

```
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassakaṇḍaṃ satabheṇḍu <note>satageṇḍu (syā.)</note>, dhajāluharitāmayaṃ;
```

```
Satasahassaniyyūhā, byamhe pātubhaviṃsu me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Soṇṇamayā maṇimayā, lohitaṅgamayāpi ca;
```

```
Phalikāpi ca pallaṅkā, yenicchakā yadicchakā <note>yenicchayā yadicchakaṃ (syā.), yadicchakāyadicchakā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Mahārahañca <pb ed="M" n="2.0085" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0084" /> sayanaṃ, tūlikāvikatīyutaṃ;
```

```
Uddhalomikaekantaṃ, bimbohanasamāyutaṃ <note>bibbohanasamāyutaṃ… (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavanā nikkhamitvāna, caranto devacārikaṃ;
```

```
Yadā icchāmi gamanaṃ, devasaṅghapurakkhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Pupphassa heṭṭhā tiṭṭhāmi, uparicchadanaṃ mama;
```

```
Samantā yojanasataṃ, kaṇikārehi chāditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Saṭṭhituriyasahassāni, sāyapātamupaṭṭhahuṃ;
```

```
Parivārenti maṃ niccaṃ, rattindivamatanditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha naccehi gītehi, tāḷehi vāditehi ca;
```

```
Ramāmi khiḍḍāratiyā, modāmi kāmakāmihaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha bhutvā pivitvā ca, modāmi tidase tadā;
```

```
Nārīgaṇehi sahito, modāmi byamhamuttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Padesarajjaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0141" /> vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavābhave saṃsaranto, mahābhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ;
```

```
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Duve <pb ed="P" n="2.0443" /> bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Duve kule pajāyāmi, khattiye cāpi brāhmaṇe;
```

```
Nīce kule na jāyāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, sivikaṃ sandamānikaṃ;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Dāsīgaṇaṃ dāsagaṇaṃ, nāriyo samalaṅkatā;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Koseyyakambaliyāni, khomakappāsikāni ca;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Navavatthaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0086" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0085" /> navaphalaṃ, navaggarasabhojanaṃ;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Imaṃ khāda imaṃ bhuñja, imamhi sayane saya;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbattha pūjito homi, yaso abbhuggato mama;
```

```
Mahāpakkho sadā homi, abhejjapariso sadā;
```

```
Ñātīnaṃ uttamo homi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Sītaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0142" /> uṇhaṃ na jānāmi, pariḷāho na vijjati;
```

```
Atho cetasikaṃ dukkhaṃ, hadaye me na vijjati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇo hutvāna, saṃsarāmi bhavābhave;
```

```
Vevaṇṇiyaṃ na jānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto, mahāsāle suaḍḍhake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca kāmaguṇe hitvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Upasampādayī buddho, guṇamaññāya cakkhumā;
```

```
Taruṇo pūjanīyohaṃ, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbacakkhu visuddhaṃ me, samādhikusalo ahaṃ;
```

```
Abhiññāpāramippatto, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā anuppatto, iddhipādesu kovido;
```

```
Dhammesu pāramippatto, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsakappasahassamhi<pb ed="P" n="2.0444" />, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0143" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0087" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0086" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tikaṇikārapupphiyo thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Tikaṇikārapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Ekapattadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare haṃsavatiyā, kumbhakāro ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Sukataṃ mattikāpattaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Pattaṃ datvā bhagavato, ujubhūtassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Bhave nibbattamānohaṃ, soṇṇathāle labhāmahaṃ;
```

```
Rūpimaye ca sovaṇṇe, taṭṭike ca maṇīmaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Pātiyo paribhuñjāmi, puññakammassidaṃ phalaṃ;
```

```
Yasānañca dhanānañca <note>yasasāva janānañca (syā.)</note>, aggabhūto <note>pattabhūto (sī. pī.)</note> ca homahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāpi bhaddake khette, bījaṃ appampi ropitaṃ;
```

```
Sammādhāraṃ pavacchante, phalaṃ toseti kassakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Tathevidaṃ pattadānaṃ, buddhakhettamhi ropitaṃ;
```

```
Pītidhāre pavassante, phalaṃ maṃ tosayissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā khettā vijjanti, saṅghāpi ca gaṇāpi ca;
```

```
Buddhakhettasamo natthi, sukhado sabbapāṇinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Namo <pb ed="T" n="2.0144" /> te purisājañña, namo te purisuttama;
```

```
Ekapattaṃ daditvāna, pattomhi acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ pattamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pattadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0087" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0088" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ekapattadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ekapattadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Kāsumāraphaliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva <pb ed="P" n="2.0445" /> jotantaṃ, nisinnaṃ pabbatantare;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, lokajeṭṭhaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Kāsumārikamādāya, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0145" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kāsumāraphaliyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Kāsumāraphaliyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Avaṭaphaliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassaraṃsī bhagavā, sayambhū aparājito;
```

```
Vivekā uṭṭhahitvāna, gocarāyābhinikkhami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Phalahattho <pb ed="V" n="2.0088" /> ahaṃ disvā, upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, avaṭaṃ adadiṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <pb ed="M" n="2.0089" /> kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0146" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā avaṭaphaliyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Avaṭaphaliyattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Pādaphaliyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ sambuddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
```

```
Rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ, pādaphalaṃ <note>vāraphalaṃ (sī.), cāraphalaṃ (syā.), pāraphalaṃ (pī.)</note> adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0446" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā pādaphaliyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Pādaphaliyattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Mātuluṅgaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṇikāraṃva <pb ed="T" n="2.0147" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0089" /> jalitaṃ, puṇṇamāyeva candimaṃ;
```

```
Jalantaṃ dīparukkhaṃva, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Mātuluṅgaphalaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0090" /> gayha, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ;
```

```
Dakkhiṇeyyassa vīrassa <note>dhīrassa (sī.)</note>, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mātuluṅgaphaladāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Mātuluṅgaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Ajeliphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Ajjuno <note>ajino (syā.)</note> nāma sambuddho, himavante vasī tadā;
```

```
Caraṇena ca sampanno, samādhikusalo muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Kumbhamattaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0148" /> gahetvāna, ajeliṃ <note>añjaliṃ (syā.), ajelaṃ (pī.)</note> jīvajīvakaṃ;
```

```
Chattapaṇṇaṃ gahetvāna, adāsiṃ satthuno ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ajeliphaladāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ajeliphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Amodaphaliyattheraapadānaṃ

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0091" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0090" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0447" /> sambuddhaṃ, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggahaṃ;
```

```
Rathiyaṃ paṭipajjantaṃ, amodamadadiṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā amodaphaliyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Amodaphaliyattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Tālaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Sataraṃsī nāma bhagavā, sayambhū aparājito;
```

```
Vivekā vuṭṭhahitvāna, gocarāyābhinikkhami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Phalahattho ahaṃ disvā, upagacchiṃ narāsabhaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, tālaphalaṃ adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0150" /> sudaṃ āyasmā tālaphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Tālaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Nāḷikeraphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="M" n="2.0092" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0091" /> bandhumatiyā, ārāmiko ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, gacchantaṃ anilañjase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Nāḷikeraphalaṃ gayha, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Ākāse ṭhitako santo, paṭiggaṇhi mahāyaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Vittisañjanano <pb ed="P" n="2.0448" /> mayhaṃ, diṭṭhadhammasukhāvaho;
```

```
Phalaṃ buddhassa datvāna, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Adhigacchiṃ tadā pītiṃ, vipulañca sukhuttamaṃ;
```

```
Uppajjateva ratanaṃ, nibbattassa tahiṃ tahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbacakkhu visuddhaṃ me, samādhikusalo ahaṃ;
```

```
Abhiññāpāramippatto, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… <pb ed="T" n="2.0151" /> kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā nāḷikeraphaladāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Nāḷikeraphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Kaṇikāravaggo ekapaññāsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kaṇikārekapattā ca, kāsumārī tathāvaṭā;
```

```
Pādañca mātuluṅgañca, ajelīmodameva ca.
```

```
Tālaṃ tathā nāḷikeraṃ, gāthāyo gaṇitā viha;
```

```
Ekaṃ gāthāsataṃ hoti, ūnādhikavivajjitaṃ.
```

### 52. Phaladāyakavaggo

#### 1. Kurañciyaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo <pb ed="T" n="2.0152" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0093" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0092" /> pure āsiṃ, vipine vicaraṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Kurañciyaphalaṃ gayha, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Puññakkhettassa tādino, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0449" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kurañciyaphaladāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kurañciyaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

```

‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre<pb ed="T" n="2.0156" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0095" />, ahosiṃ kinnaro tadā;

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, vedajāto katañjalī;
```

```

```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="2.0096" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā kinnaraṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Chattiṃsakkhattuṃ devindo, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Dasakkhattuṃ cakkavattī, mahārajjamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Sukhette vappitaṃ bījaṃ, sayambhumhi aho mama <note>ahosi me (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Kusalaṃ vijjate mayhaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Pūjāraho ahaṃ ajja, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

#### 7. Kuṭajapupphiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre, vasalo <note>cāvalo (sī. pī.), accayo (syā.)</note> nāma pabbato;
```

```
Buddho sudassano nāma, vasate pabbatantare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Pupphaṃ hemavantaṃ gayha, vehāsaṃ agamāsahaṃ;
```

```
Tatthaddasāsiṃ sambuddhaṃ, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Pupphaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0096" /> kuṭajamādāya, sire katvāna añjaliṃ <note>katvānahaṃ tadā (syā. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Buddhassa abhiropesiṃ, sayambhussa mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0097" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kuṭajapupphiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Kuṭajapupphiyattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Ghosasaññakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo <pb ed="T" n="2.0158" /> pure āsiṃ, araññe vipine ahaṃ;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, devasaṅghapurakkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Catusaccaṃ pakāsentaṃ, desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Assosiṃ madhuraṃ dhammaṃ, sikhino lokabandhuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Ghose cittaṃ pasādesiṃ, asamappaṭipuggale;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, uttariṃ <note>atariṃ (sī. pī.)</note> duttaraṃ bhavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ saññamalabhiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ghosasaññāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā ghosasaññako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ghosasaññakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Sabbaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Varuṇo <pb ed="T" n="2.0159" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0097" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0452" /> nāma nāmena, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
```

```
Chaḍḍetvā dasaputtāni, vanamajjhogahiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Assamaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0098" /> sukataṃ katvā, suvibhattaṃ manoramaṃ;
```

```
Paṇṇasālaṃ karitvāna, vasāmi vipine ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro lokavidū, āhutīnaṃ paṭiggaho;
```

```
Mamuddharitukāmo so, āgacchi mama assamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā vanasaṇḍamhi, obhāso vipulo ahu;
```

```
Buddhassa ānubhāvena, pajjalī vipinaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Disvāna taṃ pāṭihīraṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Pattapuṭaṃ gahetvāna, phalena pūjayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Upagantvāna sambuddhaṃ, sahakhārimadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Anukampāya me buddho, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna, pacchato ehi me tuvaṃ;
```

```
Paribhutte ca saṅghamhi, puññaṃ tava bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Puṭakantaṃ gahetvāna, bhikkhusaṅghassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, tusitaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha dibbehi naccehi, gītehi vāditehi ca;
```

```
Puññakammena saṃyuttaṃ, anubhomi sadā sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0160" /> yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā caturo dīpā, sasamuddā sapabbatā;
```

```
Phalaṃ buddhassa datvāna, issaraṃ kārayāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā me pakkhigaṇā, ākāse uppatanti ce;
```

```
Tepi maṃ vasamanventi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā vanasaṇḍamhi, yakkhā bhūtā ca rakkhasā;
```

```
Kumbhaṇḍā garuḷā cāpi, pāricariyaṃ upenti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Kumbhā <pb ed="V" n="2.0098" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0453" /> soṇā madhukārā, ḍaṃsā ca makasā ubho;
```

```
Tepi maṃ vasamanventi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Supaṇṇā <pb ed="M" n="2.0099" /> nāma sakuṇā, pakkhijātā mahabbalā;
```

```
Tepi maṃ saraṇaṃ yanti, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Yepi dīghāyukā nāgā, iddhimanto mahāyasā;
```

```
Tepi maṃ vasamanventi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhā byagghā ca dīpī ca, acchakokataracchakā;
```

```
Tepi maṃ vasamanventi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Osadhītiṇavāsī ca, ye ca ākāsavāsino;
```

```
Sabbe maṃ saraṇaṃ yanti, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Sududdasaṃ sunipuṇaṃ, gambhīraṃ suppakāsitaṃ;
```

```
Phassayitvā <note>phusayitvā (ka.)</note> viharāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Vimokkhe <pb ed="T" n="2.0161" /> aṭṭha phusitvā, viharāmi anāsavo;
```

```
Ātāpī nipako cāhaṃ, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Ye phalaṭṭhā buddhaputtā, khīṇadosā mahāyasā;
```

```
Ahamaññataro tesaṃ, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Abhiññāpāramiṃ gantvā, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Tevijjā iddhipattā ca, buddhaputtā mahāyasā;
```

```
Dibbasotasamāpannā, tesaṃ aññataro ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, phaladānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sabbaphaladāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sabbaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Padumadhārikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="T" n="2.0162" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0100" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0099" />, romaso nāma pabbato;
```

```
Buddhopi sambhavo nāma, abbhokāse vasī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavanā nikkhamitvāna, padumaṃ dhārayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Ekāhaṃ dhārayitvāna, bhavanaṃ punarāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse <pb ed="P" n="2.0454" /> ito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā padumadhāriko thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Padumadhārikattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Phaladāyakavaggo dvepaññāsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kurañciyaṃ kapitthañca, kosambamatha ketakaṃ;
```

```
Nāgapupphajjunañceva, kuṭajī ghosasaññako.
```

```
Thero <pb ed="T" n="2.0163" /> ca sabbaphalado, tathā padumadhāriko;
```

```
Asīti cettha gāthāyo, tisso gāthā taduttari.
```

### 53. Tiṇadāyakavaggo

#### 1. Tiṇamuṭṭhidāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Himavantassāvidūre<pb ed="M" n="2.0101" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0100" />, lambako nāma pabbato;
```

```
Tattheva tisso <note>tatthopatisso (sī. pī. ka.)</note> sambuddho, abbhokāsamhi caṅkami.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo pure āsiṃ, araññe kānane ahaṃ;
```

```
Disvāna taṃ devadevaṃ, tiṇamuṭṭhimadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Nisīdanatthaṃ buddhassa, datvā cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, pakkāmiṃ <note>pakkamiṃ (ka.)</note> uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Aciraṃ gatamattassa <note>gatamattaṃ maṃ (sī. syā.)</note>, migarājā apothayi <note>aheṭhayi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sīhena pothito <note>pātito (sī. pī.), ghāṭito (syā.)</note> santo, tattha kālaṅkato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Āsanne me kataṃ kammaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhe anāsave;
```

```
Sumutto saravegova, devalokamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Yūpo tattha subho āsi, puññakammābhinimmito;
```

```
Sahassakaṇḍo satabheṇḍu, dhajālu haritāmayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Pabhā <pb ed="T" n="2.0164" /> niddhāvate tassa, sataraṃsīva uggato;
```

```
Ākiṇṇo devakaññāhi, āmodiṃ kāmakāmihaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Devalokā <pb ed="P" n="2.0455" /> cavitvāna, sukkamūlena codito;
```

```
Āgantvāna manussattaṃ, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, nisīdanamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, tiṇamuṭṭhe idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0102" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0101" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā tiṇamuṭṭhidāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Tiṇamuṭṭhidāyakattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Mañcadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassino bhagavato, lokajeṭṭhassa tādino;
```

```
Ekamañcaṃ <note>ekaṃ veccaṃ (syā.), ekapacchaṃ (pī.)</note> mayā dinnaṃ, pasannena sapāṇinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, dibbayānaṃ samajjhagaṃ;
```

```
Tena mañcakadānena, pattomhi āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="T" n="2.0165" /> kappe, yaṃ mañcamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, mañcadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mañcadāyako <note>veccakadāyako (syā.), saddasaññikavaggepi idaṃ§apadānaṃ dissati</note> thero imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Mañcadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Saraṇagamaniyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Āruhimha tadā nāvaṃ, bhikkhu cājīviko cahaṃ;
```

```
Nāvāya bhijjamānāya, bhikkhu me saraṇaṃ adā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse <pb ed="M" n="2.0103" /> ito kappe, yaṃ so me saraṇaṃ adā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, saraṇagamane phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0102" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0166" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā saraṇagamaniyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Saraṇagamaniyattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Abbhañjanadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
