‘‘Nagare <pb ed="P" n="2.0456" /> bandhumatiyā, rājuyyāne vasāmahaṃ;
```

```
Cammavāsī tadā āsiṃ, kamaṇḍaludharo ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Addasaṃ vimalaṃ buddhaṃ, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ;
```

```
Padhānaṃ pahitattaṃ taṃ, jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ vasiṃ <note>isiṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbakāmasamiddhiñca, oghatiṇṇamanāsavaṃ;
```

```
Disvā pasanno sumano, abbhañjanamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, abbhañjanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0167" /> sudaṃ āyasmā abbhañjanadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Abbhañjanadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Supaṭadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Divāvihārā <pb ed="M" n="2.0104" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0103" /> nikkhanto, vipassī lokanāyako;
```

```
Lahuṃ supaṭakaṃ <note>supaṭikaṃ (syā.), pūpapavaṃ (pī.)</note> datvā, kappaṃ saggamhi modahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, supaṭakamadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, supaṭassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā supaṭadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Supaṭadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Daṇḍadāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Kānanaṃ vanamogayha, veḷuṃ chetvānahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Ālambaṇaṃ karitvāna, saṅghassa adadiṃ bahuṃ <note>ahaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0168" /> cittappasādena, subbate abhivādiya;
```

```
Ālambadaṇḍaṃ datvāna, pakkāmiṃ uttarāmukho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito <pb ed="P" n="2.0457" /> kappe, yaṃ daṇḍamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, daṇḍadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0104" /> sudaṃ āyasmā daṇḍadāyako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Daṇḍadāyakattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

Tevīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

#### 7. Girinelapūjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Migaluddo <pb ed="M" n="2.0105" /> pure āsiṃ, vipine vicaraṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, sabbadhammāna pāraguṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Tasmiṃ mahākāruṇike, sabbasattahite rate;
```

```
Pasannacitto sumano, nelapupphamapūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse <pb ed="T" n="2.0169" /> ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā girinelapūjako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Girinelapūjakattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Bodhisammajjakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ pure bodhipattaṃ, ujjhitaṃ cetiyaṅgaṇe;
```

```
Taṃ gahetvāna chaḍḍesiṃ, alabhiṃ vīsatīguṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa kammassa tejena, saṃsaranto bhavābhave;
```

```
Duve bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte cāpi mānuse.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, āgantvā mānusaṃ bhavaṃ;
```

```
Duve kule pajāyāmi, khattiye cāpi brāhmaṇe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Aṅgapaccaṅgasampanno, ārohapariṇāhavā;
```

```
Abhirūpo suci homi, sampuṇṇaṅgo anūnako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Devaloke <pb ed="T" n="2.0170" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0105" /> manusse vā, jāto vā yattha katthaci;
```

```
Bhave suvaṇṇavaṇṇo ca, uttattakanakūpamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Mudukā <pb ed="M" n="2.0106" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0458" /> maddavā sniddhā <note>mudu maddavā siniddhā (syā.)</note>, sukhumā sukumārikā;
```

```
Chavi me sabbadā hoti, bodhipatte suchaḍḍite <note>suchaḍḍine (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Yato kutoci gatīsu, sarīre samudāgate;
```

```
Na limpati rajojallaṃ, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Uṇhe vātātape tassa, aggitāpena vā pana;
```

```
Gatte sedā na muccanti, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Kuṭṭhaṃ gaṇḍo kilāso ca, tilakā piḷakā tathā;
```

```
Na honti kāye daddu ca, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa, nibbattati bhavābhave;
```

```
Rogā na honti kāyasmiṃ, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa, nibbattati bhavābhave;
```

```
Na hoti cittajā pīḷā, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa, nibbattati bhavābhave;
```

```
Amittā na bhavantassa, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa, nibbattati bhavābhave;
```

```
Anūnabhogo bhavati, vipāko pattachaḍḍite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Aparampi guṇaṃ tassa, nibbattati bhavābhave;
```

```
Aggirājūhi corehi, na hoti udake bhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Aparampi <pb ed="T" n="2.0171" /> guṇaṃ tassa, nibbattati bhavābhave;
```

```
Dāsidāsā anucarā, honti cittānuvattakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Yamhi āyuppamāṇamhi, jāyate mānuse bhave;
```

```
Tato na hāyate āyu, tiṭṭhate yāvatāyukaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Abbhantarā ca bāhirā <note>bahicarā (sī. pī. ka.)</note>, negamā ca saraṭṭhakā;
```

```
Nuyuttā honti sabbepi, vuddhikāmā sukhicchakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Bhogavā yasavā homi, sirimā ñātipakkhavā;
```

```
Apetabhayasantāso, bhavehaṃ sabbato bhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Devā <pb ed="M" n="2.0107" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0106" /> manussā asurā, gandhabbā yakkharakkhasā;
```

```
Sabbe te parirakkhanti, bhave saṃsarato sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Devaloke manusse ca, anubhotvā ubho yase;
```

```
Avasāne ca nibbānaṃ, sivaṃ patto anuttaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Sambuddhamuddisitvāna, bodhiṃ vā tassa satthuno;
```

```
Yo puññaṃ pasave poso, tassa kiṃ nāma dullabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Magge <pb ed="P" n="2.0459" /> phale āgame ca, jhānābhiññāguṇesu ca;
```

```
Aññesaṃ adhiko hutvā, nibbāyāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Purehaṃ bodhiyā pattaṃ, chaḍḍetvā haṭṭhamānaso;
```

```
Imehi vīsataṅgehi, samaṅgī homi sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0172" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bodhisammajjako thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Bodhisammajjakattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Āmaṇḍaphaladāyakattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Vuṭṭhahitvā samādhimhā, caṅkamī lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Khāribhāraṃ gahetvāna, āharanto phalaṃ tadā;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, caṅkamantaṃ mahāmuniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacitto sumano, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, āmaṇḍamadadiṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ phalaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, āmaṇḍassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0108" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0107" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0173" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā āmaṇḍaphaladāyako thero imā

Gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Āmaṇḍaphaladāyakattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Sugandhattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena <note>nāmena (sabbattha)</note>, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Anubyañjanasampanno, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo;
```

```
Byāmappabhāparivuto, raṃsijālasamotthaṭo <note>raṃsijālasamosaṭo (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Assāsetā yathā cando, sūriyova pabhaṅkaro;
```

```
Nibbāpetā yathā megho, sāgarova guṇākaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Dharaṇīriva <pb ed="P" n="2.0460" /> sīlena, himavāva samādhinā;
```

```
Ākāso viya paññāya, asaṅgo anilo yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Sa kadāci mahāvīro, parisāsu visārado;
```

```
Saccāni sampakāseti, uddharanto mahājanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā hi bārāṇasiyaṃ, seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso;
```

```
Āsahaṃ dhanadhaññassa <note>anantadhanadhaññassa (ka.)</note>, pahūtassa bahū tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ, migadāyamupeccahaṃ <note>mupesahaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Visaṭṭhakantavacanaṃ<pb ed="T" n="2.0174" />, karavīkasamassaraṃ;
```

```
Haṃsarutehi <note>haṃsadundubhi (syā. pī.)</note> nigghosaṃ, viññāpentaṃ mahājanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā <pb ed="M" n="2.0109" /> devātidevaṃ taṃ, sutvāva madhuraṃ giraṃ;
```

```
Pahāyanappake bhoge, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0108" /> pabbajito cāhaṃ, na cirena bahussuto;
```

```
Ahosiṃ dhammakathiko, vicittapaṭibhāṇavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāparisamajjhehaṃ, haṭṭhacitto punappunaṃ;
```

```
Vaṇṇayiṃ hemavaṇṇassa, vaṇṇaṃ vaṇṇavisārado.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Esa khīṇāsavo buddho, anīgho chinnasaṃsayo;
```

```
Sabbakammakkhayaṃ patto, vimuttopadhisaṅkhaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Esa so bhagavā buddho, esa sīho anuttaro;
```

```
Sadevakassa lokassa, brahmacakkappavattako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Danto dametā santo ca, sametā nibbuto isi;
```

```
Nibbāpetā ca assattho, assāsetā mahājanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Vīro sūro ca vikkanto <note>dhīro ca (sī. pī.)</note>, pañño kāruṇiko vasī;
```

```
Vijitāvī ca sa jino, appagabbo anālayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Aneñjo acalo dhīmā, amoho asamo muni;
```

```
Dhorayho usabho nāgo, sīho sakko garūsupi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Virāgo vimalo brahmā, vādī sūro raṇañjaho;
```

```
Akhilo ca visallo ca, asamo saṃyato <note>vusabho (syā.), payato (pī.)</note> suci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Brāhmaṇo <pb ed="T" n="2.0175" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0461" /> samaṇo nātho, bhisakko sallakattako;
```

```
Yodho buddho sutāsuto <note>suto suto (sī. pī.)</note>, acalo mudito sito <note>dito (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Dhātā dhatā ca santi ca, kattā netā pakāsitā;
```

```
Sampahaṃsitā bhettā ca, chettā sotā pasaṃsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Akhilo ca visallo ca, anīgho akathaṃkathī;
```

```
Anejo virajo kattā, gandhā vattā pasaṃsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Tāretā atthakāretā, kāretā sampadāritā;
```

```
Pāpetā sahitā kantā, hantā ātāpī tāpaso <note>hantā, tāpitā ca visositā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Samacitto <pb ed="M" n="2.0110" /> <note>saccaṭṭhito (syā.)</note> samasamo, asahāyo dayālayo <note>dayāsayo (sī.)</note>;
```

Accherasatto <note>accheramanto (syā.)</note> akuho, katāvī isisattamo.

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Nittiṇṇakaṅkho nimmāno, appameyyo anūpamo;
```

```
Sabbavākyapathātīto, sacca neyyantagū <note>sabbaneyyantiko (syā.)</note> jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Sattasāravare <pb ed="V" n="2.0109" /> <note>sataraṃsīvare (syā.)</note> tasmiṃ, pasādo amatāvaho;
```

```
Tasmā buddhe ca dhamme ca, saṅghe saddhā mahatthikā <note>mahiddhikā (sī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Guṇehi evamādīhi, tilokasaraṇuttamaṃ;
```

```
Vaṇṇento parisāmajjhe, akaṃ <note>kathiṃ (syā.)</note> dhammakathaṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutāhaṃ tusite, anubhotvā mahāsukhaṃ;
```

```
Tato cuto manussesu, jāto homi sugandhiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Nissāso mukhagandho ca, dehagandho tatheva me;
```

```
Sedagandho ca satataṃ, sabbagandhova hoti me <note>sabbagandhotiseti me (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Mukhagandho <pb ed="T" n="2.0176" /> sadā mayhaṃ, padumuppalacampako;
```

```
Parisanto <note>ādisanto (sī.), atikanto (syā.), atisanto (pī.)</note> sadā vāti, sarīro ca tatheva me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Guṇatthavassa sabbantaṃ, phalaṃ tu <note>phalantaṃ (syā.)</note> paramabbhutaṃ;
```

```
Ekaggamanasā sabbe, vaṇṇayissaṃ <note>bhāsitassa (syā.)</note> suṇātha me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Guṇaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0462" /> buddhassa vatvāna, hitāya ca na sadisaṃ <note>hitāya janasandhisu (sī. pī.), hitāya naṃ sukhāvahaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sukhito <note>sucitto (syā.)</note> homi sabbattha, saṅgho vīrasamāyuto <note>saraddhanisamāyuto (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Yasassī sukhito kanto, jutimā piyadassano;
```

```
Vattā aparibhūto ca, niddoso paññavā tathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Khīṇe āyusi <note>pāsusi (syā.)</note> nibbānaṃ, sulabhaṃ buddhabhattino;
```

```
Tesaṃ hetuṃ pavakkhāmi, taṃ suṇātha yathātathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Santaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0111" /> yasaṃ bhagavato, vidhinā abhivādayaṃ;
```

```
Tattha tatthūpapannopi <note>yattha tatthūpapannopi (sī. pī.)</note>, yasassī tena homahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Dukkhassantakaraṃ buddhaṃ, dhammaṃ santamasaṅkhataṃ;
```

```
Vaṇṇayaṃ sukhado āsiṃ, sattānaṃ sukhito tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Guṇaṃ vadanto buddhassa, buddhapītisamāyuto;
```

```
Sakantiṃ parakantiñca, janayiṃ tena kantimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Jino te titthikākiṇṇe <note>janoghe titthakākiṇṇe (sī. pī.), jino yo titthikātiṇṇo (syā.)</note>, abhibhuyya kutitthiye;
```

```
Guṇaṃ vadanto jotesiṃ <note>thomesiṃ (syā.)</note>, nāyakaṃ jutimā tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Piyakārī janassāpi, sambuddhassa guṇaṃ vadaṃ;
```

```
Saradova sasaṅkohaṃ, tenāsiṃ piyadassano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Yathāsattivasenāhaṃ<pb ed="T" n="2.0177" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0110" />, sabbavācāhi santhaviṃ;
```

```
Sugataṃ tena vāgiso, vicittapaṭibhānavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Ye bālā vimatiṃ pattā, paribhonti mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Niggahiṃ te saddhammena, paribhūto na tenahaṃ <note>paribhūtena tenahaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhavaṇṇena sattānaṃ, kilese apanesahaṃ;
```

```
Nikkilesamano homi, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Sotūnaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0463" /> vuddhimajaniṃ <note>buddhimajaniṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, buddhānussatidesako;
```

```
Tenāhamāsiṃ <note>tenāpi cāsiṃ (syā.)</note> sappañño, nipuṇatthavipassako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇo, tiṇṇasaṃsārasāgaro;
```

```
Sikhīva anupādāno, pāpuṇissāmi nibbutiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappasmiṃ, yamahaṃ santhaviṃ jinaṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhavaṇṇassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0112" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā sugandho thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Sugandhattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Tiṇadāyakavaggo tepaññāsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Tiṇado <pb ed="T" n="2.0178" /> mañcado ceva, saraṇabbhañjanappado;
```

```
Supaṭo daṇḍadāyī ca, nelapūjī tatheva ca.
```

```
Bodhisammajjako maṇḍo, sugandho dasamoti ca;
```

```
Gāthāsataṃ satevīsaṃ, gaṇitañcettha sabbaso.
```

### 54. Kaccāyanavaggo

#### 1. Mahākaccāyanattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0179" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0113" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0111" /> nāma jino, anejo ajitaṃ jayo;
```

```
Satasahasse kappānaṃ, ito uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Vīro kamalapattakkho, sasaṅkavimalānano;
```

```
Kanakācalasaṅkāso <note>kañcanatacasaṅkāso (syā.)</note>, ravidittisamappabho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Sattanettamanohārī, varalakkhaṇabhūsito;
```

```
Sabbavākyapathātīto, manujāmarasakkato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Sambuddho bodhayaṃ satte, vāgīso madhurassaro;
```

```
Karuṇānibandhasantāno, parisāsu visārado.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Deseti <pb ed="P" n="2.0464" /> madhuraṃ dhammaṃ, catusaccūpasaṃhitaṃ;
```

```
Nimugge mohapaṅkamhi, samuddharati pāṇine.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā ekacaro hutvā, tāpaso himavālayo;
```

```
Nabhasā mānusaṃ lokaṃ, gacchanto jinamaddasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Upecca santikaṃ tassa, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
```

```
Vaṇṇayantassa vīrassa, sāvakassa mahāguṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkhittena mayā vuttaṃ, vitthārena pakāsayaṃ;
```

```
Parisaṃ mañca toseti, yathā kaccāyano ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0180" /> evamidhekaccaṃ <note>evaṃvidhaṃ kañci (sī. pī.)</note>, aññaṃ passāmi sāvakaṃ;
```

```
Tasmātadagge <note>tasmetadagge (sī.)</note> esaggo, evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ vimhito hutvā, sutvā vākyaṃ manoramaṃ;
```

```
Himavantaṃ gamitvāna, āhitvā <note>āhatvā (sī. pī.)</note> pupphasañcayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjetvā lokasaraṇaṃ, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ;
```

```
Tadā mamāsayaṃ ñatvā, byākāsi sa raṇañjaho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘‘Passathetaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0112" /> isivaraṃ, niddhantakanakattacaṃ;
```

```
Uddhaggalomaṃ pīṇaṃsaṃ, acalaṃ pañjaliṃ ṭhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hāsaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0114" /> supuṇṇanayanaṃ, buddhavaṇṇagatāsayaṃ;
```

```
Dhammajaṃ uggahadayaṃ <note>dhammaṃva viggahavaraṃ (sī.), dhammapaṭiggahavaraṃ (pī.)</note>, amatāsittasannibhaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Kaccānassa guṇaṃ sutvā, taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayaṃ ṭhito;
```

```
Anāgatamhi addhāne, gotamassa mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Kaccāno nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussuto mahāñāṇī, adhippāyavidū mune;
```

```
Pāpuṇissati taṃ ṭhānaṃ, yathāyaṃ byākato mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Duve bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na gacchāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Duve <pb ed="T" n="2.0181" /> kule pajāyāmi, khattiye atha brāhmaṇe;
```

```
Nīce kule na jāyāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="P" n="2.0465" /> ca bhave dāni, jāto ujjeniyaṃ pure <note>jāto, ujjeniyaṃ pure rame (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Pajjotassa ca caṇḍassa, purohitadijādhino <note>purohitadijātino (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Putto tiriṭivacchassa <note>tiriṭavacchassa (sī.), tipitivacchassa (syā.)</note>, nipuṇo vedapāragū;
```

```
Mātā ca candimā nāma, kaccānohaṃ varattaco.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Vīmaṃsanatthaṃ buddhassa, bhūmipālena pesito;
```

```
Disvā mokkhapuradvāraṃ, nāyakaṃ guṇasañcayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā ca vimalaṃ vākyaṃ, gatipaṅkavisosanaṃ;
```

```
Pāpuṇiṃ amataṃ santaṃ, sesehi saha sattahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Adhippāyavidū jāto, sugatassa mahāmate;
```

```
Ṭhapito etadagge ca, susamiddhamanoratho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0115" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0113" /> vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike; Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākaccāyano thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Mahākaccāyanattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Vakkalittheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="T" n="2.0182" /> satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako;
```

```
Anomanāmo amito, nāmena padumuttaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Padumākāravadano, padumāmalasucchavī;
```

```
Lokenānupalittova toyena padumaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Vīro padumapattakkho, kanto ca padumaṃ yathā;
```

```
Padumuttaragandhova, tasmā so padumuttaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Lokajeṭṭho ca nimmāno, andhānaṃ nayanūpamo;
```

```
Santaveso guṇanidhi, karuṇāmatisāgaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Sa kadāci mahāvīro, brahmāsurasuraccito;
```

```
Sadevamanujākiṇṇe, janamajjhe jinuttamo <note>januttamo (syā. pī.), anuttamo (ka.) vaṅgīsattherāpadānepi</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Vadanena sugandhena, madhurena rutena ca;
```

```
Rañjayaṃ parisaṃ sabbaṃ, santhavī sāvakaṃ sakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhādhimutto <pb ed="P" n="2.0466" /> sumati, mama dassanalālaso <note>dassanasālayo (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Natthi etādiso añño, yathāyaṃ bhikkhu vakkali.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, nagare brāhmaṇatrajo;
```

```
Hutvā sutvā ca taṃ vākyaṃ, taṃ ṭhānamabhirocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Sasāvakaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0116" /> taṃ vimalaṃ, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Sattāhaṃ bhojayitvāna, dussehacchādayiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Nipacca <pb ed="T" n="2.0183" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0114" /> sirasā tassa, anantaguṇasāgare;
```

```
Nimuggo pītisampuṇṇo, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo so tayā santhavito, ito sattamake muni <note>idha saddhādhimutto isi (syā.), ito sattamakehani (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Bhikkhu saddhāvataṃ aggo, tādiso homahaṃ mune’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ vutte mahāvīro, anāvaraṇadassano;
```

```
Imaṃ vākyaṃ udīresi, parisāya mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘‘Passathetaṃ māṇavakaṃ, pītamaṭṭhanivāsanaṃ;
```

```
Hemayaññopacitaṅgaṃ <note>hemayaññopavītaṅgaṃ (sī.)</note>, jananettamanoharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘‘Eso anāgataddhāne, gotamassa mahesino;
```

```
Aggo saddhādhimuttānaṃ, sāvakoyaṃ bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devabhūto manusso vā, sabbasantāpavajjito;
```

```
Sabbabhogaparibyūḷho, sukhito saṃsarissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Vakkali nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammavisesena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbattha sukhito hutvā, saṃsaranto bhavābhave;
```

```
Sāvatthiyaṃ pure jāto, kule aññatare ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Nonītasukhumālaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0184" /> maṃ, jātapallavakomalaṃ;
```

```
Mandaṃ uttānasayanaṃ, pisācabhayatajjitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Pādamūle mahesissa, sāyesuṃ dīnamānasā;
```

```
Imaṃ dadāma te nātha, saraṇaṃ hohi nāyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0117" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0467" /> paṭiggahi so maṃ, bhītānaṃ saraṇo muni;
```

```
Jālinā cakkaṅkitena <note>saṅkalaṅkena (sī.)</note>, mudukomalapāṇinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā pabhuti tenāhaṃ, arakkheyyena rakkhito;
```

```
Sabbaveravinimutto <note>sabbabyādhivinimutto (syā.), sabbūpadhivinimutto (pī.)</note>, sukhena parivuddhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Sugatena <pb ed="V" n="2.0115" /> vinā bhūto, ukkaṇṭhāmi muhuttakaṃ;
```

```
Jātiyā sattavassohaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbapāramisambhūtaṃ, nīlakkhinayanaṃ <note>laṅkinīlayanaṃ (sī.)</note> varaṃ;
```

```
Rūpaṃ sabbasubhākiṇṇaṃ, atitto viharāmahaṃ <note>vihayāmahaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Buddharūparatiṃ <note>buddho rūparatiṃ (sī.)</note> ñatvā, tadā ovadi maṃ jino;
```

```
‘Alaṃ vakkali kiṃ rūpe, ramase bālanandite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo hi passati saddhammaṃ, so maṃ passati paṇḍito;
```

```
Apassamāno saddhammaṃ, maṃ passampi na passati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anantādīnavo kāyo, visarukkhasamūpamo;
```

```
Āvāso sabbarogānaṃ, puñjo dukkhassa kevalo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nibbindiya tato rūpe, khandhānaṃ udayabbayaṃ;
```

```
Passa upakkilesānaṃ, sukhenantaṃ gamissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0185" /> tenānusiṭṭhohaṃ, nāyakena hitesinā;
```

```
Gijjhakūṭaṃ samāruyha, jhāyāmi girikandare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Ṭhito pabbatapādamhi, assāsayi <note>mamāhaso (sī.)</note> mahāmuni;
```

```
Vakkalīti jino vācaṃ, taṃ sutvā mudito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Pakkhandiṃ selapabbhāre, anekasataporise;
```

```
Tadā buddhānubhāvena, sukheneva mahiṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Punopi <note>punāpi (syā.), muni maṃ (ka.)</note> dhammaṃ deseti, khandhānaṃ udayabbayaṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ dhammamaññāya, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Sumahāparisamajjhe<pb ed="M" n="2.0118" />, tadā maṃ caraṇantago;
```

```
Aggaṃ saddhādhimuttānaṃ, paññapesi mahāmati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0468" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="2.0116" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā vakkalitthero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Vakkalittherassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Mahākappinattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0186" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Udito ajaṭākāse <note>jagadākāse (sī.), jaladākāse (pī.)</note>, ravīva saradambare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Vacanābhāya bodheti, veneyyapadumāni so;
```

```
Kilesapaṅkaṃ soseti, matiraṃsīhi nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Titthiyānaṃ yase <note>yaso (sī. pī.)</note> hanti, khajjotābhā yathā ravi;
```

Saccatthābhaṃ pakāseti, ratanaṃva divākaro.

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Guṇānaṃ āyatibhūto, ratanānaṃva sāgaro;
```

```
Pajjunnoriva bhūtāni, dhammameghena vassati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Akkhadasso tadā āsiṃ, nagare haṃsasavhaye;
```

```
Upecca dhammamassosiṃ, jalajuttamanāmino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādakassa bhikkhūnaṃ, sāvakassa katāvino;
```

```
Guṇaṃ pakāsayantassa, tappayantassa <note>tosayantassa (sī.), hāsayantassa (syā.), vāsayantassa (pī.)</note> me manaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā patīto sumano, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Sasissaṃ bhojayitvāna, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0119" /> haṃsasamabhāgo, haṃsadundubhinissano <note>haṃsadundubhisussaro (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Passathetaṃ mahāmattaṃ, vinicchayavisāradaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Patitaṃ pādamūle me, samuggatatanūruhaṃ;
```

```
Jīmūtavaṇṇaṃ pīṇaṃsaṃ, pasannanayanānanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Parivārena <pb ed="T" n="2.0187" /> mahatā, rājayuttaṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Eso katāvino ṭhānaṃ, pattheti muditāsayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iminā <pb ed="V" n="2.0117" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0469" /> paṇipātena, cāgena paṇidhīhi ca <note>piṇḍapātena, cetanā paṇidhīhi ca (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Kappasatasahassāni, nupapajjati duggatiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devesu devasobhaggaṃ, manussesu mahantataṃ;
```

```
Anubhotvāna sesena <note>abhutvāva sesena (sī.), anubhotvāva sesena (syā.)</note>, nibbānaṃ pāpuṇissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Kappino nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Tatohaṃ sukataṃ kāraṃ, katvāna jinasāsane;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tusitaṃ agamāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Devamānusarajjāni, sataso anusāsiya;
```

```
Bārāṇasiyamāsanne, jāto keniyajātiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassaparivārena <note>satasahassaparivāro (syā.)</note>, sapajāpatiko ahaṃ;
```

```
Pañca paccekabuddhānaṃ, satāni samupaṭṭhahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Temāsaṃ bhojayitvāna, pacchādamha ticīvaraṃ;
```

```
Tato cutā mayaṃ sabbe, ahumha tidasūpagā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Puno sabbe manussattaṃ, agamimha tato cutā;
```

```
Kukkuṭamhi pure jātā, himavantassa passato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Kappino <pb ed="T" n="2.0188" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0120" /> nāmahaṃ āsiṃ, rājaputto mahāyaso;
```

```
Sesāmaccakule jātā, mameva parivārayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Mahārajjasukhaṃ patto, sabbakāmasamiddhimā;
```

```
Vāṇijehi samakkhātaṃ, buddhuppādamahaṃ suṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddho loke samuppanno, asamo ekapuggalo;
```

```
So pakāseti saddhammaṃ, amataṃ sukhamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘‘Suyuttā tassa sissā ca, sumuttā ca anāsavā’;
```

```
‘‘Sutvā nesaṃ suvacanaṃ, sakkaritvāna vāṇije.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Pahāya rajjaṃ sāmacco, nikkhamiṃ buddhamāmako;
```

```
Nadiṃ disvā mahācandaṃ, pūritaṃ samatittikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Appatiṭṭhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0118" /> anālambaṃ, duttaraṃ sīghavāhiniṃ;
```

```
Guṇaṃ saritvā buddhassa, sotthinā samatikkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhavasotaṃ sace buddho, tiṇṇo lokantagū vidū <note>vibhū (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Etena saccavajjena, gamanaṃ me samijjhatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yadi <pb ed="P" n="2.0470" /> santigamo maggo, mokkho caccantikaṃ <note>mokkhadaṃ santikaṃ (syā.)</note> sukhaṃ;
```

```
Etena saccavajjena, gamanaṃ me samijjhatu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṅgho ce tiṇṇakantāro, puññakkhetto anuttaro;
```

```
Etena saccavajjena, gamanaṃ me samijjhatu’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Saha kate saccavare, maggā apagataṃ jalaṃ;
```

```
Tato sukhena uttiṇṇo, nadītīre manorame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Nisinnaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0189" /> addasaṃ buddhaṃ, udentaṃva pabhaṅkaraṃ;
```

```
Jalantaṃ hemaselaṃva, dīparukkhaṃva jotitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Sasiṃva tārāsahitaṃ, sāvakehi purakkhataṃ;
```

```
Vāsavaṃ viya vassantaṃ, desanājaladantaraṃ <note>devena jalanandanaṃ (syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Vanditvāna sahāmacco, ekamantamupāvisiṃ;
```

```
Tato no āsayaṃ <note>tato ajjhāsayaṃ (syā.)</note> ñatvā, buddho dhammamadesayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvāna <pb ed="M" n="2.0121" /> dhammaṃ vimalaṃ, avocumha mayaṃ jinaṃ;
```

```
‘Pabbājehi mahāvīra, nibbindāmha <note>nibbinnāmha (sī. pī.), otiṇṇamha (syā.)</note> mayaṃ bhave’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘‘Svakkhāto bhikkhave dhammo, dukkhantakaraṇāya vo;
```

```
Caratha brahmacariyaṃ’, iccāha munisattamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Saha vācāya sabbepi, bhikkhuvesadharā mayaṃ;
```

```
Ahumha upasampannā, sotāpannā ca sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Tato jetavanaṃ gantvā, anusāsi vināyako;
```

```
Anusiṭṭho jinenāhaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Tato bhikkhusahassāni <note>bhikkhusahassaṃ taṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, anusāsimahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Mamānusāsanakarā, tepi āsuṃ anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhuovādakānaggo, kappinoti mahājane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahasse <pb ed="V" n="2.0119" /> kataṃ kammaṃ, phalaṃ dassesi me idha;
```

```
Pamutto saravegova, kilese jhāpayiṃ <note>jhāpayī (sī.)</note> mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0190" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākappino thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Mahākappinattherassāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Dabbamallaputtattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="P" n="2.0471" /> nāma jino, sabbalokavidū muni;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Desanākusalo buddho, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako <pb ed="M" n="2.0122" /> kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Sampatte titthiye sabbe, pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi <note>patiṭṭhahi (syā. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi, suññataṃ <note>suññakaṃ (sī.) evamuparipi</note> titthiyehi ca;
```

```
Vicittaṃ arahantehi, vasībhūtehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ, uggato so mahāmuni;
```

```
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni<pb ed="T" n="2.0191" />, āyu vijjati tāvade;
```

```
Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, seṭṭhiputto mahāyaso;
```

```
Upetvā lokapajjotaṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Senāsanāni bhikkhūnaṃ, paññāpentaṃ sasāvakaṃ;
```

```
Kittayantassa vacanaṃ, suṇitvā mudito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Adhikāraṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0120" /> sasaṅghassa, katvā tassa mahesino;
```

```
Nipacca sirasā pāde, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāha sa mahāvīro, mama kammaṃ pakittayaṃ;
```

```
‘Yo sasaṅghamabhojesi, sattāhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘‘Soyaṃ kamalapattakkho, sīhaṃso kanakattaco;
```

```
Mama pādamūle nipati <note>patito (pī.)</note>, patthayaṃ ṭhānamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sāvako tassa buddhassa, dabbo nāmena vissuto;
```

```
Senāsanapaññāpako, aggo hessatiyaṃ tadā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0192" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0123" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0472" /> vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, vipassī nāma nāyako;
```

```
Uppajji cārudassano <note>cārunayano (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, sabbadhammavipassako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Duṭṭhacitto upavadiṃ, sāvakaṃ tassa tādino;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇaṃ, suddhoti ca vijāniya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Tasseva naravīrassa, sāvakānaṃ mahesinaṃ;
```

```
Salākañca gahetvāna <note>salākaṃ paggahetvāna (sī. pī.)</note>, khīrodanamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Sāsanaṃ jotayitvāna, abhibhuyya kutitthiye;
```

```
Vineyye vinayitvāva, nibbuto so sasāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Sasisse nibbute nāthe, atthamentamhi sāsane;
```

```
Devā kandiṃsu saṃviggā, muttakesā rudammukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbāyissati <pb ed="V" n="2.0121" /> dhammakkho, na passissāma subbate;
```

```
Na suṇissāma saddhammaṃ, aho no appapuññatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāyaṃ pathavī sabbā, acalā sā calācalā <note>calācalī (sī.), pulāpulī (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sāgaro ca sasokova, vinadī karuṇaṃ giraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Catuddisā dundubhiyo, nādayiṃsu amānusā;
```

```
Samantato asaniyo, phaliṃsu ca bhayāvahā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘Ukkā <pb ed="T" n="2.0193" /> patiṃsu nabhasā, dhūmaketu ca dissati;
```

```
Sadhūmā jālavaṭṭā ca <note>sabbathalajasattā ca (sī.)</note>, raviṃsu karuṇaṃ migā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘Uppāde dāruṇe disvā, sāsanatthaṅgasūcake;
```

```
Saṃviggā bhikkhavo satta, cintayimha mayaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Sāsanena vināmhākaṃ, jīvitena alaṃ mayaṃ;
```

```
Pavisitvā mahāraññaṃ, yuñjāma jinasāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘Addasamha <pb ed="M" n="2.0124" /> tadāraññe, ubbiddhaṃ selamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Nisseṇiyā tamāruyha, nisseṇiṃ pātayimhase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="P" n="2.0473" /> ovadi no thero, buddhuppādo sudullabho;
```

```
Saddhātidullabhā laddhā, thokaṃ sesañca sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘Nipatanti khaṇātītā, anante dukkhasāgare;
```

```
Tasmā payogo kattabbo, yāva ṭhāti mune mataṃ <note>yāva tiṭṭhati sāsanaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Arahā āsi so thero, anāgāmī tadānugo;
```

```
Susīlā itare yuttā, devalokaṃ agamhase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbuto tiṇṇasaṃsāro, suddhāvāse ca ekako;
```

```
Ahañca pakkusāti ca, sabhiyo bāhiyo tathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Kumārakassapo ceva, tattha tatthūpagā mayaṃ;
```

```
Saṃsārabandhanā muttā, gotamenānukampitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Mallesu kusinārāyaṃ, jāto gabbheva me sato;
```

```
Mātā matā citāruḷhā, tato nippatito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Patito <pb ed="T" n="2.0194" /> dabbapuñjamhi, tato dabboti vissuto;
```

```
Brahmacārībalenāhaṃ, vimutto sattavassiko.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘Khīrodanabalenāhaṃ<pb ed="V" n="2.0122" />, pañcahaṅgehupāgato;
```

```
Khīṇāsavopavādena, pāpehi bahucodito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘Ubho puññañca pāpañca, vītivattomhi dānihaṃ;
```

```
Patvāna paramaṃ santiṃ, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Senāsanaṃ paññāpayiṃ, hāsayitvāna subbate;
```

```
Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā dabbamallaputto thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Dabbamallaputtattherassāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Kumārakassapattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="M" n="2.0125" /> satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako;
```

```
Sabbalokahito vīro, padumuttaranāmako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0195" /> brāhmaṇo hutvā, vissuto vedapāragū;
```

```
Divāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ, addasaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘Catusaccaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0474" /> pakāsentaṃ, bodhayantaṃ sadevakaṃ;
```

```
Vicittakathikānaggaṃ, vaṇṇayantaṃ mahājane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā muditacittohaṃ, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Nānārattehi vatthehi, alaṅkaritvāna maṇḍapaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘Nānāratanapajjotaṃ, sasaṅghaṃ bhojayiṃ tahiṃ;
```

```
Bhojayitvāna sattāhaṃ, nānaggarasabhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘Nānācittehi <note>nānāvaṇṇehi (sī.)</note> pupphehi, pūjayitvā sasāvakaṃ <note>mahāvīraṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Nipacca pādamūlamhi, taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="V" n="2.0123" /> munivaro āha, karuṇekarasāsayo <note>karuṇo karuṇālayo (syā.)</note>;
```

```
‘Passathetaṃ dijavaraṃ, padumānanalocanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pītipāmojjabahulaṃ, samuggatatanūruhaṃ;
```

```
Hāsamhitavisālakkhaṃ, mama sāsanalālasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘‘Patitaṃ pādamūle me, ekāvatthasumānasaṃ <note>ekavatthaṃ sumānasaṃ (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Esa pattheti taṃ ṭhānaṃ, vicittakathikattanaṃ <note>vicittakathikattadaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Kumārakassapo nāma, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vicittapupphadussānaṃ<pb ed="T" n="2.0196" />, ratanānañca vāhasā;
```

```
Vicittakathikānaṃ so, aggataṃ pāpuṇissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="2.0126" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Paribbhamaṃ bhavābhave <note>bhavākāse (sī. pī.)</note>, raṅgamajjhe yathā naṭo;
```

```
Sākhamigatrajo hutvā, migiyā kucchimokkamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā mayi kucchigate, vajjhavāro upaṭṭhito;
```

```
Sākhena cattā me mātā, nigrodhaṃ saraṇaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘Tena sā migarājena, maraṇā parimocitā;
```

```
Pariccajitvā sapāṇaṃ <note>saṃpāṇaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, mamevaṃ ovadī tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nigrodhameva seveyya, na sākhamupasaṃvase;
```

```
Nigrodhasmiṃ mataṃ seyyo, yañce sākhamhi jīvitaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘Tenānusiṭṭhā migayūthapena, ahañca mātā ca tathetare ca <note>citare ca (syā.), tassovādena (pī.), citare ca tassovādaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Āgamma <pb ed="P" n="2.0475" /> rammaṃ tusitādhivāsaṃ, gatā pavāsaṃ sagharaṃ yatheva.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘Puno kassapavīrassa, atthamentamhi sāsane;
```

```
Āruyha selasikharaṃ, yuñjitvā jinasāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘Idānāhaṃ rājagahe, jāto seṭṭhikule ahuṃ;
```

```
Āpannasattā me mātā, pabbaji anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘Sagabbhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0197" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0124" /> taṃ viditvāna, devadattamupānayuṃ;
```

```
So avoca ‘vināsetha, pāpikaṃ bhikkhuniṃ imaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘Idānipi munindena, jinena anukampitā;
```

```
Sukhinī ajanī mayhaṃ, mātā bhikkhunupassaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ viditvā mahīpālo, kosalo maṃ aposayi;
```

```
Kumāraparihārena, nāmenāhañca kassapo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Mahākassapamāgamma, ahaṃ kumārakassapo;
```

```
Vammikasadisaṃ kāyaṃ, sutvā buddhena desitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="M" n="2.0127" /> cittaṃ vimucci me, anupādāya sabbaso;
```

```
Pāyāsiṃ damayitvāhaṃ, etadaggamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā kumārakassapo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Kumārakassapattherassāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

Catuvīsatimaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

#### 6. Bāhiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘Ito <pb ed="T" n="2.0198" /> satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako;
```

```
Mahappabho tilokaggo, nāmena padumuttaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Khippābhiññassa bhikkhussa, guṇaṃ kittayato mune;
```

```
Sutvā udaggacittohaṃ, kāraṃ katvā mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Datvā sattāhikaṃ dānaṃ, sasissassa mune ahaṃ;
```

```
Abhivādiya sambuddhaṃ, taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Tato maṃ byākari buddho, ‘etaṃ passatha brāhmaṇaṃ;
```

```
Patitaṃ pādamūle me, cariyaṃ paccavekkhaṇaṃ <note>pasannanayanānanaṃ (sī.), pīnasampannavekkhaṇaṃ (syā.), pīṇaṃsaṃ paccavekkhaṇaṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hemayaññopacitaṅgaṃ<pb ed="V" n="2.0125" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0476" />, avadātatanuttacaṃ;
```

```
Palambabimbatamboṭṭhaṃ, setatiṇhasamaṃ dijaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘‘Guṇathāmabahutaraṃ, samuggatatanūruhaṃ;
```

```
Guṇoghāyatanībhūtaṃ, pītisamphullitānanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘‘Eso patthayate ṭhānaṃ, khippābhiññassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Anāgate mahāvīro, gotamo nāma hessati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="M" n="2.0128" /> dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Bāhiyo nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā hi tuṭṭho vuṭṭhāya, yāvajīvaṃ mahāmune;
```

```
Kāraṃ katvā cuto saggaṃ, agaṃ sabhavanaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Devabhūto <pb ed="T" n="2.0199" /> manusso vā, sukhito tassa kammuno;
```

```
Vāhasā saṃsaritvāna, sampattimanubhomahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Puna kassapavīrassa, atthamentamhi <note>atthaṅgatamhi (syā.)</note> sāsane;
```

```
Āruyha selasikharaṃ, yuñjitvā jinasāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘Visuddhasīlo sappañño, jinasāsanakārako;
```

```
Tato cutā pañca janā, devalokaṃ agamhase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘Tatohaṃ bāhiyo jāto, bhārukacche puruttame;
```

```
Tato nāvāya pakkhando <note>pakkhanto (sī.), pakkanto (pī.)</note>, sāgaraṃ appasiddhiyaṃ <note>atthasiddhiyaṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
‘‘Tato nāvā abhijjittha, gantvāna katipāhakaṃ;
```

```
Tadā bhīsanake ghore, patito makarākare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ vāyamitvāna, santaritvā mahodadhiṃ;
```

```
Suppādapaṭṭanavaraṃ <note>suppārapaṭṭanavaraṃ (sī. pī.)</note>, sampatto mandavedhito <note>mandamedhiko (sī.), mandavedito (syā.), maddaverataṃ (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘Dārucīraṃ nivāsetvā, gāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisiṃ;
```

```
Tadāha so jano tuṭṭho, arahāyamidhāgato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Imaṃ annena pānena, vatthena sayanena ca;
```

```
Bhesajjena ca sakkatvā, hessāma sukhitā mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
‘‘Paccayānaṃ tadā lābhī, tehi sakkatapūjito;
```

```
Arahāhanti saṅkappaṃ, uppādesiṃ ayoniso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="V" n="2.0126" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0477" /> me cittamaññāya, codayī pubbadevatā;
```

```
‘Na tvaṃ upāyamaggaññū, kuto tvaṃ arahā bhave’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
‘‘Codito <pb ed="T" n="2.0200" /> tāya saṃviggo, tadāhaṃ paripucchi taṃ;
```

```
‘Ke vā ete kuhiṃ loke, arahanto naruttamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sāvatthiyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0129" /> kosalamandire jino, pahūtapañño varabhūrimedhaso;
```

```
So sakyaputto arahā anāsavo, deseti dhammaṃ arahattapattiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tadassa sutvā vacanaṃ supīṇito <note>pīṇitvā (ka.)</note>, nidhiṃva laddhā kapaṇoti vimhito;
```

```
Udaggacitto arahattamuttamaṃ, sudassanaṃ daṭṭhumanantagocaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tadā tato nikkhamitvāna satthuno <note>nikkhamituna satthuvaraṃ (sī.)</note>, sadā jinaṃ passāmi vimalānanaṃ <note>parājinaṃ passāmi kamalānanaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Upecca rammaṃ vijitavhayaṃ vanaṃ, dije apucchiṃ kuhiṃ lokanandano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tato avocuṃ naradevavandito, puraṃ paviṭṭho asanesanāya so;
```

```
Sasova <note>paccehi (sī. syā.)</note> khippaṃ munidassanussuko, upecca vandāhi tamaggapuggalaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘Tatohaṃ tuvaṭaṃ gantvā, sāvatthiṃ puramuttamaṃ;
```

```
Vicarantaṃ tamaddakkhiṃ, piṇḍatthaṃ apihāgidhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘Pattapāṇiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0201" /> alolakkhaṃ, pācayantaṃ pītākaraṃ <note>bhājayantaṃ viyāmataṃ (sī.), jotayantaṃ idhāmataṃ (syā.), bhājayantaṃ idaṃmataṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sirīnilayasaṅkāsaṃ, ravidittiharānanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ samecca nipaccāhaṃ, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ;
```

```
‘Kupathe vippanaṭṭhassa, saraṇaṃ hohi gotama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pāṇasantāraṇatthāya<pb ed="P" n="2.0478" />, piṇḍāya vicarāmahaṃ;
```

```
Na te dhammakathākālo, iccāha munisattamo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā punappunaṃ buddhaṃ, āyāciṃ dhammalālaso;
```

```
Yo me dhammamadesesi, gambhīraṃ suññataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="M" n="2.0130" /> dhammaṃ suṇitvāna, pāpuṇiṃ āsavakkhayaṃ;
```

```
Parikkhīṇāyuko santo, aho satthānukampako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ thero viyākāsi, bāhiyo dārucīriyo;
```

```
Saṅkārakūṭe patito, bhūtāviṭṭhāya gāviyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘Attano <pb ed="V" n="2.0127" /> pubbacariyaṃ, kittayitvā mahāmati;
```

```
Parinibbāyi so thero <note>vīro (sī.), dhīro (syā.)</note>, sāvatthiyaṃ puruttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘Nagarā <pb ed="T" n="2.0202" /> nikkhamanto taṃ, disvāna isisattamo;
```

```
Dārucīradharaṃ dhīraṃ, bāhiyaṃ bāhitāgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘Bhūmiyaṃ patitaṃ dantaṃ, indaketūva pātitaṃ;
```

```
Gatāyuṃ sukkhakilesaṃ <note>gatāyu saṃgataklesaṃ (sī. pī.), tadāyu saṅkatālesaṃ (ka.)</note>, jinasāsanakārakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘Tato āmantayī satthā, sāvake sāsane rate;
```

```
‘Gaṇhatha netvā <note>hutvā (syā. pī. ka.)</note> jhāpetha, tanuṃ sabrahmacārino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘‘Thūpaṃ karotha pūjetha, nibbuto so mahāmati;
```

```
Khippābhiññānamesaggo, sāvako me vacokaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sahassamapi ce gāthā, anatthapadasañhitā;
```

```
Ekaṃ gāthāpadaṃ seyyo, yaṃ sutvā upasammati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yattha āpo ca pathavī, tejo vāyo na gādhati;
```

```
Na tattha sukkā jotanti, ādicco na pakāsati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na tattha candimā bhāti, tamo tattha na vijjati;
```

```
Yadā ca attanā vedi, munimonena brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atha <pb ed="M" n="2.0131" /> rūpā arūpā ca, sukhadukkhā vimuccati’;
```

```
Iccevaṃ abhaṇī nātho, tilokasaraṇo muni’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā bāhiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Bāhiyattherassāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Mahākoṭṭhikattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0203" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0479" /> nāma jino, sabbalokavidū muni;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Desanākusalo buddho, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako <pb ed="V" n="2.0128" /> kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Sampatte titthiye sabbe, pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi, suññataṃ titthiyehi ca;
```

```
Vicittaṃ arahantehi, vasībhūtehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ, uggato so mahāmuni;
```

```
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni, āyu vijjati tāvade;
```

```
Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, brāhmaṇo vedapāragū;
```

```
Upecca sabbalokaggaṃ <note>sabbasāraggaṃ (sī.), sattapāragaṃ (pī.)</note>, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā so sāvakaṃ vīro, pabhinnamatigocaraṃ;
```

```
Atthe dhamme nirutte ca, paṭibhāne ca kovidaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi, taṃ sutvā mudito ahaṃ;
```

```
Sasāvakaṃ jinavaraṃ, sattāhaṃ bhojayiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘Dussehacchādayitvāna<pb ed="T" n="2.0204" />, sasissaṃ buddhisāgaraṃ <note>buddhasāgaraṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Nipacca pādamūlamhi, taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="M" n="2.0132" /> avoca lokaggo, ‘passathetaṃ dijuttamaṃ;
```

```
Vinataṃ pādamūle me, kamalodarasappabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddhaseṭṭhassa <note>seṭṭhaṃ buddhassa (syā. ka.)</note> bhikkhussa, ṭhānaṃ patthayate ayaṃ;
```

```
Tāya saddhāya cāgena, saddhammassavanena <note>tena dhammassavena (sī. pī. ka.)</note> ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbattha sukhito hutvā, saṃsaritvā bhavābhave;
```

```
Anāgatamhi addhāne, lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="2.0480" /> dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Koṭṭhiko nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Mettacitto paricariṃ, sato paññāsamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="2.0129" /> kammavipākena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
‘‘Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
‘‘Duve <pb ed="T" n="2.0205" /> bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na gacchāmi, suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
‘‘Duve kule pajāyāmi, khattiye atha brāhmaṇe;
```

```
‘‘Nīce kule na jāyāmi, suciṇṇassa idaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, brahmabandhu ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Sāvatthiyaṃ vippakule, paccājāto mahaddhane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
‘‘Mātā candavatī nāma, pitā me assalāyano;
```

```
Yadā me pitaraṃ buddho, vinayī sabbasuddhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0133" /> pasanno sugate, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Moggallāno ācariyo, upajjhā sārisambhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
‘‘Kesesu chijjamānesu, diṭṭhi chinnā samūlikā;
```

```
Nivāsento ca kāsāvaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne ca me mati;
```

```
Pabhinnā tena lokaggo, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
‘‘Asandiṭṭhaṃ viyākāsiṃ, upatissena pucchito;
```

```
Paṭisambhidāsu tenāhaṃ, aggo sambuddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0206" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā mahākoṭṭhiko thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Mahākoṭṭhikattherassāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Uruveḷakassapattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="V" n="2.0130" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0481" /> nāma jino, sabbalokavidū muni;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Desanākusalo buddho, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Sampatte titthiye sabbe, pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi, suññataṃ titthiyehi ca;
```

```
Vicittaṃ arahantehi, vasībhūtehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ, uggato so mahāmuni;
```

```
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni<pb ed="M" n="2.0134" />, āyu vijjati tāvade;
```

```
Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyā, brāhmaṇo sādhusammato;
```

```
Upecca lokapajjotaṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="T" n="2.0207" /> mahāparisatiṃ, mahāparisasāvakaṃ;
```

```
Ṭhapentaṃ etadaggamhi, sutvāna mudito ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
‘‘Mahatā parivārena, nimantetvā mahājinaṃ;
```

```
Brāhmaṇānaṃ sahassena, sahadānamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
‘‘Mahādānaṃ daditvāna, abhivādiya nāyakaṃ;
```

```
Ekamantaṃ ṭhito haṭṭho, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tayi saddhāya me vīra, adhikāraguṇena ca;
```

```
Parisā mahatī hotu, nibbattassa tahiṃ tahiṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā avoca parisaṃ, gajagajjitasussaro;
```

```
Karavīkaruto satthā, ‘etaṃ passatha brāhmaṇaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hemavaṇṇaṃ mahābāhuṃ, kamalānanalocanaṃ;
```

```
Udaggatanujaṃ haṭṭhaṃ, saddhavantaṃ guṇe mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
‘‘‘Esa <pb ed="V" n="2.0131" /> patthayate ṭhānaṃ <note>patthayi taṃ ṭhānaṃ (syā.)</note>, sīhaghosassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Anāgatamhi addhāne, lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="2.0482" /> dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
‘‘Ito dvenavute kappe, ahu satthā anuttaro;
```

```
Anūpamo asadiso, phusso lokagganāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
‘‘So <pb ed="T" n="2.0208" /> ca sabbaṃ tamaṃ hantvā, vijaṭetvā mahājaṭaṃ;
```

```
Vassate amataṃ vuṭṭhiṃ, tappayanto sadevakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0135" /> hi bārāṇasiyaṃ, rājā paccā ahumhase;
```

```
Bhātaromha tayo sabbe, saṃvisaṭṭhāva rājino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
‘‘Vīraṅgarūpā balino, saṅgāme aparājitā;
```

```
Tadā kupitapaccanto <note>kuppati paccanto (ka.)</note>, amhe āha mahīpati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
‘‘‘Etha gantvāna paccantaṃ, sodhetvā aṭṭavībalaṃ;
```

```
Khemaṃ vijiritaṃ katvā, puna dethāti bhāsatha’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
‘‘Tato mayaṃ avocumha, yadi deyyāsi nāyakaṃ;
```

```
Upaṭṭhānāya amhākaṃ, sādhayissāma vo tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
‘‘Tato mayaṃ laddhavarā, bhūmipālena pesitā;
```

```
Nikkhittasatthaṃ paccantaṃ, katvā punarupacca taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
‘‘Yācitvā satthupaṭṭhānaṃ, rājānaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Munivīraṃ labhitvāna, yāvajīvaṃ yajimha taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
‘‘Mahagghāni ca vatthāni, paṇītāni rasāni ca;
```

```
Senāsanāni rammāni, bhesajjāni hitāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
‘‘Datvā sasaṅghamunino <note>sasaṃghassa mune (sī. pī.)</note>, dhammenuppāditāni no;
```

```
Sīlavanto kāruṇikā, bhāvanāyuttamānasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
‘‘Saddhā paricaritvāna, mettacittena nāyakaṃ;
```

```
Nibbute tamhi lokagge, pūjaṃ katvā yathābalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="2.0209" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0132" /> cutā santusitaṃ <note>tāvatiṃsaṃ (syā.)</note>, gatā tattha mahāsukhaṃ;
```

```
Anubhūtā mayaṃ sabbe, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
‘‘Māyākāro <pb ed="P" n="2.0483" /> yathā raṅge <note>laddho (syā. pī.)</note>, dassesi vikatiṃ bahuṃ;
```

```
Tathā bhave bhamantohaṃ <note>gamentohaṃ (ka.), bhavantohaṃ (syā.)</note>, videhādhipatī ahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
‘‘Guṇāceḷassa vākyena, micchādiṭṭhigatāsayo;
```

```
Narakaṃ maggamārūḷho, rucāya mama dhītuyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādaṃ nādiyitvāna, brahmunā nāradenahaṃ;
```

```
Bahudhā saṃsito santo, diṭṭhiṃ hitvāna pāpikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
‘‘Pūrayitvā <pb ed="M" n="2.0136" /> visesena, dasa kammapathānihaṃ;
```

```
Hitvāna dehamagamiṃ, saggaṃ sabhavanaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, brahmabandhu ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Bārāṇasiyaṃ phītāyaṃ, jāto vippamahākule.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
‘‘Maccubyādhijarā bhīto, ogāhetvā mahāvanaṃ <note>jahitvāna mahādhanaṃ (sī.), jahitvā ca mahādhanaṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Nibbānaṃ padamesanto, jaṭilesu paribbajiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā dve bhātaro mayhaṃ, pabbajiṃsu mayā saha;
```

```
Uruveḷāyaṃ māpetvā, assamaṃ nivasiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
‘‘Kassapo nāma gottena, uruveḷanivāsiko <note>uruveḷāya nivasiṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Tato me āsi paññatti, uruveḷakassapo iti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
‘‘Nadīsakāse bhātā me, nadīkassapasavhayo;
```

```
Āsī sakāsanāmena, gayāyaṃ gayākassapo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
‘‘Dve <pb ed="T" n="2.0210" /> satāni kaniṭṭhassa, tīṇi majjhassa bhātuno;
```

```
Mama pañca satānūnā, sissā sabbe mamānugā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā upecca maṃ buddho, katvāna vividhāni me <note>katvā nānāvidhāni me (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Pāṭihīrāni lokaggo, vinesi narasārathi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassaparivārena, ahosiṃ ehibhikkhuko;
```

```
Teheva saha sabbehi, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
‘‘Te <pb ed="P" n="2.0484" /> cevaññe ca bahavo, sissā maṃ parivārayuṃ;
```

```
Sāsituñca samatthohaṃ, tato maṃ isisattamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāparisabhāvasmiṃ<pb ed="V" n="2.0133" />, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
```

```
Aho buddhe kataṃ kāraṃ, saphalaṃ me ajāyatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0137" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā uruveḷakassapo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Uruveḷakassapattherassāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Rādhattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0211" /> nāma jino, sabbalokavidū muni;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Desanākusalo buddho, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Sampatte titthiye sabbe, pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi, suññataṃ titthiyehi ca;
```

```
Vicittaṃ arahantehi, vasībhūtehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ, uggato so mahāmuni;
```

```
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni, āyu vijjati tāvade;
```

```
Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, brāhmaṇo mantapāragū;
```

```
Upecca taṃ naravaraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
‘‘Paññapentaṃ mahāvīraṃ, parisāsu visāradaṃ;
```

```
Paṭibhāneyyakaṃ bhikkhuṃ, etadagge vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ kāraṃ katvāna, sasaṅghe lokanāyake;
```

```
Nipacca sirasā pāde, taṃ ṭhānaṃ abhipatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="2.0212" /> maṃ bhagavā āha, siṅgīnikkhasamappabho;
```

```
Sarena rajanīyena, kilesamalahārinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sukhī <pb ed="M" n="2.0138" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0134" /> bhavassu dīghāyu, sijjhatu paṇidhī tava;
```

```
Sasaṅghe me kataṃ kāraṃ, atīva vipulaṃ tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="P" n="2.0485" /> kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Rādhoti nāmadheyyena, hessati satthu sāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sa te hetuguṇe tuṭṭho, sakyaputto narāsabho <note>idaṃ pādadvayaṃ syāmamūle natthī</note>;
```

```
Paṭibhāneyyakānaggaṃ, paññapessati nāyako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Mettacitto paricariṃ, sato paññāsamāhito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
‘‘Satānaṃ tīṇikkhattuñca, devarajjamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Satānaṃ pañcakkhattuñca, cakkavattī ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhito āsiṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, giribbajapuruttame;
```

```
Jāto vippakule niddhe, vikalacchādanāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
‘‘Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ pādāsiṃ, sāriputtassa tādino;
```

```
Yadā <pb ed="T" n="2.0213" /> jiṇṇo ca vuddho ca, tadārāmamupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajati na maṃ koci <note>pabbājenti na maṃ keci (sī. syā pī.)</note>, jiṇṇadubbalathāmakaṃ;
```

```
Tena dīno vivaṇṇaṅgo <note>vivaṇṇako (ka.)</note>, soko cāsiṃ tadā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā mahākāruṇiko, mamamāha <note>mamāha so (sī.), mamāha ca (pī.)</note> mahāmuni;
```

```
‘Kimatthaṃ puttasokaṭṭo, brūhi te cittajaṃ rujaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pabbajjaṃ na labhe vīra, svākkhāte tava sāsane;
```

```
Tena sokena dīnosmi, saraṇaṃ hohi nāyaka’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0139" /> bhikkhū samānetvā, apucchi munisattamo;
```

```
‘Imassa adhikāraṃ ye, saranti byāharantu te’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
‘‘Sāriputto <pb ed="V" n="2.0135" /> tadāvoca, ‘kāramassa sarāmahaṃ;
```

```
Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ dāpesi, piṇḍāya carato mama’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sādhu sādhu kataññūsi, sāriputta imaṃ tuvaṃ;
```

```
Pabbājehi dijaṃ vuḍḍhaṃ, hessatājāniyo ayaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="P" n="2.0486" /> alatthaṃ pabbajjaṃ, kammavācopasampadaṃ;
```

```
Na cireneva kālena, pāpuṇiṃ āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
‘‘Sakkaccaṃ munino vākyaṃ, suṇāmi mudito yato;
```

```
Paṭibhāneyyakānaggaṃ, tato maṃ ṭhapayī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0214" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā rādho thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Rādhattherassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Mogharājattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbalokavidū muni;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Desanākusalo buddho, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Sampatte titthiye sabbe, pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi, suññataṃ titthiyehi ca;
```

```
Vicittaṃ arahantehi, vasībhūtehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ<pb ed="M" n="2.0140" />, uggato so mahāmuni;
```

```
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni<pb ed="V" n="2.0136" />, āyu vijjati tāvade;
```

```
Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0215" /> haṃsavatiyaṃ, kule aññatare ahuṃ;
```

```
Parakammāyane yutto, natthi me kiñci saṃdhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭikkamanasālāyaṃ, vasanto katabhūmiyaṃ;
```

```
Aggiṃ ujjālayiṃ tattha, daḷhaṃ kaṇhāsi sā <note>kaṇhā siyā (sī. pī.), ḍayhakaṇhā silā (syā.)</note> hī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā parisatiṃ nātho, catusaccapakāsako;
```

```
Sāvakaṃ sampakittesi, lūkhacīvaradhārakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa tamhi guṇe tuṭṭho, paṇipacca <note>patipajja (syā.)</note> tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Lūkhacīvaradhāraggaṃ, patthayiṃ ṭhānamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā avoca bhagavā, sāvake padumuttaro;
```

```
‘Passathetaṃ purisakaṃ, kucelaṃ tanudehakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pītippasannavadanaṃ<pb ed="P" n="2.0487" />, saddhādhanasamanvitaṃ <note>saddhāsnehasamanvataṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Udaggatanujaṃ haṭṭhaṃ, acalaṃ sālapiṇḍitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
‘‘‘Eso pattheti taṃ ṭhānaṃ, saccasenassa bhikkhuno;
```

```
Lūkhacīvaradhārissa, tassa vaṇṇasitāsayo <note>vaṇṇagatāsayo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā, nipacca sirasā jinaṃ;
```

```
Yāvajīvaṃ subhaṃ kammaṃ, karitvā jinasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsūpago ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭikkamanasālāyaṃ, bhūmidāhakakammunā;
```

```
Samasahassaṃ niraye, adayhiṃ vedanāṭṭito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0216" /> kammāvasesena, pañca jātisatānihaṃ;
```

```
Manusso kulajo hutvā, jātiyā lakkhaṇaṅkito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
‘‘Pañca <pb ed="M" n="2.0141" /> jātisatāneva, kuṭṭharogasamappito;
```

```
Mahādukkhaṃ anubhaviṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃ bhaddake kappe, upariṭṭhaṃ yasassinaṃ;
```

```
Piṇḍapātena tappesiṃ, pasannamānaso ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="2.0137" /> kammavisesena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, ajāyiṃ khattiye kule;
```

```
Pituno accayenāhaṃ, mahārajjasamappito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
‘‘Kuṭṭharogādhibhūtohaṃ, na ratiṃ na sukhaṃ labhe;
```

```
Moghaṃ rajjaṃ sukhaṃ yasmā, mogharājā tato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
‘‘Kāyassa dosaṃ disvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Bāvarissa dijaggassa, sissattaṃ ajjhupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
‘‘Mahatā parivārena, upecca naranāyakaṃ;
```

```
Apucchiṃ nipuṇaṃ pañhaṃ, taṃ vīraṃ vādisūdanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ayaṃ loko paro loko, brahmaloko sadevako;
```

```
Diṭṭhiṃ no <note>diṭṭhā no (sī.), diṭṭhaṃ no (pī.), diṭṭhiṃ te (syā.)</note> nābhijānāmi, gotamassa yasassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
‘‘‘Evābhikkantadassāviṃ<pb ed="P" n="2.0488" />, atthi pañhena āgamaṃ;
```

```
Kathaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ, maccurājā na passati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
‘‘‘Suññato <pb ed="T" n="2.0217" /> lokaṃ avekkhassu, mogharāja sadā sato;
```

```
Attānudiṭṭhiṃ uhacca, evaṃ maccutaro siyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
‘‘‘Evaṃ lokaṃ avekkhantaṃ, maccurājā na passati’;
```

```
Iti maṃ abhaṇi buddho, sabbarogatikicchako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
‘‘Saha gāthāvasānena, kesamassuvivajjito;
```

```
Kāsāvavatthavasano, āsiṃ bhikkhu tathārahā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅghikesu vihāresu, na vasiṃ rogapīḷito;
```

```
Mā vihāro padussīti, vātarogehi pīḷito <note>vācāyābhisupīḷito (syā. pī.), vātarogī supīḷito (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkārakūṭā <pb ed="M" n="2.0142" /> āhitvā, susānā rathikāhi ca;
```

```
Tato saṅghāṭiṃ karitvā, dhārayiṃ lūkhacīvaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
‘‘Mahābhisakko tasmiṃ me, guṇe tuṭṭho vināyako;
```

```
Lūkhacīvaradhārīnaṃ, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
‘‘Puññapāpaparikkhīṇo, sabbarogavivajjito;
```

```
Sikhīva anupādāno, nibbāyissamanāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0138" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0218" /> sudaṃ āyasmā mogharājā thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Mogharājattherassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Kaccāyanavaggo catupaññāsamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kaccāno vakkalī thero, mahākappinasavhayo;
```

```
Dabbo kumāranāmo ca, bāhiyo koṭṭhiko vasī.
```

```
Uruveḷakassapo rādho, mogharājā ca paṇḍito;
```

```
Tīṇi gāthāsatānettha, bāsaṭṭhi ceva piṇḍitā.
```

### 55. Bhaddiyavaggo

#### 1. Lakuṇḍabhaddiyattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0219" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0143" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0139" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0489" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, seṭṭhiputto mahaddhano;
```

```
Jaṅghāvihāraṃ vicaraṃ, saṅghārāmaṃ agacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā so lokapajjoto, dhammaṃ desesi nāyako;
```

```
Mañjussarānaṃ pavaraṃ, sāvakaṃ abhikittayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā, kāraṃ katvā mahesino;
```

```
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā buddho viyākāsi, saṅghamajjhe vināyako;
```

```
‘Anāgatamhi addhāne, lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Bhaddiyo nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute <pb ed="T" n="2.0220" /> ito kappe, phusso uppajji nāyako;
```

```
Durāsado duppasaho, sabbalokuttamo jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Caraṇena ca sampanno, brahā uju patāpavā;
```

```
Hitesī sabbasattānaṃ <note>sabbapāṇīnaṃ (sī.)</note>, bahuṃ mocesi bandhanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Nandārāmavane tassa, ahosiṃ phussakokilo <note>pussakokilo (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Gandhakuṭisamāsanne, ambarukkhe vasāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="V" n="2.0140" /> piṇḍāya gacchantaṃ, dakkhiṇeyyaṃ jinuttamaṃ;
```

```
Disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā, mañjunābhinikūjahaṃ <note>mañjunādena kūjahaṃ (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Rājuyyānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0144" /> tadā gantvā, supakkaṃ kanakattacaṃ;
```

```
Ambapiṇḍaṃ gahetvāna, sambuddhassopanāmayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā me cittamaññāya, mahākāruṇiko jino;
```

```
Upaṭṭhākassa hatthato, pattaṃ paggaṇhi nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Adāsiṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0490" /> haṭṭhacittohaṃ <note>tuṭṭhacittohaṃ (sī.)</note>, ambapiṇḍaṃ mahāmune;
```

```
Patte pakkhippa pakkhehi, pañjaliṃ <note>pakkhehañjaliṃ (sī.)</note> katvāna mañjunā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Sarena rajanīyena, savanīyena vaggunā;
```

```
Vassanto buddhapūjatthaṃ, nīḷaṃ <note>niddaṃ (syā. pī.)</note> gantvā nipajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā muditacittaṃ maṃ, buddhapemagatāsayaṃ;
```

```
Sakuṇagghi upāgantvā, ghātayī duṭṭhamānaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutohaṃ tusite, anubhotvā mahāsukhaṃ;
```

```
Manussayonimāgacchiṃ, tassa kammassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi <pb ed="T" n="2.0221" /> bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Sāsanaṃ jotayitvā so, abhibhuyya kutitthiye;
```

```
Vinayitvāna veneyye, nibbuto so sasāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbute tamhi lokagge, pasannā janatā bahū;
```

```
Pūjanatthāya buddhassa, thūpaṃ kubbanti satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattayojanikaṃ thūpaṃ, sattaratanabhūsitaṃ;
```

```
Karissāma mahesissa’, iccevaṃ mantayanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Kikino kāsirājassa, tadā senāya nāyako;
```

```
Hutvāhaṃ appamāṇassa, pamāṇaṃ cetiye vadiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā te mama vākyena, cetiyaṃ yojanuggataṃ;
```

```
Akaṃsu naravīrassa, nānāratanabhūsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="M" n="2.0145" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0141" /> ca bhave dāni, jāto seṭṭhikule ahaṃ;
```

```
Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare, iddhe phīte mahaddhane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Purappavese sugataṃ, disvā vimhitamānaso;
```

```
Pabbajitvāna na ciraṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Cetiyassa pamāṇaṃ yaṃ, akariṃ tena kammunā;
```

```
Lakuṇḍakasarīrohaṃ, jāto paribhavāraho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Sarena <pb ed="T" n="2.0222" /> madhurenāhaṃ, pūjitvā isisattamaṃ;
```

```
Mañjussarānaṃ bhikkhūnaṃ, aggattamanupāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Phaladānena <pb ed="P" n="2.0491" /> buddhassa, guṇānussaraṇena ca;
```

```
Sāmaññaphalasampanno, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgova bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ āyasmā lakuṇḍabhaddiyo thero imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Lakuṇḍabhaddiyattherassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Kaṅkhārevatattheraapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Sīhahanu brahmagiro, haṃsadundubhinissano <note>haṃsadundubhinissaro (sī.) … nissavano (pī.) … sāvano (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Nāgavikkantagamano, candasūrādikappabho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Mahāmatī <pb ed="M" n="2.0146" /> mahāvīro, mahājhāyī mahābalo <note>mahāgati (syā.), mahāhito (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Mahākāruṇiko nātho, mahātamapanūdano <note>mahātamavidhaṃsano (syā.), mahātamanisūdano (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Sa <pb ed="T" n="2.0223" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0142" /> kadāci tilokaggo, veneyyaṃ vinayaṃ bahuṃ <note>veneyye viniyaṃ bahū (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Dhammaṃ desesi sambuddho, sattāsayavidū muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Jhāyiṃ jhānarataṃ vīraṃ, upasantaṃ anāvilaṃ;
```

```
Vaṇṇayanto parisatiṃ, tosesi <note>toseti (syā. pī. ka.)</note> janataṃ jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, brāhmaṇo vedapāragū;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvāna mudito, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
