‘‘Pūrayitvā <pb ed="M" n="2.0192" /> paramannaṃ, gandhālepaṃ akāsahaṃ;
```

```
Jālena pidahitvāna, vatthayugena <note>pītacoḷena (syā.), mahānelena (pī.)</note> chādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Ārammaṇaṃ mamaṃ etaṃ, sarāmi yāvajīvihaṃ;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Tiṃsānaṃ devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Manasā patthitaṃ mayhaṃ, nibbattati yathicchitaṃ <note>yaticchakaṃ (syā.), yadicchakaṃ (pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Vīsānaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Ocitattāva <note>upacitattā (syā.)</note> hutvāna, saṃsarāmi bhavesvahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbabandhanamuttāhaṃ, apetā me upādikā;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0261" /> nābhijānāmi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ ekapiṇḍapātadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ekapiṇḍapātadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍacāraṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0185" /> carantassa, tissanāmassa satthuno;
```

```
Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ paggayha, buddhaseṭṭhassa dāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā <pb ed="P" n="2.0517" /> sambuddho, tisso lokagganāyako;
```

```
Vīthiyā saṇṭhito satthā, akā me anumodanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0193" /> datvāna, tāvatiṃsaṃ gamissasi;
```

```
Chattiṃsadevarājūnaṃ, mahesittaṃ karissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paññāsaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittaṃ karissasi;
```

```
Manasā patthitaṃ sabbaṃ, paṭilacchasi sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sampattiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0262" /> anubhotvāna, pabbajissasikiñcanā;
```

```
Sabbāsave pariññāya, nibbāyissasināsavā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Idaṃ vatvāna sambuddho, tisso lokagganāyako;
```

```
Nabhaṃ abbhuggamī vīro, haṃsarājāva ambare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Sudinnaṃ me dānavaraṃ <note>sudinnameva me dānaṃ (syā.)</note>, suyiṭṭhā yāgasampadā;
```

```
Kaṭacchubhikkhaṃ datvāna, pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Dvenavute ito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, bhikkhādānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kaṭacchubhikkhādāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Sattuppalamālikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="V" n="2.0186" /> aruṇavatiyā, aruṇo nāma <note>aruṇavā nāma (sī. pī.)</note> ttiyo;
```

```
Tassa rañño ahuṃ bhariyā, vāritaṃ vārayāmahaṃ <note>cārikaṃ cārayāmahaṃ (sī.), na gulaṃ pādayāmahaṃ (syā.), na mālaṃ pādayāmahaṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Sattamālaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0263" /> gahetvāna, uppalā devagandhikā;
```

```
Nisajja pāsādavare, evaṃ cintesi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kiṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0194" /> me imāhi mālāhi, sirasāropitāhi me;
```

```
Varaṃ me buddhaseṭṭhassa, ñāṇamhi abhiropitaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Sambuddhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0518" /> paṭimānentī, dvārāsanne nisīdahaṃ;
```

```
‘Yadā ehiti sambuddho, pūjayissaṃ mahāmuniṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Kakudho vilasantova, migarājāva kesarī;
```

```
Bhikkhusaṅghena sahito, āgacchi vīthiyā jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa raṃsiṃ disvāna, haṭṭhā saṃviggamānasā;
```

```
Dvāraṃ avāpuritvāna <note>apāpuṇitvā (syā.)</note>, buddhaseṭṭhamapūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Satta uppalapupphāni, parikiṇṇāni <note>suvitthiṇṇāni (syā.)</note> ambare;
```

```
Chadiṃ karonto buddhassa, matthake dhārayanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Udaggacittā sumanā, vedajātā katañjalī;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Mahānelassa chādanaṃ, dhārenti mama muddhani;
```

```
Dibbagandhaṃ pavāyāmi, sattuppalassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Kadāci nīyamānāya, ñātisaṅghena me tadā;
```

```
Yāvatā parisā mayhaṃ, mahānelaṃ dharīyati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Sattati devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha issarā hutvā, saṃsarāmi bhavābhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Tesaṭṭhi <pb ed="T" n="2.0264" /> cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Sabbe mamanuvattanti, ādeyyavacanā ahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Uppalasseva me vaṇṇo, gandho ceva pavāyati;
```

```
Dubbaṇṇiyaṃ na jānāmi <note>duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi (syā. pī.)</note>, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhipādesu <pb ed="V" n="2.0187" /> kusalā, bojjhaṅgabhāvanā ratā;
```

```
Abhiññāpāramippattā, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Satipaṭṭhānakusalā, samādhijhānagocarā;
```

```
Sammappadhānamanuyuttā, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Vīriyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0195" /> me dhuradhorayhaṃ, yogakkhemādhivāhanaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse <pb ed="P" n="2.0519" /> ito kappe, yaṃ pupphamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ sattuppalamālikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sattuppalamālikātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Pañcadīpikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="T" n="2.0265" /> haṃsavatiyā, cārikī <note>cāriniṃ (syā.)</note> āsahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Ārāmena ca ārāmaṃ, carāmi kusalatthikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Kāḷapakkhamhi divase, addasaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, bodhimūle nisīdahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Garucittaṃ upaṭṭhetvā, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Somanassaṃ pavedetvā, evaṃ cintesi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yadi buddho amitaguṇo, asamappaṭipuggalo;
```

```
Dassetu pāṭihīraṃ me, bodhi obhāsatu ayaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Saha āvajjite mayhaṃ, bodhi pajjali tāvade;
```

```
Sabbasoṇṇamayā āsi, disā sabbā virocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Sattarattindivaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0188" /> <note>sattarattidivaṃ (pī. ka.)</note> tattha, bodhimūle nisīdahaṃ;
```

```
Sattame divase patte, dīpapūjaṃ akāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Āsanaṃ parivāretvā, pañcadīpāni pajjaluṃ;
```

```
Yāva udeti sūriyo, dīpā me pajjaluṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="M" n="2.0196" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, pañcadīpāti vuccati;
```

```
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ <note>satayojanamubbedhaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ <note>saṭṭhi… (syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṅkhiyāni <pb ed="T" n="2.0266" /> dīpāni, parivāre jalanti me;
```

```
Yāvatā devabhavanaṃ, dīpālokena jotati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Parammukhā <pb ed="P" n="2.0520" /> nisīditvā <note>puratthābhimukhā santi (syā.), puratthābhimukhā thitā (pī.)</note>, yadi icchāmi passituṃ;
```

```
Uddhaṃ adho ca tiriyaṃ, sabbaṃ passāmi cakkhunā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā abhikaṅkhāmi, daṭṭhuṃ sugataduggate <note>sukatadukkate (pī.</note>;
```

```
Tattha āvaraṇaṃ natthi, rukkhesu pabbatesu vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Asīti devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Satānaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Dīpasatasahassāni, parivāre jalanti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, uppajjiṃ mātukucchiyaṃ;
```

```
Mātukucchigatā santī <note>mātukucchigataṃ santiṃ (sī.)</note>, akkhi me na nimīlati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Dīpasatasahassāni, puññakammasamaṅgitā;
```

```
Jalanti sūtikāgehe <note>sūtighare pajjalanti (sabbattha)</note>, pañcadīpānidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, mānasaṃ vinivattayiṃ;
```

```
Ajarāmataṃ sītibhāvaṃ, nibbānaṃ phassayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassāhaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ;
```

```
Upasampādayī buddho, guṇamaññāya gotamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, pāsādesu guhāsu vā;
```

```
Suññāgāre <pb ed="T" n="2.0267" /> vasantiyā <note>ca jhāyante (sī.), ca jhāyantā (pī.), pajjhāyantā (syā.)</note>, pañcadīpā jalanti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbacakkhu <pb ed="M" n="2.0197" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0189" /> visuddhaṃ me, samādhikusalā ahaṃ;
```

```
Abhiññāpāramippattā, pañcadīpānidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbavositavosānā, katakiccā anāsavā;
```

```
Pañcadīpā mahāvīra, pāde vandāmi <note>vandati (sī. ka.)</note> cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dīpamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pañcadīpānidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0521" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ pañcadīpikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pañcadīpikātheriyāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Udakadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare bandhumatiyā, ahosiṃ udahārikā;
```

```
Udahārena jīvāmi, tena posemi dārake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Deyyadhammo ca me natthi, puññakkhette anuttare;
```

```
Koṭṭhakaṃ upasaṅkamma, udakaṃ paṭṭhapesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0268" /> kammena sukatena, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ;
```

```
Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, udahārena nimmitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Accharānaṃ sahassassa, ahañhi pavarā tadā;
```

```
Dasaṭṭhānehi tā sabbā, abhibhomi sadā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Paññāsaṃ devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Vīsaticakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Duve bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, dakadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbatagge <pb ed="M" n="2.0198" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0190" /> dumagge vā, antalikkhe ca bhūmiyaṃ;
```

```
Yadā udakamicchāmi, khippaṃ paṭilabhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘Avuṭṭhikā disā natthi, santattā kuthitāpi <note>santattā kuthitā na ca (sī. pī.), santattā khuppitā hi me (syā.)</note> ca;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, mahāmegho pavassati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Kadāci nīyamānāya, ñātisaṅghena me tadā;
```

```
Yadā icchāmahaṃ vassaṃ, mahāmegho ajāyatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Uṇhaṃ vā pariḷāho vā, sarīre me na vijjati;
```

```
Kāye ca me rajo natthi, dakadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Visuddhamanasā <pb ed="P" n="2.0522" /> ajja, apetamanapāpikā;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, yaṃ dakaṃ adadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0269" /> nābhijānāmi, dakadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ udakadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Udakadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Sumedhāvaggo paṭhamo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Sumedhā mekhalādāyī, maṇḍapaṃ saṅkamaṃ dadā;
```

```
Naḷamālī piṇḍadadā, kaṭacchu uppalappadā.
```

```
Dīpadā dakadā ceva, gāthāyo gaṇitā iha;
```

```
Ekagāthāsatañceva, tiṃsati ca taduttari <note>sattarasaṃ taduttari (syā.), sattādasa taduttariṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

### 2. Ekūposathikavaggo

#### 1. Ekūposathikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="T" n="2.0270" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0199" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0191" /> bandhumatiyā, bandhumā nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Divase puṇṇamāya so, upavasi uposathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ tena samayena, kumbhadāsī ahaṃ tahiṃ;
```

```
Disvā sarājakaṃ senaṃ, evāhaṃ cintayiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘Rājāpi rajjaṃ chaḍḍetvā, upavasi uposathaṃ;
```

```
Saphalaṃ nūna taṃ kammaṃ, janakāyo pamodito’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Yoniso <pb ed="P" n="2.0523" /> paccavekkhitvā, duggaccañca <note>duggatiñca (syā.)</note> daliddataṃ <note>daḷiddataṃ (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Mānasaṃ sampahaṃsitvā, upavasiṃ uposathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ uposathaṃ katvā, sammāsambuddhasāsane;
```

```
Tena kammena sukatena, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, ubbhayojanamuggataṃ <note>uddhaṃ yojanamuggataṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Kūṭāgāravarūpetaṃ, mahāsanasubhūsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Accharā satasahassā, upatiṭṭhanti maṃ sadā;
```

```
Aññe deve atikkamma, atirocāmi sabbadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Catusaṭṭhi devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Tesaṭṭhi cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Suvaṇṇavaṇṇā <pb ed="T" n="2.0271" /> hutvāna, bhavesu saṃsarāmahaṃ;
```

```
Sabbattha pavarā homi, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Hatthiyānaṃ assayānaṃ, rathayānañca sīvikaṃ <note>kevalaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Labhāmi sabbamevetaṃ, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Soṇṇamayaṃ rūpimayaṃ, athopi phalikāmayaṃ;
```

```
Lohitaṅgamayañceva, sabbaṃ paṭilabhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Koseyyakambaliyāni<pb ed="V" n="2.0192" />, khomakappāsikāni ca;
```

```
Mahagghāni ca vatthāni, sabbaṃ paṭilabhāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Annaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0200" /> pānaṃ khādanīyaṃ, vatthasenāsanāni ca;
```

```
Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Varagandhañca mālañca, cuṇṇakañca vilepanaṃ;
```

```
Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgārañca pāsādaṃ, maṇḍapaṃ hammiyaṃ guhaṃ;
```

```
Sabbametaṃ paṭilabhe, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassāhaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Aḍḍhamāse asampatte, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="P" n="2.0524" /> kappe, yaṃ kammamakariṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, uposathassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0272" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ ekūposathikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ekūposathikātheriyāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Saḷalapupphikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre, ahosiṃ kinnarī tadā;
```

```
Addasāhaṃ devadevaṃ, caṅkamantaṃ narāsabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Ocinitvāna saḷalaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassadāsahaṃ;
```

```
Upasiṅghi mahāvīro, saḷalaṃ devagandhikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā <pb ed="V" n="2.0193" /> sambuddho, vipassī lokanāyako;
```

```
Upasiṅghi mahāvīro, pekkhamānāya me tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, vanditvā dvipaduttamaṃ <note>dipaduttamaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Sakaṃ cittaṃ pasādetvā, tato pabbatamāruhiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="M" n="2.0201" /> kappe, yaṃ pupphamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, buddhapūjāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="T" n="2.0273" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ saḷalapupphikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Saḷalapupphikātheriyāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Modakadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare bandhumatiyā, kumbhadāsī ahosahaṃ;
```

```
Mama bhāgaṃ gahetvāna, gacchaṃ udakahārikā <note>udakahārikaṃ (sī.), udakahārike (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Panthamhi samaṇaṃ disvā, santacittaṃ samāhataṃ;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, modake tīṇidāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="P" n="2.0525" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Ekanavutikappāni <note>ekūnatiṃsakappāni (syā.)</note>, vinipātaṃ nagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Sampatti taṃ <note>sampattiñca (syā.), sampattikaṃ (ka.)</note> karitvāna, sabbaṃ anubhaviṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Modake tīṇi datvāna, pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0274" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="2.0194" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ modakadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Modakadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Ekāsanadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="M" n="2.0202" /> haṃsavatiyā, ahosiṃ bālikā <note>mālikā (syā. pī.)</note> tadā;
```

```
Mātā ca me pitā ceva, kammantaṃ agamaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Majjhanhikamhi sūriye, addasaṃ samaṇaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Vīthiyā anugacchantaṃ, āsanaṃ paññapesahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Gonakāvikatikāhi <note>gonakacittakādīhi (sī.)</note>, paññapetvā mamāsanaṃ;
```

```
Pasannacittā sumanā, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘‘Santattā kuthitā bhūmi, sūro majjhanhike ṭhito;
```

```
Mālutā ca na vāyanti, kālo cevettha mehiti <note>cettha upaṭṭhito (sī.), cevatthaṃ eti taṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paññattamāsanamidaṃ, tavatthāya mahāmuni;
```

```
Anukampaṃ upādāya, nisīda mama āsane’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Nisīdi tattha samaṇo, sudanto suddhamānaso;
```

```
Tassa pattaṃ gahetvāna, yathārandhaṃ adāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0275" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, āsanena sunimmitaṃ;
```

```
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Soṇṇamayā <pb ed="P" n="2.0526" /> maṇimayā, athopi phalikāmayā;
```

```
Lohitaṅgamayā ceva, pallaṅkā vividhā mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Tūlikā vikatikāhi, kaṭṭissacittakāhi ca;
```

```
Uddaekantalomī ca, pallaṅkā me susaṇṭhitā <note>susanthatā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="V" n="2.0195" /> icchāmi gamanaṃ, hāsakhiḍḍasamappitā;
```

```
Saha pallaṅkaseṭṭhena, gacchāmi mama patthitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Asīti devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Sattati cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavābhave <pb ed="M" n="2.0203" /> saṃsarantī, mahābhogaṃ labhāmahaṃ;
```

```
Bhoge me ūnatā natthi, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ <note>ekāsanaphalaṃ idaṃ (sabbattha) evamuparipi</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Duve bhave saṃsarāmi, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Aññe bhave na jānāmi, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Duve kule pajāyāmi, khattiye cāpi brāhmaṇe;
```

```
Uccākulīnā <note>uccākulikā (syā. pī. ka.)</note> sabbattha, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Domanassaṃ na jānāmi, cittasantāpanaṃ mama;
```

```
Vevaṇṇiyaṃ na jānāmi, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Dhātiyo <pb ed="T" n="2.0276" /> maṃ upaṭṭhanti, khujjā celāpikā <note>khelāpikā (sī.), celāvikā (pī.)</note> bahū;
```

```
Aṅkena aṅkaṃ gacchāmi, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Aññā nhāpenti bhojenti, aññā ramenti maṃ sadā;
```

```
Aññā gandhaṃ vilimpanti, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ <note>aññā mameva nhāpenti, aññā bhojenti bhojanaṃ; aññā maṃ alaṅkaronti, aññā ramenti maṃ saddhā; (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, suññāgāre vasantiyā;
```

```
Mama saṅkappamaññāya, pallaṅko upatiṭṭhati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Ayaṃ pacchimako mayhaṃ, carimo vattate bhavo;
```

```
Ajjāpi rajjaṃ chaḍḍetvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, ekāsanassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ ekāsanadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Ekāsanadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Pañcadīpadāyikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare <pb ed="T" n="2.0277" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0204" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0196" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0527" /> haṃsavatiyā, cārikī <note>cārikā (sī. syā.)</note> āsahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Ārāmena ca ārāmaṃ <note>ārāmena vihārena (syā. pī.)</note>, carāmi kusalatthikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Kāḷapakkhamhi divase, addasaṃ bodhimuttamaṃ;
```

```
Tattha cittaṃ pasādetvā, bodhimūle nisīdahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Garucittaṃ upaṭṭhetvā, sire katvāna añjaliṃ;
```

```
Somanassaṃ pavedetvā, evaṃ cintesi tāvade.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yadi buddho amitaguṇo, asamappaṭipuggalo;
```

```
Dassetu pāṭihīraṃ me, bodhi obhāsatu ayaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Saha āvajjite mayhaṃ, bodhi pajjali tāvade;
```

```
Sabbasoṇṇamayā āsi, disā sabbā virocati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Sattarattindivaṃ tattha, bodhimūle nisīdahaṃ;
```

```
Sattame divase patte, dīpapūjaṃ akāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Āsanaṃ parivāretvā, pañca dīpāni pajjaluṃ;
```

```
Yāva udeti sūriyo, dīpā me pajjaluṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Tattha me sukataṃ byamhaṃ, pañcadīpāti vuccati;
```

```
Saṭṭhiyojanamubbedhaṃ, tiṃsayojanavitthataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Asaṅkhiyāni <pb ed="T" n="2.0278" /> dīpāni, parivāre jaliṃsu me;
```

```
Yāvatā devabhavanaṃ, dīpālokena jotati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Parammukhā <note>pubbamukhā (syā.)</note> nisīditvā, yadi icchāmi passituṃ;
```

```
Uddhaṃ adho ca tiriyaṃ, sabbaṃ passāmi cakkhunā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Yāvatā abhikaṅkhāmi, daṭṭhuṃ sugataduggate <note>sukatadukkaṭe (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tattha āvaraṇaṃ natthi, rukkhesu pabbatesu vā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Asīti devarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Satānaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0205" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0197" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0528" /> yaṃ yonupapajjāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Dīpasatasahassāni, parivāre jalanti me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Devalokā cavitvāna, uppajjiṃ mātukucchiyaṃ;
```

```
Mātukucchigatā santī, akkhi me na nimīlati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Dīpasatasahassāni, puññakammasamaṅgitā;
```

```
Jalanti sūtikāgehe, pañcadīpānidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, mānasaṃ vinivattayiṃ;
```

```
Ajarāmataṃ sītibhāvaṃ, nibbānaṃ phassayiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Jātiyā sattavassāhaṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ;
```

```
Upasampādayī buddho, guṇamaññāya gotamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇḍape rukkhamūle vā, suññāgāre vasantiyā;
```

```
Sadā pajjalate dīpaṃ, pañcadīpānidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbacakkhu visuddhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0279" /> me, samādhikusalā ahaṃ;
```

```
Abhiññāpāramippattā, pañcadīpānidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbavositavosānā, katakiccā anāsavā;
```

```
Pañcadīpā mahāvīra, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, yaṃ dīpamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, pañcadīpānidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ pañcadīpadāyikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pañcadīpadāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Naḷamālikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Candabhāgānadītīre<pb ed="V" n="2.0198" />, ahosiṃ kinnarī tadā;
```

```
Addasaṃ virajaṃ buddhaṃ, sayambhuṃ aparājitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Pasannacittā <pb ed="M" n="2.0206" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0529" /> sumanā, vedajātā katañjalī;
```

```
Naḷamālaṃ gahetvāna, sayambhuṃ abhipūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0280" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā kinnarīdehaṃ <note>mānasaṃ dehaṃ (sī. pī. ka.) sumedhāvaggepi</note>, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Chattiṃsadevarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Manasā patthitaṃ mayhaṃ, nibbattati yathicchitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Dasannaṃ cakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Ocitattāva <note>sucitattāva (pī.)</note> hutvāna, saṃsarāmi bhavesvahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Kusalaṃ vijjate mayhaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Pūjārahā ahaṃ ajja, sakyaputtassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Visuddhamanasā ajja, apetamanapāpikā;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Catunnavutito kappe, yaṃ buddhamabhipūjayiṃ;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, naḷamālāyidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ naḷamālikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Naḷamālikātheriyāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Mahāpajāpatigotamītherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Ekadā <pb ed="T" n="2.0281" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0199" /> lokapajjoto, vesāliyaṃ mahāvane;
```

```
Kūṭāgāre susālāyaṃ, vasate narasārathi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā jinassa mātucchā, mahāgotami bhikkhunī;
```

```
Tahiṃ kate <note>tahiṃyeva (syā.)</note> pure ramme, vasī bhikkhunupassaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhunīhi <pb ed="M" n="2.0207" /> vimuttāhi, satehi saha pañcahi;
```

```
Rahogatāya tassevaṃ, citassāsi <note>cittassāpi (syā.)</note> vitakkitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa parinibbānaṃ, sāvakaggayugassa vā;
```

```
Rāhulānandanandānaṃ, nāhaṃ lacchāmi passituṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa parinibbānā, sāvakaggayugassa vā;
```

```
Mahākassapanandānaṃ, ānandarāhulāna ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭikaccāyusaṅkhāraṃ <note>paṭigaccāyusaṅkhāre (sī.)</note><pb ed="P" n="2.0530" />, osajjitvāna nibbutiṃ;
```

```
Gaccheyyaṃ lokanāthena, anuññātā mahesinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Tathā pañcasatānampi, bhikkhunīnaṃ vitakkitaṃ;
```

```
Āsi khemādikānampi, etadeva vitakkitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Bhūmicālo tadā āsi, nāditā devadundubhī;
```

```
Upassayādhivatthāyo, devatā sokapīḷitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Vilapantā sukaruṇaṃ <note>sakaruṇaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, tatthassūni pavattayuṃ;
```

```
Mittā <note>sabbā (syā. pī.)</note> bhikkhuniyo tāhi, upagantvāna gotamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Nipacca sirasā pāde, idaṃ vacanamabravuṃ;
```

```
‘Tattha toyalavāsittā, mayamayye rahogatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sā <pb ed="T" n="2.0282" /> calā calitā bhūmi, nāditā devadundubhī;
```

```
Paridevā ca suyyante, kimatthaṃ nūna gotamī’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā avoca sā sabbaṃ, yathāparivitakkitaṃ;
```

```
Tāyopi sabbā āhaṃsu, yathāparivitakkitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yadi te rucitaṃ ayye, nibbānaṃ paramaṃ sivaṃ;
```

```
Nibbāyissāma sabbāpi, buddhānuññāya subbate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mayaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0200" /> sahāva nikkhantā, gharāpi ca bhavāpi ca;
```

```
Sahāyeva gamissāma, nibbānaṃ padamuttamaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nibbānāya vajantīnaṃ, kiṃ vakkhāmī’ti sā vadaṃ;
```

```
Saha sabbāhi niggañchi, bhikkhunīnilayā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Upassaye <pb ed="M" n="2.0208" /> yādhivatthā, devatā tā khamantu me;
```

```
Bhikkhunīnilayassedaṃ, pacchimaṃ dassanaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Na jarā maccu vā yattha, appiyehi samāgamo;
```

```
Piyehi na viyogotthi, taṃ vajissaṃ <note>taṃ vajjiyaṃ (syā.)</note> asaṅkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Avītarāgā taṃ sutvā, vacanaṃ sugatorasā;
```

```
Sokaṭṭā parideviṃsu, aho no appapuññatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhunīnilayo <pb ed="P" n="2.0531" /> suñño, bhūto tāhi vinā ayaṃ;
```

```
Pabhāte viya tārāyo, na dissanti jinorasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbānaṃ gotamī yāti, satehi saha pañcahi;
```

```
Nadīsatehiva saha, gaṅgā pañcahi sāgaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Rathiyāya <pb ed="T" n="2.0283" /> vajantiyo <note>vajantiṃ taṃ (sī.), vajanti taṃ (syā.), vajantānaṃ (pī.)</note>, disvā saddhā upāsikā;
```

```
Gharā nikkhamma pādesu, nipacca idamabravuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pasīdassu mahābhoge, anāthāyo vihāya no;
```

```
Tayā na yuttā <note>yuttaṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nibbātuṃ, icchaṭṭā vilapiṃsu tā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Tāsaṃ sokapahānatthaṃ, avoca madhuraṃ giraṃ;
```

```
‘Ruditena alaṃ puttā, hāsakāloyamajja vo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pariññātaṃ mayā dukkhaṃ, dukkhahetu vivajjito;
```

```
Nirodho me sacchikato, maggo cāpi subhāvito.
```

Paṭhamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddho <pb ed="V" n="2.0201" /> tassa ca saddhammo, anūno yāva tiṭṭhati;
```

```
Nibbātuṃ tāva kālo me, mā maṃ socatha puttikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘‘Koṇḍaññānandanandādī<pb ed="M" n="2.0209" />, tiṭṭhanti rāhulo jino;
```

```
Sukhito sahito saṅgho, hatadabbā ca titthiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘‘Okkākavaṃsassa yaso, ussito māramaddano;
```

```
Nanu sampati kālo me, nibbānatthāya puttikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cirappabhuti <pb ed="T" n="2.0284" /> yaṃ mayhaṃ, patthitaṃ ajja sijjhate;
```

```
Ānandabherikāloyaṃ, kiṃ vo assūhi puttikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sace mayi dayā atthi, yadi catthi kataññutā;
```

```
Saddhammaṭṭhitiyā sabbā, karotha vīriyaṃ daḷhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘‘Thīnaṃ adāsi pabbajjaṃ, sambuddho yācito mayā;
```

```
Tasmā yathāhaṃ nandissaṃ, tathā tamanutiṭṭhatha’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Tā evamanusāsitvā, bhikkhunīhi purakkhatā;
```

```
Upecca buddhaṃ vanditvā, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ahaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0532" /> sugata te mātā, tvañca vīra pitā mama;
```

```
Saddhammasukhada <note>saddhammasukhado (sī. syā. pī.)</note> nātha, tayā jātāmhi gotama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṃvaddhitoyaṃ sugata, rūpakāyo mayā tava;
```

```
Anindito <note>ānandiyo (syā.), anindiyo (pī.)</note> dhammakāyo <note>dhammatanu (sī. pī. ka.)</note>, mama saṃvaddhito tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘‘Muhuttaṃ taṇhāsamaṇaṃ, khīraṃ tvaṃ pāyito mayā;
```

```
Tayāhaṃ santamaccantaṃ, dhammakhīrañhi <note>dhammakhīrampi (syā., ka.)</note> pāyitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bandhanārakkhane mayhaṃ, aṇaṇo <note>anaṇo (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tvaṃ mahāmune;
```

```
Puttakāmā thiyo yācaṃ, labhanti tādisaṃ sutaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mandhātādinarindānaṃ, yā mātā sā bhavaṇṇave;
```

```
Nimuggāhaṃ tayā putta, tāritā bhavasāgarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rañño mātā mahesīti, sulabhaṃ nāmamitthinaṃ;
```

```
Buddhamātāti yaṃ nāmaṃ, etaṃ paramadullabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tañca <pb ed="T" n="2.0285" /> laddhaṃ mahāvīra, paṇidhānaṃ mamaṃ tayā;
```

```
Aṇukaṃ vā mahantaṃ vā, taṃ sabbaṃ pūritaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘‘Parinibbātumicchāmi<pb ed="M" n="2.0210" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0202" />, vihāyemaṃ kaḷevaraṃ;
```

```
Anujānāhi me vīra, dukkhantakara nāyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cakkaṅkusadhajākiṇṇe, pāde kamalakomale;
```

```
Pasārehi paṇāmaṃ te, karissaṃ puttauttame <note>puttapemasā (sī. pī.), puttapemahaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘‘Suvaṇṇarāsisaṅkāsaṃ, sarīraṃ kuru pākaṭaṃ;
```

```
Katvā dehaṃ sudiṭṭhaṃ te, santiṃ gacchāmi nāyaka’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Dvattiṃsalakkhaṇūpetaṃ, suppabhālaṅkataṃ tanuṃ;
```

```
Sañjhāghanāva bālakkaṃ, mātucchaṃ dassayī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Phullāravindasaṃkāse, taruṇādiccasappabhe;
```

```
Cakkaṅkite pādatale, tato sā sirasā pati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṇamāmi narādicca, ādiccakulaketukaṃ;
```

```
Pacchime maraṇe mayhaṃ <note>saraṇaṃ mayhaṃ (syā.)</note>, na taṃ ikkhāmahaṃ puno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘‘Itthiyo <pb ed="P" n="2.0533" /> nāma lokagga, sabbadosākarā matā;
```

```
Yadi ko catthi doso me, khamassu karuṇākara.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘‘Itthikānañca pabbajjaṃ, haṃ taṃ yāciṃ punappunaṃ;
```

```
Tattha ce atthi doso me, taṃ khamassu narāsabha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mayā bhikkhuniyo vīra, tavānuññāya sāsitā;
```

```
Tatra ce atthi dunnītaṃ, taṃ khamassu khamādhipa <note>khamādhiti (syā.), khamāpito (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘‘Akkhante <pb ed="T" n="2.0286" /> nāma khantabbaṃ, kiṃ bhave guṇabhūsane;
```

```
Kimuttaraṃ te vakkhāmi, nibbānāya vajantiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘‘Suddhe anūne mama bhikkhusaṅghe, lokā ito nissarituṃ khamante;
```

```
Pabhātakāle byasanaṅgatānaṃ, disvāna niyyātiva candalekhā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tadetarā bhikkhuniyo jinaggaṃ, tārāva candānugatā sumeruṃ;
```

```
Padakkhiṇaṃ kacca nipacca pāde, ṭhitā mukhantaṃ samudikkhamānā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na <pb ed="M" n="2.0211" /> tittipubbaṃ tava dassanena, cakkhuṃ na sotaṃ tava bhāsitena;
```

```
Cittaṃ mamaṃ kevalamekameva, pappuyya taṃ dhammarasena titti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nadato parisāyaṃ te, vāditabbapahārino;
```

```
Ye te dakkhanti vadanaṃ, dhaññā te narapuṅgava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dīghaṅgulī <pb ed="V" n="2.0203" /> tambanakhe, subhe āyatapaṇhike;
```

```
Ye pāde paṇamissanti <note>paṇamāyanti (syā.)</note>, tepi dhaññā guṇandhara.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘‘Madhurāni <pb ed="P" n="2.0534" /> pahaṭṭhāni, dosagghāni hitāni ca;
```

```
Ye te vākyāni suyyanti, tepi dhaññā naruttama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhaññāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0287" /> te mahāvīra, pādapūjanatapparā <note>mānapūjanatapparā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tiṇṇasaṃsārakantārā, suvākyena sirīmato’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘Tato sā anusāvetvā <note>anumāne tvā (ka.)</note>, bhikkhusaṅghampi subbatā;
```

```
Rāhulānandanande ca, vanditvā idamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āsīvisālayasame, rogāvāse kaḷevare;
```

```
Nibbindā dukkhasaṅghāṭe, jarāmaraṇagocare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nānākalimalākiṇṇe <note>nānākuṇapamalākiṇṇe (syā.), nānākāḷamalākiṇṇe (ka.)</note>, parāyatte nirīhake;
```

```
Tena nibbātumicchāmi, anumaññatha puttakā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘Nando rāhulabhaddo ca, vītasokā nirāsavā;
```

```
Ṭhitācalaṭṭhiti thirā, dhammatamanucintayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhiratthu saṅkhataṃ lolaṃ, asāraṃ kadalūpamaṃ;
```

```
Māyāmarīcisadisaṃ, itaraṃ anavaṭṭhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yattha nāma jinassāyaṃ, mātucchā buddhaposikā;
```

```
Gotamī nidhanaṃ yāti, aniccaṃ sabbasaṅkhataṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘Ānando ca tadā sekho, sokaṭṭo <note>kaniṭṭho (syā.)</note> jinavacchalo;
```

```
Tatthassūni karonto so, karuṇaṃ paridevati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Hā santiṃ <note>bhāsantī (syā.)</note> gotamī yāti, nūna buddhopi nibbutiṃ;
```

```
Gacchati na cireneva, aggiriva nirindhano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0212" /> vilāpamānaṃ taṃ, ānandaṃ āha gotamī;
```

```
Sutasāgaragambhīra<pb ed="T" n="2.0288" />, buddhopaṭṭhānatappara.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na yuttaṃ socituṃ putta, hāsakāle upaṭṭhite;
```

```
Tayā me saraṇaṃ putta, nibbānaṃ tamupāgataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tayā tāta samajjhiṭṭho, pabbajjaṃ anujāni no;
```

```
Mā putta vimano hohi, saphalo te parissamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0204" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0535" /> na diṭṭhaṃ purāṇehi, titthikācariyehipi;
```

```
Taṃ padaṃ sukumārīhi, sattavassāhi veditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddhasāsanapāleta, pacchimaṃ dassanaṃ tava;
```

```
Tattha gacchāmahaṃ putta, gato yattha na dissate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kadāci dhammaṃ desento, khipī lokagganāyako;
```

```
Tadāhaṃ āsīsavācaṃ, avocaṃ anukampikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ciraṃ jīva mahāvīra, kappaṃ tiṭṭha mahāmune;
```

```
Sabbalokassa atthāya, bhavassu ajarāmaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘‘Taṃ tathāvādiniṃ buddho, mamaṃ so etadabravi;
```

```
‘Na hevaṃ vandiyā buddhā, yathā vandasi gotamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kathaṃ carahi sabbaññū, vanditabbā tathāgatā;
```

```
Kathaṃ avandiyā buddhā, taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āraddhavīriye pahitatte, niccaṃ daḷhaparakkame;
```

```
Samagge sāvake passa, etaṃ buddhānavandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tato upassayaṃ gantvā, ekikāhaṃ vicintayiṃ;
```

```
Samaggaparisaṃ nātho, rodhesi tibhavantago.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘‘Handāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0289" /> parinibbissaṃ, mā vipattitamaddasaṃ;
```

```
Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, disvāna isisattamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘‘Parinibbānakālaṃ me, ārocesiṃ <note>ārocemi (syā.)</note> vināyakaṃ;
```

```
Tato so samanuññāsi, kālaṃ jānāhi gotamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0213" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘‘Thīnaṃ dhammābhisamaye, ye bālā vimatiṃ gatā;
```

```
Tesaṃ diṭṭhippahānatthaṃ, iddhiṃ dassehi gotamī’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā nipacca sambuddhaṃ, uppatitvāna ambaraṃ;
```

```
Iddhī anekā dassesi, buddhānuññāya gotamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Ekikā bahudhā āsi, bahukā cetikā tathā;
```

```
Āvibhāvaṃ tirobhāvaṃ, tirokuṭṭaṃ <note>tirokuḍḍaṃ (syā.)</note> tironagaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Asajjamānā <pb ed="V" n="2.0205" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0536" /> agamā, bhūmiyampi nimujjatha;
```

```
Abhijjamāne udake, agañchi mahiyā yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Sakuṇīva tathākāse, pallaṅkena kamī tadā;
```

```
Vasaṃ vattesi kāyena, yāva brahmanivesanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Sineruṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0290" /> daṇḍaṃ katvāna, chattaṃ katvā mahāmahiṃ;
```

```
Samūlaṃ parivattetvā, dhārayaṃ caṅkamī nabhe.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Chassūrodayakāleva, lokañcākāsi dhūmikaṃ;
```

```
Yugante viya lokaṃ sā, jālāmālākulaṃ akā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Mucalindaṃ mahāselaṃ, merumūlanadantare <note>merumandāradaddare (sī. pī.), meruṃ mandāradantare (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Sāsapāriva sabbāni, ekenaggahi muṭṭhinā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Aṅgulaggena chādesi, bhākaraṃ sanisākaraṃ;
```

```
Candasūrasahassāni, āveḷamiva dhārayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Catusāgaratoyāni, dhārayī ekapāṇinā;
```

```
Yugantajaladākāraṃ, mahāvassaṃ pavassatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkavattiṃ saparisaṃ, māpayī sā nabhattale;
```

```
Garuḷaṃ dviradaṃ sīhaṃ, vinadantaṃ padassayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘Ekikā abhinimmitvā, appameyyaṃ bhikkhunīgaṇaṃ;
```

```
Puna antaradhāpetvā, ekikā munimabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mātucchā <pb ed="M" n="2.0214" /> te mahāvīra, tava sāsanakārikā;
```

```
Anuppattā sakaṃ atthaṃ, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
‘‘Dassetvā vividhā iddhī, orohitvā nabhattalā;
```

```
Vanditvā lokapajjotaṃ, ekamantaṃ nisīdi sā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘Sā vīsavassasatikā, jātiyāhaṃ mahāmune;
```

```
Alamettāvatā vīra, nibbāyissāmi nāyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘Tadātivimhitā <pb ed="T" n="2.0291" /> sabbā, parisā sā katañjalī;
```

```
Avocayye kathaṃ āsi, atuliddhiparakkamā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="P" n="2.0537" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0206" /> haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātāmaccakule ahuṃ;
```

```
Sabbopakārasampanne, iddhe phīte mahaddhane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
‘‘Kadāci pitunā saddhiṃ, dāsigaṇapurakkhatā;
```

```
Mahatā parivārena, taṃ upecca narāsabhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
‘‘Vāsavaṃ viya vassantaṃ, dhammameghaṃ anāsavaṃ <note>pavassayaṃ (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Saradādiccasadisaṃ, raṃsijālasamujjalaṃ <note>raṃsimālākulaṃ jinaṃ (sī. syā.), raṃsijālākulaṃ jinaṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā cittaṃ pasādetvā, sutvā cassa subhāsitaṃ;
```

```
Mātucchaṃ bhikkhuniṃ agge, ṭhapentaṃ naranāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā datvā mahādānaṃ, sattāhaṃ tassa tādino;
```

```
Sasaṅghassa naraggassa, paccayāni bahūni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘‘Nipacca pādamūlamhi, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ;
```

```
Tato mahāparisatiṃ, avoca isisattamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yā sasaṅghaṃ abhojesi, sattāhaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Tamahaṃ kittayissāmi, suṇātha mama bhāsato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="T" n="2.0292" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0215" /> dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Gotamī nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa buddhassa mātucchā, jīvitāpādikā <note>jīvitapālikā (syā.)</note> ayaṃ;
```

```
Rattaññūnañca aggattaṃ, bhikkhunīnaṃ labhissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvāna pamoditvā <note>taṃ sutvāhaṃ pamuditā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Paccayehi upaṭṭhitvā, tato kālaṅkatā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘Tāvatiṃsesu devesu, sabbakāmasamiddhisu;
```

```
Nibbattā dasahaṅgehi, aññe abhibhaviṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpasaddehi gandhehi, rasehi phusanehi ca;
```

```
Āyunāpi ca vaṇṇena, sukhena yasasāpi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘Tathevādhipateyyena, adhigayha virocahaṃ;
```

```
Ahosiṃ amarindassa, mahesī dayitā tahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘Saṃsāre <pb ed="V" n="2.0207" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0538" /> saṃsarantīhaṃ, kammavāyusameritā;
```

```
Kāsissa rañño visaye, ajāyiṃ dāsagāmake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcadāsasatānūnā, nivasanti tahiṃ tadā;
```

```
Sabbesaṃ tattha yo jeṭṭho, tassa jāyā ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘Sayambhuno pañcasatā, gāmaṃ piṇḍāya pāvisuṃ;
```

```
Te disvāna ahaṃ tuṭṭhā, saha sabbāhi itthibhi <note>ñātibhi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘Pūgā hutvāva sabbāyo <note>katvā pañcasatakuṭī (sī. syā.)</note>, catumāse upaṭṭhahuṃ <note>upaṭṭhiya (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ticīvarāni datvāna, saṃsarimha <note>pasannāmha (syā.)</note> sasāmikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="2.0293" /> cutā sabbāpi tā, tāvatiṃsagatā mayaṃ;
```

```
Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātā devadahe pure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘Pitā añjanasakko me, mātā mama sulakkhaṇā;
```

```
Tato kapilavatthusmiṃ, suddhodanagharaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘Sesā <note>sabbā (syā.)</note> sakyakule jātā, sakyānaṃ gharamāgamuṃ;
```

```
Ahaṃ visiṭṭhā sabbāsaṃ, jinassāpādikā ahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘Mama <pb ed="M" n="2.0216" /> puttobhinikkhamma <note>sa me putto… (syā.)</note>, buddho āsi vināyako;
```

```
Pacchāhaṃ pabbajitvāna, satehi saha pañcahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘Sākiyānīhi dhīrāhi, saha santisukhaṃ phusiṃ;
```

```
Ye tadā pubbajātiyaṃ, amhākaṃ āsu sāmino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
‘‘Sahapuññassa kattāro, mahāsamayakārakā;
```

```
Phusiṃsu arahattaṃ te, sugatenānukampitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘Tadetarā bhikkhuniyo, āruhiṃsu nabhattalaṃ;
```

```
Saṃgatā <note>khagatā (sī.)</note> viya tārāyo, virociṃsu mahiddhikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhī anekā dassesuṃ, piḷandhavikatiṃ yathā;
```

```
Kammāro kanakasseva, kammaññassa susikkhito <note>puṇṇakammesu sikkhitā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
‘‘Dassetvā pāṭihīrāni, vicittāni <note>vividhāni (syā.)</note> bahūni ca;
```

```
Tosetvā vādipavaraṃ, muniṃ saparisaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
‘‘Orohitvāna gaganā, vanditvā isisattamaṃ;
```

```
Anuññātā naraggena, yathāṭhāne nisīdisuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ahonukampikā <pb ed="V" n="2.0208" /> amhaṃ, sabbāsaṃ cira gotamī;
```

```
Vāsitā tava puññehi, pattā no āsavakkhayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0539" /> jhāpitā amhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāma anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
‘‘‘Svāgataṃ vata no āsi, buddhaseṭṭhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homa, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homa mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāma, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atthe <pb ed="M" n="2.0217" /> dhamme ca nerutte, paṭibhāne <note>paṭibhāṇe (sī. syā.)</note> ca vijjati;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ amhaṃ mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘‘Asmābhi pariciṇṇosi, mettacittāhi nāyaka;
```

```
Anujānāhi sabbāsaṃ <note>sabbāyo (syā. pī.)</note>, nibbānāya mahāmune’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbāyissāma iccevaṃ, kiṃ vakkhāmi vadantiyo;
```

```
Yassa dāni ca vo kālaṃ, maññathāti jinobravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
‘‘Gotamīādikā tāyo, tadā bhikkhuniyo jinaṃ;
```

```
Vanditvā āsanā tamhā, vuṭṭhāya agamiṃsu tā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘Mahatā <pb ed="T" n="2.0295" /> janakāyena, saha lokagganāyako;
```

```
Anusaṃyāyī so <note>anusaṃsāvayī (syā. ka.)</note> vīro, mātucchaṃ yāvakoṭṭhakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā nipati pādesu, gotamī lokabandhuno;
```

```
Saheva tāhi sabbāhi, pacchimaṃ pādavandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
‘‘‘Idaṃ pacchimakaṃ mayhaṃ, lokanāthassa dassanaṃ;
```

```
Na puno amatākāraṃ, passissāmi mukhaṃ tava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na ca me vandanaṃ <note>vadanaṃ (ka.)</note> vīra, tava pāde sukomale;
```

```
Samphusissati lokagga, ajja gacchāmi nibbutiṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpena <pb ed="V" n="2.0209" /> kiṃ tavānena, diṭṭhe dhamme yathātathe;
```

```
Sabbaṃ saṅkhatamevetaṃ, anassāsikamittaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
‘‘Sā saha tāhi gantvāna, bhikkhunupassayaṃ sakaṃ;
```

```
Aḍḍhapallaṅkamābhujja, nisīdi paramāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā upāsikā tattha, buddhasāsanavacchalā;
```

```
Tassā pavattiṃ sutvāna, upesuṃ pādavandikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
‘‘Karehi uraṃ pahantā, chinnamūlā yathā latā;
```

```
Rodantā karuṇaṃ ravaṃ, sokaṭṭā bhūmipātitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
‘‘Mā <pb ed="P" n="2.0540" /> no saraṇade nāthe, vihāya gami nibbutiṃ;
```

```
Nipatitvāna yācāma, sabbāyo sirasā mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
‘‘Yā <pb ed="M" n="2.0218" /> padhānatamā tāsaṃ, saddhā paññā upāsikā;
```

```
Tassā sīsaṃ pamajjantī, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
‘‘‘Alaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0296" /> puttā visādena, mārapāsānuvattinā;
```

```
Aniccaṃ saṅkhataṃ sabbaṃ, viyogantaṃ calācalaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
‘‘Tato sā tā visajjitvā, paṭhamaṃ jhānamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Dutiyañca tatiyañca, samāpajji catutthakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
‘‘Ākāsāyatanañceva, viññāṇāyatanaṃ tathā;
```

```
Ākiñcaṃ nevasaññañca, samāpajji yathākkamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭilomena jhānāni, samāpajjittha gotamī;
```

```
Yāvatā paṭhamaṃ jhānaṃ, tato yāvacatutthakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
‘‘Tato vuṭṭhāya nibbāyi, dīpaccīva nirāsavā <note>nirāsanā (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Bhūmicālo mahā āsi, nabhasā vijjutā pati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
‘‘Panāditā dundubhiyo, parideviṃsu devatā;
```

```
Pupphavuṭṭhī ca gaganā, abhivassatha medaniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
‘‘Kampito merurājāpi, raṅgamajjhe yathā naṭo;
```

```
Sokena cātidīnova viravo āsi sāgaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
‘‘Devā nāgāsurā brahmā, saṃviggāhiṃsu taṅkhaṇe;
```

```
‘Aniccā vata saṅkhārā, yathāyaṃ vilayaṃ gatā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
‘‘Yā <pb ed="V" n="2.0210" /> ce maṃ parivāriṃsu, satthu sāsanakārikā;
```

```
Tāyopi anupādānā, dīpacci viya <note>dīpasikhā viya (syā.)</note> nibbutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
‘‘Hā yogā vippayogantā, hāniccaṃ sabbasaṅkhataṃ;
```

```
Hā jīvitaṃ vināsantaṃ, iccāsi paridevanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="2.0297" /> devā ca brahmā ca, lokadhammānuvattanaṃ;
```

```
Kālānurūpaṃ kubbanti, upetvā isisattamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="P" n="2.0541" /> āmantayī satthā, ānandaṃ sutasāgaraṃ <note>sutisāgaraṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
‘Gacchānanda nivedehi, bhikkhūnaṃ mātu nibbutiṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
‘‘Tadānando <pb ed="M" n="2.0219" /> nirānando, assunā puṇṇalocano;
```

```
Gaggarena sarenāha, ‘samāgacchantu bhikkhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pubbadakkhiṇapacchāsu, uttarāya ca santike;
```

```
Suṇantu bhāsitaṃ mayhaṃ, bhikkhavo sugatorasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yā vaḍḍhayi payattena, sarīraṃ pacchimaṃ mune;
```

```
Sā gotamī gatā santiṃ, tārāva sūriyodaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
‘‘‘Buddhamātāti paññattiṃ <note>saññattiṃ (syā.)</note>, ṭhapayitvā gatāsamaṃ;
```

```
Na yattha pañcanettopi, gatiṃ <note>gataṃ (sī. pī.), tattha (syā.)</note> dakkhati nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yassatthi sugate saddhā, yo ca piyo mahāmune;
```

```
Buddhamātussa <note>buddhamātari (sī.), buddhassa mātu (syā.)</note> sakkāraṃ, karotu sugatoraso’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
‘‘Sudūraṭṭhāpi taṃ sutvā, sīghamāgacchu bhikkhavo;
```

```
Keci buddhānubhāvena, keci iddhīsu kovidā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgāravare ramme, sabbasoṇṇamaye subhe;
```

```
Mañcakaṃ samāropesuṃ, yattha suttāsi gotamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
‘‘Cattāro lokapālā te, aṃsehi samadhārayuṃ;
```

```
Sesā sakkādikā devā, kūṭāgāre samaggahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
‘‘Kūṭāgārāni <pb ed="T" n="2.0298" /> sabbāni, āsuṃ pañcasatānipi;
```

```
Saradādiccavaṇṇāni, vissakammakatāni hi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbā tāpi bhikkhuniyo, āsuṃ mañcesu sāyitā;
```

```
Devānaṃ khandhamāruḷhā, niyyanti anupubbaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbaso <pb ed="V" n="2.0211" /> chāditaṃ āsi, vitānena nabhattalaṃ;
```

```
Satārā candasūrā ca, lañchitā kanakāmayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭākā <pb ed="P" n="2.0542" /> ussitānekā, vitatā pupphakañcukā;
```

```
Ogatākāsapadumā <note>ogatākāsadhūmāva (pī.)</note>, mahiyā pupphamuggataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
‘‘Dassanti candasūriyā, pajjalanti ca tārakā;
```

```
Majjhaṃ gatopi cādicco, na tāpesi sasī yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
‘‘Devā <pb ed="M" n="2.0220" /> dibbehi gandhehi, mālehi surabhīhi ca;
```

```
Vāditehi ca naccehi, saṅgītīhi ca pūjayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
‘‘Nāgāsurā ca brahmāno, yathāsatti yathābalaṃ;
```

```
Pūjayiṃsu ca niyyantiṃ, nibbutaṃ buddhamātaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbāyo purato nītā, nibbutā sugatorasā;
```

```
Gotamī niyyate pacchā, sakkatā buddhaposikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
‘‘Purato devamanujā, sanāgāsurabrahmakā;
```

```
Pacchā sasāvako buddho, pūjatthaṃ yāti mātuyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa parinibbānaṃ, nedisaṃ āsi yādisaṃ;
```

```
Gotamīparinibbānaṃ, atevacchariyaṃ <note>atīvacchariyaṃ (sabbattha) mogallānabyākaraṇaṃ oloketabbaṃ</note> ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
‘‘Buddho <pb ed="T" n="2.0299" /> buddhassa nibbāne <note>na buddho buddhanibbāne (syā. pī.)</note>, nopaṭiyādi <note>nopadissati (sī. pī.), sāriputtādi (syā.)</note> bhikkhavo;
```

```
Buddho gotaminibbāne, sāriputtādikā tathā <note>yathā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
‘‘Citakāni karitvāna, sabbagandhamayāni te;
```

```
Gandhacuṇṇapakiṇṇāni, jhāpayiṃsu ca tā tahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
‘‘Sesabhāgāni ḍayhiṃsu, aṭṭhī sesāni sabbaso;
```

```
Ānando ca tadāvoca, saṃvegajanakaṃ vaco.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
‘‘‘Gotamī nidhanaṃ yātā, ḍayhañcassā sarīrakaṃ;
```

```
Saṅketaṃ buddhanibbānaṃ, na cirena bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
‘‘Tato gotamidhātūni, tassā pattagatāni so;
```

```
Upanāmesi nāthassa, ānando buddhacodito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
‘‘Pāṇinā tāni paggayha, avoca isisattamo;
```

```
‘Mahato sāravantassa, yathā rukkhassa tiṭṭhato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo <pb ed="V" n="2.0212" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0543" /> so mahattaro khandho, palujjeyya aniccatā;
```

```
Tathā bhikkhunisaṅghassa, gotamī parinibbutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aho acchariyaṃ mayhaṃ <note>ānanda passa buddhassa (syā.)</note>, nibbutāyapi mātuyā;
```

```
Sarīramattasesāya, natthi sokapariddavo <note>na sokaparidevanā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na <pb ed="M" n="2.0221" /> sociyā paresaṃ sā, tiṇṇasaṃsārasāgarā;
```

```
Parivajjitasantāpā, sītibhūtā sunibbutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṇḍitāsi mahāpaññā, puthupaññā tatheva ca;
```

```
Rattaññū bhikkhunīnaṃ sā, evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="T" n="2.0300" /> ca vasī āsi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī āsi ca gotamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pubbenivāsamaññāsi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi tassā punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Parisuddhaṃ ahu ñāṇaṃ, tasmā socaniyā na sā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ayoghanahatasseva, jalato jātavedassa;
```

```
Anupubbūpasantassa, yathā na ñāyate gati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
‘‘‘Evaṃ sammā vimuttānaṃ, kāmabandhoghatārinaṃ;
```

```
Paññāpetuṃ gati natthi, pattānaṃ acalaṃ sukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
‘‘‘Attadīpā tato hotha, satipaṭṭhānagocarā;
```

```
Bhāvetvā sattabojjhaṅge, dukkhassantaṃ karissatha’’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ mahāpajāpatigotamī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Mahāpajāpatigotamītheriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Khemātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0301" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0213" /> haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ <note>ahu (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Nānāratanapajjote, mahāsukhasamappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
‘‘Upetvā <pb ed="P" n="2.0544" /> taṃ mahāvīraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
```

```
Tato jātappasādāhaṃ, upemi saraṇaṃ jinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
‘‘Mātaraṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0222" /> pitaraṃ cāhaṃ, āyācitvā vināyakaṃ;
```

```
Nimantayitvā sattāhaṃ, bhojayiṃ sahasāvakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
‘‘Atikkante ca sattāhe, mahāpaññānamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Bhikkhuniṃ etadaggamhi, ṭhapesi narasārathi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, puno tassa mahesino;
```

```
Kāraṃ katvāna taṃ ṭhānaṃ, paṇipacca paṇīdahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
‘‘Tato mama jino <note>maṃ sa jino (syā.)</note> āha, ‘sijjhataṃ paṇidhī tava;
```

```
Sasaṅghe me kataṃ kāraṃ, appameyyaphalaṃ tayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Etadaggamanuppattā, khemā nāma bhavissati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsūpagā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutā yāmamagaṃ, tatohaṃ tusitaṃ gatā;
```

```
Tato ca nimmānaratiṃ, vasavattipuraṃ tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha <pb ed="T" n="2.0302" /> yatthūpapajjāmi, tassa kammassa vāhasā;
```

```
Tattha tattheva rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutā manussatte, rājūnaṃ cakkavattinaṃ;
```

```
Maṇḍalīnañca rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
‘‘Sampattiṃ anubhotvāna, devesu manujesu ca;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhitā hutvā, nekakappesu saṃsariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, vipassī lokanāyako;
```

```
Uppajji cārudassano <note>cārunayano (sī. pī.)</note>, sabbadhammavipassako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
‘‘Tamahaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0214" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0545" /> lokanāyakaṃ, upetvā narasārathiṃ;
```

```
Dhammaṃ bhaṇitaṃ sutvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
‘‘Dasavassasahassāni<pb ed="M" n="2.0223" />, tassa vīrassa sāsane;
```

```
Brahmacariyaṃ caritvāna, yuttayogā bahussutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
‘‘Paccayākārakusalā, catusaccavisāradā;
```

```
Nipuṇā cittakathikā, satthusāsanakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutāhaṃ tusitaṃ, upapannā yasassinī;
```

```
Abhibhomi tahiṃ aññe, brahmacārīphalenahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha yatthūpapannāhaṃ, mahābhogā mahaddhanā;
```

```
Medhāvinī sīlavatī <note>rūpavatī (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, vinītaparisāpi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavāmi tena kammena, yogena jinasāsane;
```

```
Sabbā sampattiyo mayhaṃ, sulabhā manaso piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
‘‘Yopi <pb ed="T" n="2.0303" /> me bhavate bhattā, yattha yattha gatāyapi;
```

```
Vimāneti na maṃ koci, paṭipattibalena me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Nāmena koṇāgamano, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā hi bārāṇasiyaṃ, susamiddhakulappajā <note>susamiddhi… (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Dhanañjānī sumedhā ca, ahampi ca tayo janā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅghārāmamadāsimha, dānasahāyikā pure <note>neke sahassike mune (syā.), dānaṃ sahassikaṃ mune (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Saṅghassa ca vihārampi <note>sasaṃghassa vihāraṃ hi (syā. pī.)</note>, uddissa kārikā <note>dāyikā (pī.)</note> mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutā mayaṃ sabbā, tāvatiṃsūpagā ahuṃ;
```

```
Yasasā aggataṃ pattā, manussesu tatheva ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappamhi, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
```

```
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāsiṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0224" /> jeṭṭhikā dhītā, samaṇī iti vissutā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
‘‘Anujāni <pb ed="V" n="2.0215" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0546" /> na no tāto, agāreva tadā mayaṃ;
```

```
Vīsavassasahassāni, vicarimha atanditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
‘‘Komāribrahmacariyaṃ, rājakaññā sukhedhitā;
```

```
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, muditā satta dhītaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇī <pb ed="T" n="2.0304" /> samaṇaguttā ca, bhikkhunī bhikkhudāyikā;
```

```
Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca, sattamī saṅghadāyikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ uppalavaṇṇā ca, paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā;
```

```
Kisāgotamī dhammadinnā, visākhā hoti sattamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
‘‘Kadāci so narādicco, dhammaṃ desesi abbhutaṃ;
```

```
Mahānidānasuttantaṃ, sutvā taṃ pariyāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi kammehi sukatehi, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, sākalāya puruttame;
```

```
Rañño maddassa dhītāmhi, manāpā dayitā piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
‘‘Saha me jātamattamhi, khemaṃ tamhi pure ahu;
```

```
Tato khemāti nāmaṃ me, guṇato upapajjatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘Yadāhaṃ yobbanaṃ pattā, rūpalāvaññabhūsitā <note>rūpavaṇṇavibhūsitā (syā.), rūpavantā vibhūsitā (pī.), rūpavilāsabhūsitā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tadā adāsi maṃ tāto, bimbisārassa rājino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ suppiyā āsiṃ, rūpake lāyane ratā;
```

```
Rūpānaṃ dosavādīti, na upesiṃ mahādayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
‘‘Bimbisāro tadā rājā, mamānuggahabuddhiyā;
```

```
Vaṇṇayitvā veḷuvanaṃ, gāyake gāpayī mamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
‘‘Rammaṃ veḷuvanaṃ yena, na diṭṭhaṃ sugatālayaṃ;
```

```
Na tena nandanaṃ diṭṭhaṃ, iti maññāmase mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
‘‘Yena <pb ed="T" n="2.0305" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0225" /> veḷuvanaṃ diṭṭhaṃ, naranandananandanaṃ;
```

```
Sudiṭṭhaṃ nandanaṃ tena, amarindasunandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
‘‘Vihāya <pb ed="P" n="2.0547" /> nandanaṃ devā, otaritvā mahītalaṃ <note>mahītale (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Rammaṃ veḷuvanaṃ disvā, na tappanti suvimhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
‘‘Rājapuññena <pb ed="V" n="2.0216" /> nibbattaṃ, buddhapuññena bhūsitaṃ;
```

```
Ko vattā tassa nissesaṃ, vanassa guṇasañcayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā vanasamiddhaṃ, mama sotamanoharaṃ;
```

```
Daṭṭhukāmā tamuyyānaṃ, rañño ārocayiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
‘‘Mahatā parivārena, tadā ca so <note>tadā maṃ so (syā. pī.)</note> mahīpati;
```

```
Maṃ pesesi <note>saṃpesesi (syā.), sampāpesi (pī.)</note> tamuyyānaṃ, dassanāya samussukaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
‘‘Gaccha passa mahābhoge, vanaṃ nettarasāyanaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃ sadā bhāti siriyā, sugatābhānurañjitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā ca piṇḍāya muni, giribbajapuruttamaṃ;
```

```
Paviṭṭhohaṃ tadāyeva, vanaṃ daṭṭhumupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā taṃ phullavipinaṃ, nānābhamarakūjitaṃ;
```

```
Kokilāgītasahitaṃ, mayūragaṇanaccitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
‘‘Appasaddamanākiṇṇaṃ, nānācaṅkamabhūsitaṃ;
```

```
Kuṭimaṇḍapasaṅkiṇṇaṃ, yogīvaravirājitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
‘‘Vicarantī amaññissaṃ, saphalaṃ nayanaṃ mama;
```

```
Tatthāpi taruṇaṃ bhikkhuṃ, yuttaṃ disvā vicintayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
‘‘‘Īdise <pb ed="T" n="2.0306" /> vipine ramme, ṭhitoyaṃ navayobbane;
```

```
Vasantamiva kantena, rūpena ca samanvito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nisinno rukkhamūlamhi, muṇḍo saṅghāṭipāruto;
```

```
Jhāyate vatayaṃ bhikkhu, hitvā visayajaṃ ratiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nanu nāma gahaṭṭhena, kāmaṃ bhutvā yathāsukhaṃ;
```

```
Pacchā jiṇṇena dhammoyaṃ, caritabbo subhaddako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
‘‘Suññakanti <pb ed="M" n="2.0226" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0548" /> viditvāna, gandhagehaṃ jinālayaṃ;
```

```
Upetvā jinamaddakkhaṃ, udayantaṃva bhākaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
‘‘Ekakaṃ sukhamāsīnaṃ, bījamānaṃ varitthiyā;
```

```
Disvānevaṃ vicintesiṃ, nāyaṃ lūkho narāsabho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
‘‘Sā kaññā kanakābhāsā, padumānanalocanā;
```

```
Bimboṭṭhī kundadasanā, manonettarasāyanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
‘‘Hemadolābhasavanā <pb ed="V" n="2.0217" /> <note>hemadolā suvadīnā (syā.)</note>, kalikākārasutthanī <note>kalasākārasuttanī (sī. pī.), kamalākārasuttanī (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Vedimajjhāva sussoṇī <note>kanumajjhāva sussoṇī (sī.), vedimajjhā varasoṇī (syā. pī.)</note>, rambhoru cārubhūsanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
‘‘Rattaṃsakupasaṃbyānā, nīlamaṭṭhanivāsanā;
```

```
Atappaneyyarūpena, hāsabhāvasamanvitā <note>hāvabhāvasamanvitā (sī.), sabbābharaṇamaṇḍitā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā tamevaṃ cintesiṃ, ahoyamabhirūpinī;
```

```
Na mayānena nettena, diṭṭhapubbā kudācanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
‘‘Tato jarābhibhūtā sā, vivaṇṇā vikatānanā;
```

```
Bhinnadantā setasirā, salālā vadanāsuci.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkhittakaṇṇā <pb ed="T" n="2.0307" /> setakkhī, lambāsubhapayodharā;
```

```
Valivitatasabbaṅgī, sirāvitatadehinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
‘‘Nataṅgā daṇḍadutiyā, upphāsulikatā <note>uppaṇḍupaṇḍukā (sī. syā.)</note> kisā;
```

```
Pavedhamānā patitā, nissasantī muhuṃ muhuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
‘‘Tato me āsi saṃvego, abbhuto lomahaṃsano;
```

```
Dhiratthu rūpaṃ asuciṃ, ramante yattha bālisā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā mahākāruṇiko, disvā saṃviggamānasaṃ;
```

```
Udaggacitto sugato, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āturaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0549" /> asuciṃ pūtiṃ, passa kheme samussayaṃ;
```

```
Uggharantaṃ paggharantaṃ, bālānaṃ abhinanditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
‘‘‘Asubhāya <pb ed="M" n="2.0227" /> cittaṃ bhāvehi, ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ;
```

```
Sati kāyagatā tyatthu, nibbidā bahulā bhava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ, yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃ;
```

```
Ajjhattañca bahiddhā ca, kāye chandaṃ virājaya.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
‘‘‘Animittañca bhāvehi, mānānusayamujjaha;
```

```
Tato mānābhisamayā, upasantā carissasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ye rāgarattānupatanti sotaṃ, sayaṃ kataṃ makkaṭakova jālaṃ;
```

```
Etampi chetvāna paribbajanti, na pekkhino <note>anapekkhino (sī. syā. pī.)</note> kāmasukhaṃ pahāya’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="2.0308" /> kallitacittaṃ <note>kallikacittaṃ (syā.), kalikacittaṃ (pī.)</note> maṃ, ñatvāna narasārathi;
```

```
Mahānidānaṃ desesi, suttantaṃ vinayāya me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā <pb ed="V" n="2.0218" /> suttantaseṭṭhaṃ taṃ, pubbasaññamanussariṃ;
```

```
Tattha ṭhitāvahaṃ santī, dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
‘‘Nipatitvā mahesissa, pādamūlamhi tāvade;
```

```
Accayaṃ desanatthāya, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
‘‘‘Namo te sabbadassāvī, namo te karuṇākara;
```

```
Namo te tiṇṇasaṃsāra, namo te amataṃ dada.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§363.</p>

```
‘‘‘Diṭṭhigahanapakkhandā <note>… pakkhantā (sī. syā.)</note>, kāmarāgavimohitā;
```

```
Tayā sammā upāyena, vinītā vinaye ratā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§364.</p>

```
‘‘‘Adassanena vibhogā <note>vibbhogā (sī.), vihitā (syā.)</note>, tādisānaṃ mahesinaṃ;
```

```
Anubhonti mahādukkhaṃ, sattā saṃsārasāgare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§365.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yadāhaṃ lokasaraṇaṃ, araṇaṃ araṇantaguṃ <note>maraṇantagaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Nāddasāmi adūraṭṭhaṃ, desayāmi <note>desessāmi (syā.)</note> tamaccayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§366.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahāhitaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0228" /> varadadaṃ, ahitoti visaṅkitā;
```

```
Nopesiṃ rūpaniratā, desayāmi tamaccayaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§367.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="P" n="2.0550" /> madhuranigghoso, mahākāruṇiko jino;
```

```
Avoca tiṭṭha khemeti, siñcanto amatena maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§368.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā paṇamya sirasā, katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
```

```
Gantvā disvā narapatiṃ, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§369.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aho <pb ed="T" n="2.0309" /> sammā upāyo te, cintitoyamarindama;
```

```
Vanadassanakāmāya, diṭṭho nibbānato muni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§370.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yadi te ruccate rāja <note>rājā (syā.)</note>, sāsane tassa tādino;
```

```
Pabbajissāmi rūpehaṃ, nibbinnā munivāṇinā’ <note>munibhāṇinā (syā. pī.)</note>.
```

Dutiyaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§371.</p>

```
‘‘Añjaliṃ paggahetvāna, tadāha sa mahīpati;
```

```
‘Anujānāmi te bhadde, pabbajjā tava sijjhatu’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§372.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvā tadā cāhaṃ, addhamāse <note>sattamāse (syā.)</note> upaṭṭhite;
```

```
Dīpodayañca bhedañca, disvā saṃviggamānasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§373.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbinnā <pb ed="V" n="2.0219" /> sabbasaṅkhāre, paccayākārakovidā;
```

```
Caturoghe atikkamma, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§374.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī āsiṃ, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī cāpi bhavāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§375.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§376.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Parisuddhaṃ mama ñāṇaṃ, uppannaṃ buddhasāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§377.</p>

```
‘‘Kusalāhaṃ visuddhīsu, kathāvatthuvisāradā;
```

```
Abhidhammanayaññū ca, vasippattāmhi sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§378.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="2.0310" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0229" /> toraṇavatthusmiṃ, raññā kosalasāminā;
```

```
Pucchitā nipuṇe pañhe, byākarontī yathātathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§379.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā sa rājā sugataṃ, upasaṅkamma pucchatha;
```

```
Tatheva buddho byākāsi, yathā te byākatā mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§380.</p>

```
‘‘Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
```

```
Mahāpaññānamaggāti, bhikkhunīnaṃ naruttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§381.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0551" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§382.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§383.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ khemā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Khemātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Uppalavaṇṇātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§384.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhunī uppalavaṇṇā, iddhiyā pāramiṃ gatā;
```

```
Vanditvā satthuno pāde, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§385.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nitthiṇṇā <pb ed="V" n="2.0220" /> jātisaṃsāraṃ <note>jātisaṃsārā (pī.)</note>, pattāhaṃ acalaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Sabbadukkhaṃ mayā khīṇaṃ, ārocemi mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§386.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yāvatā <pb ed="T" n="2.0311" /> parisā atthi, pasannā jinasāsane;
```

```
Yassā ca meparādhotthi, khamantu jinasammukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§387.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṃsāre saṃsarantiyā <note>saṃsarantā me (syā.)</note>, khalitaṃ me sace bhave;
```

```
Ārocemi mahāvīra, aparādhaṃ khamassu taṃ <note>me (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§388.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iddhiñcāpi nidassehi, mama sāsanakārike;
```

```
Catasso parisā ajja, kaṅkhaṃ chindāhi yāvatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§389.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhītā tuyhaṃ mahāvīra, paññavanta jutindhara;
```

```
Bahuñca dukkaraṃ kammaṃ, kataṃ me atidukkaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§390.</p>

```
‘‘‘Uppalasseva <pb ed="M" n="2.0230" /> me vaṇṇo, nāmenuppalanāmikā;
```

```
Sāvikā te mahāvīra, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§391.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rāhulo ca ahañceva, nekajātisate bahū;
```

```
Ekasmiṃ sambhave jātā, samānachandamānasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§392.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nibbatti ekato hoti, jātiyāpi ca ekato <note>jātīsu bahuso mama (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Pacchime bhave sampatte, ubhopi nānāsambhavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§393.</p>

```
‘‘‘Putto ca rāhulo nāma, dhītā uppalasavhayā;
```

```
Passa vīra mamaṃ iddhiṃ, balaṃ dassemi satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§394.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahāsamudde <pb ed="P" n="2.0552" /> caturo, pakkhipi hatthapātiyaṃ;
```

```
Telaṃ hatthagatañceva, khiḍḍo <note>vejjo (sī. pī.)</note> komārako yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§395.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ubbattayitvā pathaviṃ, pakkhipi hatthapātiyaṃ;
```

```
Cittaṃ muñjaṃ yathā nāma, luñci komārako yuvā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§396.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cakkavāḷasamaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0312" /> pāṇiṃ, chādayitvāna matthake;
```

```
Vassāpetvāna phusitaṃ, nānāvaṇṇaṃ punappunaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§397.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhūmiṃ udukkhalaṃ katvā, dhaññaṃ katvāna sakkharaṃ;
```

```
Sineruṃ musalaṃ katvā, maddi komārikā yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§398.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhītāhaṃ buddhaseṭṭhassa, nāmenuppalasavhayā;
```

```
Abhiññāsu vasībhūtā, tava sāsanakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§399.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nānāvikubbanaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0221" /> katvā, dassetvā lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Nāmagottañca sāvetvā <note>pakāsetvā (syā.)</note>, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§400.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§401.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§402.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ <note>vipulaṃ (syā.)</note> suddhaṃ, sabhāvena mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§403.</p>

```
‘‘‘Purimānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0231" /> jinaggānaṃ, saṅgamaṃ te nidassitaṃ <note>sammukhā ca parammukhā (sī.)</note>;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§404.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yaṃ mayā pūritaṃ kammaṃ, kusalaṃ sara me muni;
```

```
Tavatthāya mahāvīra, puññaṃ upacitaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§405.</p>

```
‘‘‘Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā, vārayantī <note>parivajjanti (sī.), paripācento (syā.)</note> anācaraṃ;
```

```
Tavatthāya mahāvīra, cattaṃ me jīvituttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§406.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dasakoṭisahassāni<pb ed="T" n="2.0313" />, adāsiṃ mama jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Pariccattā ca me homi, tavatthāya mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§407.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tadātivimhitā sabbā, sirasāva katañjalī;
```

```
Avocayye kathaṃ āsi, atuliddhiparakkamā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§408.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="P" n="2.0553" /> kappe, nāgakaññā ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Vimalā nāma nāmena, kaññānaṃ sādhusammatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§409.</p>

```
‘‘Mahorago mahānāgo, pasanno jinasāsane;
```

```
Padumuttaraṃ mahātejaṃ, nimantesi sasāvakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§410.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanamayaṃ maṇḍapaṃ, pallaṅkaṃ ratanāmayaṃ;
```

```
Ratanaṃ vālukākiṇṇaṃ, upabhogaṃ ratanāmayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§411.</p>

```
‘‘Maggañca paṭiyādesi, ratanaddhajabhūsitaṃ;
```

```
Paccuggantvāna sambuddhaṃ, vajjanto tūriyehi so.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§412.</p>

```
‘‘Parisāhi ca catūhi <note>parisāhi catūhi so (sī.), parisāhi catasso hi (pī.)</note>, parivuto <note>sahito (sī.), pharate (syā.), pareto (pī.)</note> lokanāyako;
```

```
Mahoragassa bhavane, nisīdi paramāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§413.</p>

```
‘‘Annaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0222" /> pānaṃ khādanīyaṃ, bhojanañca mahārahaṃ;
```

```
Varaṃ varañca pādāsi, nāgarājā mahāyasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§414.</p>

```
‘‘Bhuñjitvāna sambuddho, pattaṃ dhovitvā yoniso;
```

```
Anumodanīyaṃkāsi, nāgakaññā mahiddhikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§415.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbaññuṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0232" /> phullitaṃ disvā, nāgakaññā mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Pasannaṃ satthuno cittaṃ, sunibandhañca mānasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§416.</p>

```
‘‘Mamañca <pb ed="T" n="2.0314" /> cittamaññāya, jalajuttamanāmako;
```

```
Tasmiṃ khaṇe mahāvīro, bhikkhuniṃ dassayiddhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§417.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhī anekā dassesi, bhikkhunī sā visāradā;
```

```
Pamoditā vedajātā, satthāraṃ idamabravi <note>etadabraviṃ (syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§418.</p>

```
‘‘‘Addasāhaṃ imaṃ iddhiṃ, sumanaṃ itarāyapi;
```

```
Kathaṃ ahosi sā vīra, iddhiyā suvisāradā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§419.</p>

```
‘‘‘Orasā mukhato jātā, dhītā mama mahiddhikā;
```

```
Mamānusāsanikarā, iddhiyā suvisāradā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§420.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhassa vacanaṃ sutvā, evaṃ patthesahaṃ tadā <note>tuṭṭhā evaṃ avocahaṃ (syā.), evamahosahaṃ tadā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
Ahampi tādisā homi, iddhiyā suvisāradā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§421.</p>

```
‘‘Pamoditāhaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0554" /> sumanā, patthe uttamamānasā <note>pattauttamamānasā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Anāgatamhi addhāne, īdisā homi nāyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§422.</p>

```
‘‘Maṇimayamhi pallaṅke, maṇḍapamhi pabhassare;
```

```
Annapānena tappetvā, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§423.</p>

```
‘‘Nāgānaṃ pavaraṃ pupphaṃ, aruṇaṃ nāma uppalaṃ;
```

```
Vaṇṇaṃ me īdisaṃ hotu, pūjesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§424.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§425.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutāhaṃ manuje, upapannā sayambhuno;
```

```
Uppalehi paṭicchannaṃ, piṇḍapātamadāsahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§426.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="T" n="2.0315" /> kappe, vipassī nāma nāyako;
```

```
Uppajji cārudassano, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§427.</p>

```
‘‘Seṭṭhidhītā <pb ed="V" n="2.0223" /> tadā hutvā, bārāṇasipuruttame;
```

```
Nimantetvāna sambuddhaṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§428.</p>

```
‘‘Mahādānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0233" /> daditvāna, uppalehi vināyakaṃ;
```

```
