Pūjayitvā cetasāva <note>ca teheva (syā. pī.)</note>, vaṇṇasobhaṃ apatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§429.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§430.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
```

```
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§431.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāsiṃ dutiyā dhītā, samaṇaguttasavhayā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§432.</p>

```
‘‘Anujāni na no tāto, agāreva tadā mayaṃ;
```

```
Vīsavassasahassāni, vicarimha atanditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§433.</p>

```
‘‘Komāribrahmacariyaṃ, rājakaññā sukhedhitā;
```

```
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, muditā sattadhītaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§434.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇī samaṇaguttā ca, bhikkhunī bhikkhudāyikā <note>bhikkhudāsikā (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca, sattamī saṅghadāyikā <note>saṃghadāsikā (sī. syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§435.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ khemā ca sappaññā, paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā;
```

```
Kisāgotamī dhammadinnā, visākhā hoti sattamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§436.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi <pb ed="T" n="2.0316" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0555" /> kammehi sukatehi, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§437.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutā manussesu, upapannā mahākule;
```

```
Pītaṃ maṭṭhaṃ varaṃ dussaṃ, adaṃ arahato ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§438.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutāriṭṭhapure, jātā vippakule ahaṃ;
```

```
Dhītā tiriṭivacchassa, ummādantī manoharā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§439.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutā janapade, kule aññatare ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasūtā nātiphītamhi, sāliṃ gopemahaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§440.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā paccekasambuddhaṃ, pañcalājāsatānihaṃ;
```

```
Datvā padumacchannāni, pañca puttasatānihaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§441.</p>

```
‘‘Patthayiṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0234" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0224" /> tepi patthesuṃ, madhuṃ datvā sayambhuno;
```

```
Tato cutā araññehaṃ, ajāyiṃ padumodare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§442.</p>

```
‘‘Kāsirañño mahesīhaṃ, hutvā sakkatapūjitā;
```

```
Ajaniṃ rājaputtānaṃ, anūnaṃ satapañcakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§443.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā te yobbanappattā, kīḷantā jalakīḷitaṃ;
```

```
Disvā opattapadumaṃ, āsuṃ paccekanāyakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§444.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ tehi vinābhūtā, sutavīrehi sokinī <note>sutavarehi sokinī (sī. syā.)</note>;
```

```
Cutā isigilipasse, gāmakamhi ajāyihaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§445.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā buddhā sutamatī, sutānaṃ bhattunopi ca <note>kasataṃ tadā (sī.), attanopi ca (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Yāguṃ ādāya gacchantī, aṭṭha paccekanāyake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§446.</p>

```
‘‘Bhikkhāya <pb ed="T" n="2.0317" /> gāmaṃ gacchante, disvā putte anussariṃ;
```

```
Khīradhārā viniggacchi, tadā me puttapemasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§447.</p>

```
‘‘Tato tesaṃ adaṃ yāguṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi;
```

```
Tato cutāhaṃ tidasaṃ, nandanaṃ upapajjahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§448.</p>

```
‘‘Anubhotvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ, saṃsaritvā bhavābhave;
```

```
Tavatthāya mahāvīra, pariccattañca jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§449.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0556" /> bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ, sampattī ca bahubbidhā;
```

```
Pacchime bhave sampatte, jātā sāvatthiyaṃ pure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§450.</p>

```
‘‘Mahādhanaseṭṭhikule, sukhite sajjite tathā;
```

```
Nānāratanapajjote, sabbakāmasamiddhine.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§451.</p>

```
‘‘Sakkatā pūjitā ceva, mānitāpacitā tathā;
```

```
Rūpasīrimanuppattā <note>rūpasobhaggasampannā (sī.)</note>, kulesu atisakkatā <note>abhisammatā (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§452.</p>

```
‘‘Atīva patthitā cāsiṃ, rūpabhogasirīhi ca;
```

```
Patthitā seṭṭhiputtehi, anekehi satehipi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§453.</p>

```
‘‘Agāraṃ pajahitvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Aḍḍhamāse asampatte, catusaccamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§454.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhiyā <pb ed="M" n="2.0235" /> abhinimmitvā, caturassaṃ rathaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Buddhassa pāde vandissaṃ, lokanāthassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§455.</p>

```
‘‘‘Supupphitaggaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0225" /> upagamma pādapaṃ <note>bhikkhunī (sī. pī. ka.) therīgā. 230</note>, ekā tuvaṃ tiṭṭhasi sālamūle;
```

```
Na <pb ed="T" n="2.0318" /> cāpi te dutiyo atthi koci <note>na catthi te dutiyā vaṇṇadhātu (sī. pī. ka.)</note>, bāle na tvaṃ bhāyasi dhuttakānaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§456.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sataṃ sahassānipi dhuttakānaṃ <note>sahassānampi dhuttakānaṃ (pī.) therīgā. 231</note>, samāgatā edisakā bhaveyyuṃ;
```

```
Lomaṃ na iñje na sampavedhe, kiṃ me tuvaṃ māra karissaseko <note>na māra bhāyāmi tavekikāpi (sī. ka.) … tamekikāsiṃ (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§457.</p>

```
‘‘‘Esā antaradhāyāmi, kucchiṃ vā pavisāmi te;
```

```
Bhamukantarikāyampi, tiṭṭhantiṃ maṃ na dakkhasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§458.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cittasmiṃ vasībhūtāmhi, iddhipādā subhāvitā;
```

```
Sabbabandhanamuttāmhi, na taṃ bhāyāmi āvuso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§459.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sattisūlūpamā kāmā, khandhāsaṃ adhikuṭṭanā;
```

```
Yaṃ tvaṃ kāmaratiṃ brūsi, aratī dāni sā mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§460.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbattha <pb ed="P" n="2.0557" /> vihatā nandī, tamokhandho padālito;
```

```
Evaṃ jānāhi pāpima, nihato tvamasi antaka’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§461.</p>

```
‘‘Jino tamhi guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
```

```
Aggā iddhimatīnanti, parisāsu vināyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§462.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§463.</p>

```
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§464.</p>

```
‘‘Cīvaraṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0319" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0236" /> piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Khaṇena upanāmenti, sahassāni samantato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§465.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā;
```

<p rend="hangnum">§466.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§467.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ uppalavaṇṇā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Uppalavaṇṇātheriyāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Paṭācārātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§468.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="V" n="2.0226" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§469.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ;
```

```
Nānāratanapajjote, mahāsukhasamappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§470.</p>

```
‘‘Upetvā taṃ mahāvīraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
```

```
Tato jātapasādāhaṃ, upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§471.</p>

```
‘‘Tato vinayadhārīnaṃ, aggaṃ vaṇṇesi nāyako;
```

```
Bhikkhuniṃ lajjiniṃ tādiṃ, kappākappavisāradaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§472.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="T" n="2.0320" /> muditacittāhaṃ, taṃ ṭhānamabhikaṅkhinī;
```

```
Nimantetvā dasabalaṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§473.</p>

```
‘‘Bhojayitvāna sattāhaṃ, daditvāva ticīvaraṃ <note>daditvā pattacīvaraṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Nipacca sirasā pāde, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§474.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yā tayā vaṇṇitā vīra, ito aṭṭhamake muni;
```

```
Tādisāhaṃ bhavissāmi, yadi sijjhati nāyaka’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§475.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="P" n="2.0558" /> avoca maṃ satthā, ‘bhadde mā bhāyi assasa;
```

```
Anāgatamhi addhāne, lacchase taṃ manorathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§476.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="M" n="2.0237" /> kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§477.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Paṭācārāti nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§478.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ muditā <note>pamudī (ka.)</note> hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Mettacittā paricariṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§479.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§480.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§481.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko <pb ed="V" n="2.0227" /> mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
```

```
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§482.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāsiṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0321" /> tatiyā dhītā, bhikkhunī iti vissutā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§483.</p>

```
‘‘Anujāni na no tāto, agāreva tadā mayaṃ;
```

```
Vīsavassasahassāni, vicarimha atanditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§484.</p>

```
‘‘Komāribrahmacariyaṃ, rājakaññā sukhedhitā;
```

```
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, muditā sattadhītaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§485.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇī samaṇaguttā ca, bhikkhunī bhikkhudāyikā;
```

```
Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca, sattamī saṅghadāyikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§486.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ uppalavaṇṇā ca, khemā bhaddā ca bhikkhunī;
```

```
Kisāgotamī dhammadinnā, visākhā hoti sattamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§487.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi kammehi sukatehi, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§488.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātā seṭṭhikule ahaṃ;
```

```
Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare, iddhe phīte mahaddhane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§489.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0238" /> ca yobbanūpetā, vitakkavasagā ahaṃ;
```

```
Naraṃ jārapatiṃ disvā, tena saddhiṃ agacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§490.</p>

```
‘‘Ekaputtapasūtāhaṃ<pb ed="P" n="2.0559" />, dutiyo kucchiyā mamaṃ;
```

```
Tadāhaṃ mātāpitaro, okkhāmīti <note>ikkhāmīti (syā.), dakkhāmīti (sī.)</note> sunicchitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§491.</p>

```
‘‘Nārocesiṃ patiṃ mayhaṃ, tadā tamhi pavāsite;
```

```
Ekikā niggatā gehā, gantuṃ sāvatthimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§492.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="2.0322" /> me sāmi āgantvā, sambhāvesi pathe mamaṃ;
```

```
Tadā me kammajā vātā, uppannā atidāruṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§493.</p>

```
‘‘Uṭṭhito ca mahāmegho, pasūtisamaye mama;
```

```
Dabbatthāya tadā gantvā, sāmi sappena mārito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§494.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā vijātadukkhena, anāthā kapaṇā ahaṃ;
```

```
Kunnadiṃ pūritaṃ disvā, gacchantī sakulālayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§495.</p>

```
‘‘Bālaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0228" /> ādāya atariṃ, pārakūle ca ekakaṃ;
```

```
Sāyetvā <note>pāyetvā (syā.), pātetvā (ka.)</note> bālakaṃ puttaṃ, itaraṃ taraṇāyahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§496.</p>

```
‘‘Nivattā ukkuso hāsi, taruṇaṃ vilapantakaṃ;
```

```
Itarañca vahī soto, sāhaṃ sokasamappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§497.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvatthinagaraṃ gantvā, assosiṃ sajane mate;
```

```
Tadā avocaṃ sokaṭṭā, mahāsokasamappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§498.</p>

```
‘‘Ubho puttā kālaṅkatā, panthe mayhaṃ patī mato;
```

```
Mātā pitā ca bhātā ca, ekacitamhi ḍayhare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§499.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā kisā ca paṇḍu ca, anāthā dīnamānasā;
```

```
Ito tato bhamantīhaṃ <note>gacchantīhaṃ (syā.), gamentīhaṃ (ka.)</note>, addasaṃ narasārathiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§500.</p>

```
‘‘Tato avoca maṃ satthā, ‘putte mā soci assasa;
```

```
Attānaṃ te gavesassu, kiṃ niratthaṃ vihaññasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§501.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na santi puttā tāṇāya, na ñātī napi bandhavā;
```

```
Antakenādhipannassa, natthi ñātīsu tāṇatā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§502.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0323" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0239" /> sutvā munino vākyaṃ, paṭhamaṃ phalamajjhagaṃ;
```

```
Pabbajitvāna naciraṃ, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§503.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="P" n="2.0560" /> ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Paracittāni jānāmi, satthusāsanakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§504.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§505.</p>

```
‘‘Tatohaṃ vinayaṃ sabbaṃ, santike sabbadassino;
```

```
Uggahiṃ sabbavitthāraṃ, byāhariñca yathātathaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§506.</p>

```
‘‘Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
```

```
Aggā vinayadhārīnaṃ, paṭācārāva ekikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§507.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§508.</p>

```
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§509.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0229" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§510.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§511.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0324" /> sudaṃ paṭācārā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Paṭācārātheriyāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Ekūposathikavaggo dutiyo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Ekūposathikā ceva, saḷalā cātha modakā;
```

```
Ekāsanā pañcadīpā, naḷamālī ca gotamī.
```

```
Khemā uppalavaṇṇā ca, paṭācārā ca bhikkhunī;
```

```
Gāthā satāni pañceva, nava cāpi taduttari.
```

### 3. Kuṇḍalakesīvaggo

#### 1. Kuṇḍalakesātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0325" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0240" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0230" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ;
```

```
Nānāratanapajjote, mahāsukhasamappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Upetvā <pb ed="P" n="2.0561" /> taṃ mahāvīraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
```

```
Tato jātappasādāhaṃ, upesiṃ saraṇaṃ jinaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā mahākāruṇiko, padumuttaranāmako;
```

```
Khippābhiññānamagganti, ṭhapesi bhikkhuniṃ subhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, dānaṃ datvā mahesino;
```

```
Nipacca sirasā pāde, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Anumodi mahāvīro, ‘bhadde yaṃ tebhipatthitaṃ;
```

```
Samijjhissati taṃ sabbaṃ, sukhinī hohi nibbutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Bhaddākuṇḍalakesāti, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0326" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutā yāmamagaṃ, tatohaṃ tusitaṃ gatā;
```

```
Tato ca nimmānaratiṃ, vasavattipuraṃ tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha yatthūpapajjāmi, tassa kammassa vāhasā;
```

```
Tattha tattheva rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="V" n="2.0231" /> cutā manussesu, rājūnaṃ cakkavattinaṃ;
```

```
Maṇḍalīnañca rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Sampattiṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0241" /> anubhotvāna, devesu mānusesu ca;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhitā hutvā, nekakappesu saṃsariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
```

```
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa dhītā catutthāsiṃ, bhikkhudāyīti vissutā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Anujāni na no tāto, agāreva tadā mayaṃ;
```

```
Vīsavassasahassāni, vicarimha atanditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Komāribrahmacariyaṃ, rājakaññā sukhedhitā;
```

```
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, muditā satta dhītaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇī <pb ed="T" n="2.0327" /> samaṇaguttā ca, bhikkhunī bhikkhudāyikā;
```

```
Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca, sattamī saṅghadāyikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Khemā <pb ed="P" n="2.0562" /> uppalavaṇṇā ca, paṭācārā ahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Kisāgotamī dhammadinnā, visākhā hoti sattamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi kammehi sukatehi, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, giribbajapuruttame;
```

```
Jātā seṭṭhikule phīte, yadāhaṃ yobbane ṭhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Coraṃ vadhatthaṃ nīyantaṃ, disvā rattā tahiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Pitā me taṃ sahassena, mocayitvā vadhā tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Adāsi tassa maṃ tāto, viditvāna manaṃ mama;
```

```
Tassāhamāsiṃ visaṭṭhā, atīva dayitā hitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘So me bhūsanalobhena, balimajjhāsayo <note>khalitajjhāsayo (sī.), baliṃ paccāharaṃ (syā.), mālapacchāhataṃ (pī.)</note> diso;
```

```
Corappapātaṃ netvāna, pabbataṃ cetayī vadhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0242" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0232" /> paṇamitvāna, sattukaṃ sukatañjalī;
```

```
Rakkhantī attano pāṇaṃ, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘‘Idaṃ suvaṇṇakeyūraṃ, muttā veḷuriyā bahū;
```

```
Sabbaṃ harassu <note>varassu (ka.)</note> bhaddante, mañca dāsīti sāvaya’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘‘Oropayassu kalyāṇī, mā bāḷhaṃ paridevasi;
```

```
Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi, ahantvā dhanamābhataṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yato <pb ed="T" n="2.0328" /> sarāmi attānaṃ, yato pattosmi viññutaṃ;
```

```
Na cāhaṃ abhijānāmi, aññaṃ piyataraṃ tayā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘‘Ehi taṃ upagūhissaṃ, katvāna taṃ padakkhiṇaṃ;
```

```
Na ca dāni puno atthi <note>taṃ vandāmi puna natthi (syā.)</note>, mama tuyhañca saṅgamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, puriso hoti paṇḍito;
```

```
Itthīpi paṇḍitā hoti, tattha tattha vicakkhaṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na hi sabbesu ṭhānesu, puriso hoti paṇḍito;
```

```
Itthīpi paṇḍitā hoti, lahuṃ atthavicintikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘‘Lahuñca <pb ed="P" n="2.0563" /> vata khippañca, nikaṭṭhe <note>nekatthe (sī. syā.)</note> samacetayiṃ;
```

```
Migaṃ uṇṇā yathā evaṃ <note>cittapuṇṇāya tāneva (syā.), migaṃ puṇṇāya teneva (pī.)</note>, tadāhaṃ sattukaṃ vadhiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, na khippamanubujjhati;
```

```
So haññate mandamati, corova girigabbhare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo ca uppatitaṃ atthaṃ, khippameva nibodhati;
```

```
Muccate sattusambādhā, tadāhaṃ sattukā yathā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ pātayitvāna, giriduggamhi sattukaṃ;
```

```
Santikaṃ setavatthānaṃ, upetvā pabbajiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Saṇḍāsena ca kese me, luñcitvā sabbaso tadā;
```

```
Pabbajitvāna samayaṃ, ācikkhiṃsu nirantaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Tato taṃ uggahetvāhaṃ, nisīditvāna ekikā;
```

```
Samayaṃ taṃ vicintesiṃ, suvāno mānusaṃ karaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Chinnaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0329" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0243" /> gayha samīpe me, pātayitvā apakkami;
```

```
Disvā nimittamalabhiṃ, hatthaṃ taṃ puḷavākulaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="V" n="2.0233" /> uṭṭhāya saṃviggā, apucchiṃ sahadhammike;
```

```
Te avocuṃ vijānanti, taṃ atthaṃ sakyabhikkhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ tamatthaṃ pucchissaṃ, upetvā buddhasāvake;
```

```
Te mamādāya gacchiṃsu, buddhaseṭṭhassa santikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘So me dhammamadesesi, khandhāyatanadhātuyo;
```

```
Asubhāniccadukkhāti, anattāti ca nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ, dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ;
```

```
Tato viññātasaddhammā, pabbajjaṃ upasampadaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘Āyācito tadā āha, ‘ehi bhadde’ti nāyako;
```

```
Tadāhaṃ upasampannā, parittaṃ toyamaddasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Pādapakkhālanenāhaṃ<pb ed="P" n="2.0564" />, ñatvā saudayabbayaṃ;
```

```
Tathā sabbepi saṅkhāre, īdisaṃ cintayiṃ <note>saṅkhārā, iti saṃcintayiṃ (sī. syā. pī.)</note> tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cittaṃ vimucci me, anupādāya sabbaso;
```

```
Khippābhiññānamaggaṃ me, tadā paññāpayī jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Paracittāni jānāmi, satthusāsanakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo <pb ed="T" n="2.0330" /> mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="M" n="2.0244" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="V" n="2.0234" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhaddākuṇḍalakesā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kuṇḍalakesātheriyāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Kisāgotamītherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0331" /> haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā aññatare kule;
```

```
Upetvā taṃ naravaraṃ, saraṇaṃ samupāgamiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Dhammañca tassa assosiṃ, catusaccūpasañhitaṃ;
```

```
Madhuraṃ paramassādaṃ, vaṭṭasantisukhāvahaṃ <note>cittasanti … (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā ca bhikkhuniṃ vīro, lūkhacīvaradhāriniṃ;
```

```
Ṭhapento etadaggamhi, vaṇṇayī purisuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘Janetvānappakaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0565" /> pītiṃ, sutvā bhikkhuniyā guṇe;
```

```
Kāraṃ katvāna buddhassa, yathāsatti yathābalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Nipacca munivaraṃ taṃ, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ;
```

```
Tadānumodi sambuddho, ṭhānalābhāya nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Kisāgotamī <note>gotamī nāma (sī. ka.)</note> nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0245" /> sutvā muditā hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Mettacittā paricariṃ, paccayehi vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi <pb ed="V" n="2.0235" /> bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko <pb ed="T" n="2.0332" /> mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
```

```
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcamī tassa dhītāsiṃ, dhammā nāmena vissutā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Anujāni na no tāto, agāreva tadā mayaṃ;
```

```
Vīsavassasahassāni, vicarimha atanditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Komāribrahmacariyaṃ, rājakaññā sukhedhitā;
```

```
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, muditā satta dhītaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇī samaṇaguttā ca, bhikkhunī bhikkhudāyikā;
```

```
Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca, sattamī saṅghadāyikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Khemā uppalavaṇṇā ca, paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā;
```

```
Ahañca dhammadinnā ca, visākhā hoti sattamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi kammehi sukatehi, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātā seṭṭhikule ahaṃ;
```

```
Duggate adhane naṭṭhe <note>nīce (syā.), niddhe (pī.)</note>, gatā ca sadhanaṃ kulaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Patiṃ ṭhapetvā sesā me, dessanti adhanā iti;
```

```
Yadā ca pasūtā <note>sasutā (sī. pī.)</note> āsiṃ, sabbesaṃ dayitā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="P" n="2.0566" /> so taruṇo bhaddo <note>putto (sī. syā.)</note>, komalako <note>komārako (syā.), komalaṅgo (sī. pī.)</note> sukhedhito;
```

```
Sapāṇamiva kanto me, tadā yamavasaṃ gato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Sokaṭṭā <pb ed="T" n="2.0333" /> dīnavadanā<pb ed="M" n="2.0246" />, assunettā rudammukhā;
```

```
Mataṃ kuṇapamādāya, vilapantī gamāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā ekena sandiṭṭhā, upetvābhisakkuttamaṃ;
```

```
Avocaṃ dehi bhesajjaṃ, puttasañjīvananti bho.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Na vijjante matā yasmiṃ, gehe siddhatthakaṃ tato;
```

```
Āharāti jino āha, vinayopāyakovido.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="V" n="2.0236" /> gamitvā sāvatthiṃ, na labhiṃ tādisaṃ gharaṃ;
```

```
Kuto siddhatthakaṃ tasmā, tato laddhā satiṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Kuṇapaṃ chaḍḍayitvāna, upesiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Dūratova mamaṃ disvā, avoca madhurassaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo ca vassasataṃ jīve, apassaṃ udayabbayaṃ;
```

```
Ekāhaṃ jīvitaṃ seyyo, passato udayabbayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na gāmadhammo nigamassa dhammo, na cāpiyaṃ ekakulassa dhammo;
```

```
Sabbassa lokassa sadevakassa, eseva dhammo yadidaṃ aniccatā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ sutvānimā <note>sahasutvānimā (ka.)</note> gāthā, dhammacakkhuṃ visodhayiṃ;
```

```
Tato viññātasaddhammā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Tathā pabbajitā santī, yuñjantī jinasāsane;
```

```
Na cireneva kālena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="T" n="2.0334" /> ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Paracittāni jānāmi, satthusāsanakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Yassatthāya <pb ed="M" n="2.0247" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0567" /> pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘Saṅkārakūṭā āhitvā, susānā rathiyāpi ca;
```

```
Tato saṅghāṭikaṃ katvā, lūkhaṃ dhāremi cīvaraṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, lūkhacīvaradhāraṇe;
```

```
Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi, parisāsu vināyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0237" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0335" /> sudaṃ kisāgotamī bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Kisāgotamītheriyāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Dhammadinnātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, kule aññatare ahuṃ;
```

```
Parakammakārī āsiṃ, nipakā sīlasaṃvutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttarabuddhassa, sujāto aggasāvako;
```

```
Vihārā abhinikkhamma, piṇḍapātāya <note>pattamādāya (ka.)</note> gacchati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Ghaṭaṃ gahetvā gacchantī, tadā udakahārikā;
```

```
Taṃ disvā adadaṃ pūpaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭiggahetvā tattheva, nisinno paribhuñji so;
```

```
Tato netvāna taṃ gehaṃ, adāsiṃ tassa bhojanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="M" n="2.0248" /> me ayyako tuṭṭho, akarī suṇisaṃ sakaṃ;
```

```
Sassuyā saha gantvāna, sambuddhaṃ abhivādayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā so dhammakathikaṃ, bhikkhuniṃ parikittayaṃ;
```

```
Ṭhapesi etadaggamhi, taṃ sutvā muditā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Nimantayitvā <pb ed="P" n="2.0568" /> sugataṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Mahādānaṃ daditvāna, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="T" n="2.0336" /> maṃ sugato āha, ghananinnādasussaro <note>ghananinnādasussare (ka.)</note>;
```

```
‘Mamupaṭṭhānanirate, sasaṅghaparivesike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saddhammassavane <pb ed="V" n="2.0238" /> yutte, guṇavaddhitamānase;
```

```
Bhadde bhavassu muditā, lacchase paṇidhīphalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Dhammadinnāti nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ mahāmuniṃ;
```

```
Mettacittā paricariṃ, paccayehi vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Upaṭṭhāko mahesissa, tadā āsi narissaro;
```

```
Kāsirājā kikī nāma, bārāṇasipuruttame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Chaṭṭhā tassāsahaṃ dhītā, sudhammā iti vissutā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvā jinaggassa, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Anujāni na no tāto, agāreva tadā mayaṃ;
```

```
Vīsavassasahassāni, vicarimha atanditā.
```

Tatiyaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Komāribrahmacariyaṃ<pb ed="T" n="2.0337" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0249" />, rājakaññā sukhedhitā;
```

```
Buddhopaṭṭhānaniratā, muditā satta dhītaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Samaṇī samaṇaguttā ca, bhikkhunī bhikkhudāyikā;
```

```
Dhammā ceva sudhammā ca, sattamī saṅghadāyikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Khemā uppalavaṇṇā ca, paṭācārā ca kuṇḍalā;
```

```
Gotamī ca ahañceva, visākhā hoti sattamī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Tehi kammehi sukatehi, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="V" n="2.0239" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0569" /> ca bhave dāni, giribbajapuruttame;
```

```
Jātā seṭṭhikule phīte, sabbakāmasamiddhine.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā rūpaguṇūpetā, paṭhame yobbane ṭhitā;
```

```
Tadā parakulaṃ gantvā, vasiṃ sukhasamappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Upetvā lokasaraṇaṃ, suṇitvā dhammadesanaṃ;
```

```
Anāgāmiphalaṃ patto, sāmiko me subuddhimā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ anujānetvā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Na cireneva kālena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā upāsako so maṃ, upagantvā apucchatha;
```

```
Gambhīre nipuṇe pañhe, te sabbe byākariṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
```

```
‘Bhikkhuniṃ dhammakathikaṃ, nāññaṃ passāmi edisiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘Dhammadinnā <pb ed="T" n="2.0338" /> yathā dhīrā, evaṃ dhāretha bhikkhavo’;
```

```
‘‘Evāhaṃ paṇḍitā homi <note>jātā (sī.), nāma (syā.)</note>, nāyakenānukampitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Yassatthāya pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```

```

So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="M" n="2.0250" /> ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Paracittāni jānāmi, satthusāsanakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ dhammadinnā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Dhammadinnātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Sakulātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0339" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0240" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Hitāya sabbasattānaṃ, sukhāya vadataṃ varo;
```

```
Atthāya purisājañño, paṭipanno sadevake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘Yasaggapatto <pb ed="P" n="2.0570" /> sirimā, kittivaṇṇagato jino;
```

```
Pūjito sabbalokassa, disāsabbāsu vissuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘Uttiṇṇavicikiccho so, vītivattakathaṃkatho;
```

```
Sampuṇṇamanasaṅkappo, patto sambodhimuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Anuppannassa maggassa, uppādetā naruttamo;
```

```
Anakkhātañca akkhāsi, asañjātañca sañjanī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘Maggaññū ca maggavidū, maggakkhāyī narāsabho;
```

```
Maggassa kusalo satthā, sārathīnaṃ varuttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘Mahākāruṇiko satthā, dhammaṃ desesi nāyako;
```

```
Nimugge kāmapaṅkamhi, samuddharati pāṇine.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā khattiyanandanā;
```

```
Surūpā sadhanā cāpi, dayitā ca sirīmatī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Ānandassa <pb ed="M" n="2.0251" /> mahārañño, dhītā paramasobhaṇā;
```

```
Vemātā <note>vemātu (sī.)</note> bhaginī cāpi, padumuttaranāmino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Rājakaññāhi <pb ed="T" n="2.0340" /> sahitā, sabbābharaṇabhūsitā;
```

```
Upāgamma mahāvīraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā hi so lokagaru, bhikkhuniṃ dibbacakkhukaṃ;
```

```
Kittayaṃ parisāmajjhe <note>catuparisāya majjhe (syā.)</note>, aggaṭṭhāne ṭhapesi taṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Suṇitvā tamahaṃ haṭṭhā, dānaṃ datvāna satthuno;
```

```
Pūjitvāna ca sambuddhaṃ, dibbacakkhuṃ apatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Tato avoca maṃ satthā, ‘nande lacchasi patthitaṃ;
```

```
Padīpadhammadānānaṃ, phalametaṃ sunicchitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="V" n="2.0241" /> kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Sakulā nāma nāmena <note>sakulāti ca nāmena (syā.)</note>, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="P" n="2.0571" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘Paribbājakinī āsiṃ, tadāhaṃ ekacārinī;
```

```
Bhikkhāya vicaritvāna, alabhiṃ telamattakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘Tena dīpaṃ padīpetvā, upaṭṭhiṃ sabbasaṃvariṃ;
```

```
Cetiyaṃ dvipadaggassa <note>dipadaggassa (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0341" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha yatthūpapajjāmi, tassa kammassa vāhasā;
```

```
Pajjalanti <note>sañjalanti (syā. ka.), saṃcaranti (pī.)</note> mahādīpā, tattha tattha gatāya me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘Tirokuṭṭaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0252" /> tiroselaṃ, samatiggayha pabbataṃ;
```

```
Passāmahaṃ yadicchāmi, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘Visuddhanayanā homi, yasasā ca jalāmahaṃ;
```

```
Saddhāpaññāvatī ceva, dīpadānassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātā vippakule ahaṃ;
```

```
Pahūtadhanadhaññamhi, mudite rājapūjite.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ sabbaṅgasampannā, sabbābharaṇabhūsitā;
```

```
Purappavese sugataṃ, vātapāne ṭhitā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā jalantaṃ yasasā, devamanussasakkataṃ;
```

```
Anubyañjanasampannaṃ, lakkhaṇehi vibhūsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘Udaggacittā sumanā, pabbajjaṃ samarocayiṃ;
```

```
Na cireneva kālena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="V" n="2.0242" /> ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Paracittāni jānāmi, satthusāsanakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, visuddhāsiṃ sunimmalā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘Pariciṇṇo <pb ed="T" n="2.0342" /> mayā satthā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ;
```

```
Ohito garuko bhāro, bhavanetti samūhatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Yassatthāya <pb ed="P" n="2.0572" /> pabbajitā, agārasmānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
So me attho anuppatto, sabbasaṃyojanakkhayo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Tato mahākāruṇiko, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
```

```
Dibbacakkhukānaṃ aggā, sakulāti naruttamo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ sakulā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sakulātheriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Nandātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="M" n="2.0253" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādako viññāpako, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Desanākusalo buddho, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘Anukampako <pb ed="T" n="2.0343" /> kāruṇiko, hitesī sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Sampatte titthiye sabbe, pañcasīle patiṭṭhapi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ nirākulaṃ āsi, suññataṃ titthiyehi ca;
```

```
Vicittaṃ arahantehi, vasībhūtehi tādibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘Ratanānaṭṭhapaññāsaṃ<pb ed="V" n="2.0243" />, uggatova mahāmuni;
```

```
Kañcanagghiyasaṅkāso, bāttiṃsavaralakkhaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘Vassasatasahassāni, āyu vijjati tāvade;
```

```
Tāvatā tiṭṭhamāno so, tāresi janataṃ bahuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātā seṭṭhikule ahuṃ;
```

```
Nānāratanapajjote, mahāsukhasamappitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Upetvā taṃ mahāvīraṃ, assosiṃ dhammadesanaṃ;
```

```
Amataṃ paramassādaṃ, paramatthanivedakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā nimantayitvāna, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Datvā tassa mahādānaṃ, pasannā sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Jhāyinīnaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0573" /> bhikkhunīnaṃ, aggaṭṭhānamapatthayiṃ;
```

```
Nipacca sirasā dhīraṃ, sasaṅghaṃ lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā adantadamako, tilokasaraṇo pabhū;
```

```
Byākāsi narasārathi, ‘lacchase taṃ supatthitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="T" n="2.0344" /> dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Nandāti nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0254" /> sutvā muditā hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Mettacittā paricariṃ, paccayehi vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutā yāmamagaṃ, tatohaṃ tusitaṃ gatā <note>agaṃ (sī. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Tato ca nimmānaratiṃ, vasavattipuraṃ tato <note>gatā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha yatthūpapajjāmi, tassa kammassa vāhasā;
```

```
Tattha tattheva rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cutā manussatte, rājānaṃ cakkavattinaṃ;
```

```
Maṇḍalīnañca rājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Sampattiṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0244" /> anubhotvāna, devesu manujesu ca;
```

```
Sabbattha sukhitā hutvā, nekakappesu saṃsariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, suramme <note>purasmiṃ (syā.)</note> kapilavhaye;
```

```
Rañño suddhodanassāhaṃ, dhītā āsiṃ aninditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Siriyā <note>siriṃva (sī.), raṃsiriva (syā.)</note> rūpiniṃ disvā, nanditaṃ āsi taṃ kulaṃ;
```

```
Tena nandāti me nāmaṃ, sundaraṃ pavaraṃ ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Yuvatīnañca sabbāsaṃ, kalyāṇīti ca vissutā;
```

```
Tasmimpi nagare ramme, ṭhapetvā taṃ yasodharaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Jeṭṭho <pb ed="T" n="2.0345" /> bhātā tilokaggo, pacchimo <note>majjhimo (pī.)</note> arahā tathā;
```

```
Ekākinī gahaṭṭhāhaṃ, mātarā paricoditā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sākiyamhi <pb ed="P" n="2.0574" /> kule jātā, putte buddhānujā tuvaṃ;
```

```
Nandenapi vinā bhūtā, agāre kiṃ nu acchasi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘‘Jarāvasānaṃ yobbaññaṃ, rūpaṃ asucisammataṃ;
```

```
Rogantamapicārogyaṃ, jīvitaṃ maraṇantikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
‘‘‘Idampi te subhaṃ rūpaṃ, sasīkantaṃ manoharaṃ;
```

```
Bhūsanānaṃ alaṅkāraṃ, sirisaṅghāṭasannibhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘‘Puñjitaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0255" /> lokasāraṃva, nayanānaṃ rasāyanaṃ;
```

```
Puññānaṃ kittijananaṃ, ukkākakulanandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘‘Na cireneva kālena, jarā samadhisessati <note>samabhibhossati (sī. syā.), samadhihessati (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Vihāya gehaṃ kāruññe <note>kāruññe (sī. pī.), pārayhiṃ (syā.)</note>, cara dhammamanindite’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvāhaṃ mātu vacanaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Dehena na tu cittena, rūpayobbanalāḷitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
‘‘Mahatā ca payattena, jhānajjhena paraṃ mama;
```

```
Kātuñca vadate mātā, na cāhaṃ tattha ussukā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
‘‘Tato mahākāruṇiko, disvā maṃ kāmalālasaṃ <note>kamalānanaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Nibbindanatthaṃ rūpasmiṃ, mama cakkhupathe jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
‘‘Sakena ānubhāvena, itthiṃ māpesi sobhiniṃ;
```

```
Dassanīyaṃ suruciraṃ, mamatopi surūpiniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
‘‘Tamahaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0346" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0245" /> vimhitā disvā, ativimhitadehiniṃ;
```

```
Cintayiṃ saphalaṃ meti, nettalābhañca mānusaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘Tamahaṃ ehi subhage, yenattho taṃ vadehi me;
```

```
Kulaṃ te nāmagottañca, vada me yadi te piyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘Na <pb ed="P" n="2.0575" /> vañcakālo subhage <note>pañhakālo subhaṇe (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, ucchaṅge maṃ nivāsaya;
```

```
Sīdantīva mamaṅgāni, pasuppaya muhuttakaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘Tato sīsaṃ mamaṅke sā, katvā sayi sulocanā;
```

```
Tassā nalāṭe patitā, luddhā <note>lūtā (syā.)</note> paramadāruṇā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘Saha tassā nipātena, piḷakā upapajjatha;
```

```
Pagghariṃsu pabhinnā ca, kuṇapā pubbalohitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘Pabhinnaṃ vadanañcāpi, kuṇapaṃ pūtigandhanaṃ;
```

```
Uddhumātaṃ vinilañca, pubbañcāpi sarīrakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘Sā paveditasabbaṅgī, nissasantī muhuṃ muhuṃ;
```

```
Vedayantī sakaṃ dukkhaṃ, karuṇaṃ paridevayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dukkhena <pb ed="M" n="2.0256" /> dukkhitā homi, phusayanti ca vedanā;
```

```
Mahādukkhe nimuggamhi, saraṇaṃ hohi me sakhī’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kuhiṃ vadanasobhaṃ te, kuhiṃ te tuṅganāsikā;
```

```
Tambabimbavaroṭṭhaṃ te, vadanaṃ te kuhiṃ gataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kuhiṃ sasīnibhaṃ vaṇṇaṃ, kambugīvā kuhiṃ gatā;
```

```
Doḷālolāva <note>dāmāmālañca (syā.), dololullāva (ka.)</note> te kaṇṇā, vevaṇṇaṃ samupāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘‘Makuḷakhārakākārā <pb ed="T" n="2.0347" /> <note>makulamburūhākārā (sī.), makuḷapadumākārā (syā.)</note>, kalikāva <note>kalasāva (sī. syā. pī.)</note> payodharā;
```

```
Pabhinnā pūtikuṇapā, duṭṭhagandhittamāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vedimajjhāva sussoṇī <note>tanumajjhā puthussoṇī (sī. syā.), vedimajjhā puthussoṇī (pī.)</note>, sūnāva nītakibbisā;
```

```
Jātā amejjhabharitā, aho rūpamasassataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sabbaṃ sarīrasañjātaṃ, pūtigandhaṃ bhayānakaṃ;
```

```
Susānamiva bībhacchaṃ, ramante yattha bālisā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="P" n="2.0576" /> mahākāruṇiko, bhātā me lokanāyako;
```

```
Disvā saṃviggacittaṃ maṃ, imā gāthā abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āturaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0246" /> kuṇapaṃ pūtiṃ, passa nande samussayaṃ;
```

```
Asubhāya cittaṃ bhāvehi, ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ, yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃ;
```

```
Duggandhaṃ pūtikaṃ vāti, bālānaṃ abhinanditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘‘Evametaṃ avekkhantī, rattindivamatanditā;
```

```
Tato sakāya paññāya, abhinibbijjha dakkhasi’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘Tatohaṃ atisaṃviggā, sutvā gāthā subhāsitā;
```

```
Tatraṭṭhitāvahaṃ santī, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha yattha nisinnāhaṃ, sadā jhānaparāyanā;
```

```
Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0348" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0257" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ nandā bhikkhunī janapadakalyāṇī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Nandātheriyāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

#### 6. Soṇātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā seṭṭhikule jātā, sukhitā pūjitā piyā;
```

```
Upetvā taṃ munivaraṃ, assosiṃ madhuraṃ vacaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
‘‘Āraddhavīriyānaggaṃ, vaṇṇesi <note>vaṇṇeti (syā.)</note> bhikkhuniṃ jino;
```

```
Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, kāraṃ katvāna satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
‘‘Abhivādiya sambuddhaṃ, ṭhānaṃ taṃ patthayiṃ tadā;
```

```
Anumodi mahāvīro, ‘sijjhataṃ paṇidhī tava.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="V" n="2.0247" /> kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa <pb ed="T" n="2.0349" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0577" /> dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Soṇāti nāma nāmena, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Mettacittā paricariṃ, paccayehi vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātā seṭṭhikule ahaṃ;
```

```
Sāvatthiyaṃ puravare, iddhe phīte mahaddhane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0258" /> ca yobbanappattā, gantvā patikulaṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Dasa puttāni ajaniṃ, surūpāni visesato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhedhitā ca te sabbe, jananettamanoharā;
```

```
Amittānampi rucitā, mama pageva te piyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
‘‘Tato mayhaṃ akāmāya, dasaputtapurakkhato;
```

```
Pabbajittha sa me bhattā, devadevassa sāsane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
‘‘Tadekikā vicintesiṃ, jīvitenālamatthu me;
```

```
Cattāya patiputtehi, vuḍḍhāya ca varākiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘Ahampi tattha gacchissaṃ, sampatto yattha me pati;
```

```
Evāhaṃ cintayitvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§234.</p>

```
‘‘Tato ca maṃ bhikkhuniyo, ekaṃ bhikkhunupassaye;
```

```
Vihāya gacchumovādaṃ, tāpehi udakaṃ iti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§235.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="T" n="2.0350" /> udakamāhitvā, okiritvāna kumbhiyā;
```

```
Culle ṭhapetvā āsīnā, tato cittaṃ samādahiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§236.</p>

```
‘‘Khandhe aniccato disvā, dukkhato ca anattato;
```

```
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§237.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāgantvā bhikkhuniyo, uṇhodakamapucchisuṃ;
```

```
Tejodhātumadhiṭṭhāya, khippaṃ santāpayiṃ jalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§238.</p>

```
‘‘Vimhitā <pb ed="V" n="2.0248" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0578" /> tā jinavaraṃ, etamatthamasāvayuṃ;
```

```
Taṃ sutvā mudito nātho, imaṃ gāthaṃ abhāsatha.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§239.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo ca vassasataṃ jīve, kusīto hīnavīriyo;
```

```
Ekāhaṃ jīvitaṃ seyyo, vīriyamārabhato daḷhaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§240.</p>

```
‘‘Ārādhito mahāvīro, mayā suppaṭipattiyā;
```

```
Āraddhavīriyānaggaṃ, mamāha sa mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§241.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§242.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§243.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0259" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ soṇā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Soṇātheriyāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Bhaddakāpilānītherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§244.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0351" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū <note>sabbadhammesu cakkhumā (sī. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§245.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhu haṃsavatiyaṃ, videho nāma nāmato <note>nāmako (syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
Seṭṭhī pahūtaratano, tassa jāyā ahosahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§246.</p>

```
‘‘Kadāci so narādiccaṃ, upecca saparijjano;
```

```
Dhammamassosi buddhassa, sabbadukkhabhayappahaṃ <note>dukkhakkhayāvahaṃ (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§247.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvakaṃ dhutavādānaṃ, aggaṃ kittesi nāyako;
```

```
Sutvā sattāhikaṃ dānaṃ, datvā buddhassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§248.</p>

```
‘‘Nipacca sirasā pāde, taṃ ṭhānamabhipatthayiṃ;
```

```
Sa hāsayanto parisaṃ, tadā hi narapuṅgavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§249.</p>

```
‘‘Seṭṭhino anukampāya, imā gāthā abhāsatha;
```

```
‘Lacchase patthitaṃ ṭhānaṃ, nibbuto hohi puttaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§250.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito <pb ed="V" n="2.0249" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0579" /> kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§251.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādo, oraso dhammanimmito;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, hessati satthu sāvako’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§252.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā mudito hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Mettacitto paricari, paccayehi vināyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§253.</p>

```
‘‘Sāsanaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0352" /> jotayitvāna, so madditvā kutitthiye;
```

```
Veneyyaṃ vinayitvā ca, nibbuto so sasāvako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§254.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbute <pb ed="M" n="2.0260" /> tamhi lokagge, pūjanatthāya satthuno;
```

```
Ñātimitte samānetvā, saha tehi akārayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§255.</p>

```
‘‘Sattayojanikaṃ thūpaṃ, ubbiddhaṃ ratanāmayaṃ;
```

```
Jalantaṃ sataraṃsiṃva, sālarājaṃva phullitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§256.</p>

```
‘‘Sattasatasahassāni, pātiyo <note>cātiyo (syā.)</note> tattha kārayi;
```

```
Naḷaggī viya jotantī <note>jotante (syā. pī.)</note>, rataneheva sattahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§257.</p>

```
‘‘Gandhatelena pūretvā, dīpānujjalayī tahiṃ;
```

```
Pūjanatthāya <note>pūjatthāya (sī. ka.)</note> mahesissa, sabbabhūtānukampino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§258.</p>

```
‘‘Sattasatasahassāni, puṇṇakumbhāni kārayi;
```

```
Rataneheva puṇṇāni, pūjanatthāya mahesino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§259.</p>

```
‘‘Majjhe aṭṭhaṭṭhakumbhīnaṃ, ussitā kañcanagghiyo;
```

```
Atirocanti vaṇṇena, saradeva divākaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§260.</p>

```
‘‘Catudvāresu sobhanti, toraṇā ratanāmayā;
```

```
Ussitā phalakā rammā, sobhanti ratanāmayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§261.</p>

```
‘‘Virocanti parikkhittā <note>parikkhāyo (syā.)</note>, avaṭaṃsā sunimmitā;
```

```
Ussitāni paṭākāni, ratanāni virocare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§262.</p>

```
‘‘Surattaṃ sukataṃ cittaṃ, cetiyaṃ ratanāmayaṃ;
```

```
Atirocati vaṇṇena, sasañjhova <note>sasajjhāva (syā. ka.), sasañjāva (pī.)</note> divākaro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§263.</p>

```
‘‘Thūpassa <pb ed="T" n="2.0353" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0580" /> vediyo tisso, haritālena pūrayi;
```

```
Ekaṃ manosilāyekaṃ, añjanena ca ekikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§264.</p>

```
‘‘Pūjaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0250" /> etādisaṃ rammaṃ, kāretvā varavādino;
```

```
Adāsi dānaṃ saṅghassa, yāvajīvaṃ yathābalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§265.</p>

```
‘‘Sahāva seṭṭhinā tena, tāni puññāni sabbaso;
```

```
Yāvajīvaṃ karitvāna, sahāva sugatiṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§266.</p>

```
‘‘Sampattiyonubhotvāna, devatte atha mānuse;
```

```
Chāyā viya sarīrena, saha teneva saṃsariṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§267.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="M" n="2.0261" /> kappe, vipassī nāma nāyako;
```

```
Uppajji cārudassano, sabbadhammavipassako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§268.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāyaṃ bandhumatiyaṃ, brāhmaṇo sādhusammato;
```

```
Aḍḍho santo guṇenāpi <note>satthāgamenāsi (sī.)</note>, dhanena ca suduggato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§269.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāpi tassāhaṃ āsiṃ, brāhmaṇī samacetasā;
```

```
Kadāci so dijavaro, saṅgamesi mahāmuniṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§270.</p>

```
‘‘Nisinnaṃ janakāyamhi, desentaṃ amataṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Sutvā dhammaṃ pamudito, adāsi ekasāṭakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§271.</p>

```
‘‘Gharamekena vatthena, gantvānetaṃ sa mabravi <note>mamabravi (sī. syā. pī.)</note>;
```

```
‘Anumoda mahāpuññaṃ <note>mahāpaññe (sī.), mahāpuññe (syā. ka.)</note>, dinnaṃ buddhassa sāṭakaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§272.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ añjaliṃ katvā, anumodiṃ supīṇitā <note>suviditā (syā.), supītiyā (ka.)</note>;
```

```
‘Sudinno sāṭako sāmi, buddhaseṭṭhassa tādino’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§273.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhito <pb ed="T" n="2.0354" /> sajjito hutvā, saṃsaranto bhavābhave;
```

```
Bārāṇasipure ramme, rājā āsi mahīpati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§274.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="P" n="2.0581" /> tassa mahesīhaṃ, itthigumbassa uttamā;
```

```
Tassāti dayitā <note>tassāvi dutiyikā (syā.)</note> āsiṃ, pubbasnehena bhattuno <note>cuttari (syā. pī. ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§275.</p>

```
‘‘Piṇḍāya vicarante te <note>so (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, aṭṭha paccekanāyake;
```

```
Disvā pamudito hutvā, datvā piṇḍaṃ mahārahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§276.</p>

```
‘‘Puno nimantayitvāna, katvā ratanamaṇḍapaṃ;
```

```
Kammārehi kataṃ pattaṃ <note>kataṃ chattaṃ (sī.), katamaṭṭhaṃ (syā.)</note>, sovaṇṇaṃ vata tattakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§277.</p>

```
‘‘Samānetvāna te sabbe, tesaṃ dānamadāsi so;
```

```
Soṇṇāsane paviṭṭhānaṃ, pasanno sehi pāṇibhi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§278.</p>

```
‘‘Tampi <pb ed="V" n="2.0251" /> dānaṃ sahādāsiṃ, kāsirājenahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Punāhaṃ bārāṇasiyaṃ, jātā kāsikagāmake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§279.</p>

```
‘‘Kuṭumbikakule <pb ed="M" n="2.0262" /> phīte, sukhito so sabhātuko;
```

```
Jeṭṭhassa bhātuno jāyā, ahosiṃ supatibbatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§280.</p>

```
‘‘Paccekabuddhaṃ disvāna, kaniyassa mama bhattuno <note>bhattukaniyaso (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Bhāgannaṃ tassa datvāna, āgate tamhi pāvadiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§281.</p>

```
‘‘Nābhinandittha so dānaṃ, tato tassa adāsahaṃ;
```

```
Ukhā <note>buddhā (syā.)</note> āniya taṃ annaṃ, puno tasseva so adā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§282.</p>

```
‘‘Tadannaṃ chaḍḍayitvāna, duṭṭhā buddhassahaṃ tadā;
```

```
Pattaṃ kalalapuṇṇaṃ taṃ, adāsiṃ tassa tādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§283.</p>

```
‘‘Dāne <pb ed="T" n="2.0355" /> ca gahaṇe ceva, apace padusepi ca;
```

```
Samacittamukhaṃ disvā, tadāhaṃ saṃvijiṃ bhusaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§284.</p>

```
‘‘Puno <pb ed="P" n="2.0582" /> pattaṃ gahetvāna, sodhayitvā sugandhinā;
```

```
Pasannacittā pūretvā, saghataṃ sakkaraṃ adaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§285.</p>

```
‘‘Yattha yatthūpapajjāmi, surūpā homi dānato;
```

```
Buddhassa apakārena, duggandhā vadanena ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§286.</p>

```
‘‘Puna kassapavīrassa, nidhāyantamhi cetiye;
```

```
Sovaṇṇaṃ iṭṭhakaṃ varaṃ, adāsiṃ muditā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§287.</p>

```
‘‘Catujjātena gandhena, nicayitvā tamiṭṭhakaṃ;
```

```
Muttā duggandhadosamhā, sabbaṅgasusamāgatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§288.</p>

```
‘‘Sattapātisahassāni, rataneheva sattahi;
```

```
Kāretvā ghatapūrāni, vaṭṭīni <note>vaṭṭīyo (sī.)</note> ca sahassaso.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§289.</p>

```
‘‘Pakkhipitvā padīpetvā, ṭhapayiṃ sattapantiyo;
```

```
Pūjanatthaṃ lokanāthassa, vippasannena cetasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§290.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāpi tamhi puññamhi, bhāginīyi visesato;
```

```
Puna kāsīsu sañjāto, sumittā iti vissuto.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§291.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāhaṃ bhariyā āsiṃ, sukhitā sajjitā piyā;
```

```
Tadā paccekamunino, adāsiṃ ghanaveṭhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§292.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāpi <pb ed="M" n="2.0263" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0252" /> bhāginī āsiṃ, moditvā dānamuttamaṃ;
```

```
Punāpi kāsiraṭṭhamhi, jāto koliyajātiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§293.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="T" n="2.0356" /> koliyaputtānaṃ, satehi saha pañcahi;
```

```
Pañcapaccekabuddhānaṃ, satāni samupaṭṭhahi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§294.</p>

```
‘‘Temāsaṃ tappayitvāna <note>vāsayitvāna (syā. pī.)</note>, adāsi ca ticīvare <note>ticīvaraṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Jāyā tassa tadā āsiṃ, puññakammapathānugā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§295.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="P" n="2.0583" /> cuto ahu rājā, nando nāma mahāyaso;
```

```
Tassāpi mahesī āsiṃ, sabbakāmasamiddhinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§296.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā rājā bhavitvāna, brahmadatto mahīpati;
```

```
Padumavatīputtānaṃ, paccekamuninaṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§297.</p>

```
‘‘Satāni pañcanūnāni, yāvajīvaṃ upaṭṭhahiṃ;
```

```
Rājuyyāne nivāsetvā, nibbutāni ca pūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§298.</p>

```
‘‘Cetiyāni ca kāretvā, pabbajitvā ubho mayaṃ;
```

```
Bhāvetvā appamaññāyo, brahmalokaṃ agamhase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§299.</p>

```
‘‘Tato cuto mahātitthe, sujāto pipphalāyano;
```

```
Mātā sumanadevīti, kosigotto dijo pitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§300.</p>

```
‘‘Ahaṃ madde janapade, sākalāya puruttame;
```

```
Kappilassa dijassāsiṃ, dhītā mātā sucīmati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§301.</p>

```
‘‘Ghanakañcanabimbena, nimminitvāna maṃ pitā;
```

```
Adā kassapadhīrassa, kāmehi vajjitassamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§302.</p>

```
‘‘Kadāci so kāruṇiko, gantvā kammantapekkhako;
```

```
Kākādikehi khajjante, pāṇe disvāna saṃviji.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§303.</p>

```
‘‘Gharevāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0357" /> tile jāte, disvānātapatāpane;
```

```
Kimi kākehi khajjante, saṃvegamalabhiṃ tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§304.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā so pabbajī dhīro, ahaṃ tamanupabbajiṃ;
```

```
Pañcavassāni nivasiṃ, paribbājavate <note>paribbājapathe (syā. pī.)</note> ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§305.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0264" /> pabbajitā āsi, gotamī jinaposikā;
```

```
Tadāhaṃ tamupagantvā, buddhena anusāsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§306.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="V" n="2.0253" /> cireneva kālena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ;
```

```
Aho kalyāṇamittattaṃ, kassapassa sirīmato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§307.</p>

```
‘‘Suto buddhassa dāyādo, kassapo susamāhito;
```

```
Pubbenivāsaṃ yo vedi, saggāpāyañca passati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§308.</p>

```
‘‘Atho <pb ed="P" n="2.0584" /> jātikkhayaṃ patto, abhiññāvosito muni;
```

```
Etāhi tīhi vijjāhi, tevijjo hoti brāhmaṇo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§309.</p>

```
‘‘Tatheva bhaddakāpilānī <note>bhaddākāpilānī (sī. pī.)</note>, tevijjā maccuhāyinī;
```

```
Dhāreti antimaṃ dehaṃ, jitvā māraṃ savāhanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§310.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā ādīnavaṃ loke, ubho pabbajitā mayaṃ;
```

```
Tyamha khīṇāsavā dantā, sītibhūtāmha nibbutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§311.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§312.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§313.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0358" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ bhaddakāpilānī bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Bhaddakāpilānītheriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Yasodharātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§314.</p>

```
Ekasmiṃ samaye ramme, iddhe rājagahe pure;
```

```
Pabbhāramhi varekamhi, vasante naranāyake.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§315.</p>

```
Vasantiyā tamhi nagare, ramme bhikkhunupassaye;
```

```
Yasodharābhikkhuniyā, evaṃ āsi vitakkitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§316.</p>

```
‘‘Suddhodano mahārājā, gotamī ca pajāpatī;
```

```
Abhiññātā mahātherā, theriyo ca mahiddhikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§317.</p>

```
‘‘Santiṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0265" /> gatāva āsuṃ te, dīpaccīva nirāsavā;
```

```
Lokanāthe dharanteva, ahampi ca sivaṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§318.</p>

```
‘‘Gamissāmīti <pb ed="V" n="2.0254" /> cintetvā, passantī āyumattano;
```

```
Passitvā āyusaṅkhāraṃ, tadaheva khayaṃ gataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§319.</p>

```
‘‘Pattacīvaramādāya, nikkhamitvā sakassamā;
```

```
Purakkhatā bhikkhunībhi, satehi sahassehi sā <note>saha pañcahi (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§320.</p>

```
‘‘Mahiddhikā mahāpaññā, sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkami;
```

```
Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, satthuno cakkalakkhaṇe;
```

```
Nisinnā ekamantamhi, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§321.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhasattativassāhaṃ, pacchimo vattate vayo <note>pacchimā vattayi vayā (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Pabbhāramhi anuppattā, ārocemi mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§322.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paripakko vayo mayhaṃ, parittaṃ mama jīvitaṃ;
```

```
Pahāya vo gamissāmi, kataṃ me saraṇamattano.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§323.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vayamhi pacchime kāle, maraṇaṃ uparuddhati;
```

```
Ajjarattiṃ mahāvīra, pāpuṇissāmi nibbutiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§324.</p>

```
‘‘‘Natthi jāti jarā byādhi, maraṇañca mahāmune;
```

```
Ajarāmaraṇaṃ puraṃ, gamissāmi asaṅkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§325.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yāvatā parisā nāma, samupāsanti satthuno;
```

```
Aparādhamajānantī <note>sace metthi (sī.), pajānantī (ka.)</note>, khamantaṃ sammukhā mune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§326.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṃsaritvā <pb ed="T" n="2.0359" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0585" /> ca saṃsāre, khalitañce mamaṃ tayi;
```

```
Ārocemi mahāvīra, aparādhaṃ khamassu me’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§327.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvāna vacanaṃ tassā, munindo idamabravi;
```

```
‘Kimuttaraṃ te vakkhāmi, nibbānāya vajantiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§328.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iddhiñcāpi nidassehi, mama sāsanakārike;
```

```
Parisānañca sabbāsaṃ, kaṅkhaṃ chindassu yāvatā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§329.</p>

```
‘‘Sutvā taṃ munino vācaṃ, bhikkhunī sā yasodharā;
```

```
Vanditvā munirājaṃ taṃ, idaṃ vacanamabravi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§330.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasodharā <pb ed="M" n="2.0266" /> ahaṃ vīra, agāre te pajāpati;
```

```
Sākiyamhi kule jātā, itthiaṅge patiṭṭhitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§331.</p>

```
‘‘‘Thīnaṃ satasahassānaṃ, navutīnaṃ chaduttari;
```

```
Agāre te ahaṃ vīra, pāmokkhā sabbā issarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§332.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rūpācāraguṇūpetā<pb ed="V" n="2.0255" />, yobbanaṭṭhā piyaṃvadā;
```

```
Sabbā maṃ apacāyanti, devatā viya mānusā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§333.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kaññāsatasahassapamukhā, sakyaputtanivesane;
```

```
Samānasukhadukkhatā, devatā viya nandane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§334.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kāmadhātumatikkamma <note>kāmadhātumatikkantā (sī. syā. pī. ka.)</note>, saṇṭhitā rūpadhātuyā;
```

```
Rūpena sadisā natthi, ṭhapetvā lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§335.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, iddhiṃ dassesi satthuno;
```

```
Nekā nānāvidhākārā, mahāiddhīpi dassayī <note>evamādīni vatvāna, upatitvāna ambaraṃ; iddhī anekā dassesi, buddhānuññā yasodharā; (sī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§336.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cakkavāḷasamaṃ kāyaṃ, sīsaṃ uttarato kuru;
```

```
Ubho pakkhā duve dīpā, jambudīpaṃ sarīrato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§337.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dakkhiṇañca saraṃ piñchaṃ, nānāsākhā tu pattakā;
```

```
Candañca sūriyañcakkhi, merupabbatato sikhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§338.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cakkavālagiriṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0360" /> tuṇḍaṃ, jamburukkhaṃ samūlakaṃ;
```

```
Bījamānā upāgantvā, vandantī lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§339.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthivaṇṇaṃ tathevassaṃ, pabbataṃ jaladhiṃ tathā;
```

```
Candimaṃ sūriyaṃ meruṃ, sakkavaṇṇañca dassayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§340.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasodharā <pb ed="P" n="2.0586" /> ahaṃ vīra, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma;
```

```
Sahassalokadhātūnaṃ, phullapadmena chādayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§341.</p>

```
‘‘‘Brahmavaṇṇañca māpetvā, dhammaṃ desesi suññataṃ;
```

```
Yasodharā ahaṃ vīra, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§342.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§343.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0267" /> jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§344.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ mayhaṃ mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§345.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pubbānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ, saṅgamaṃ te nidassitaṃ <note>sudassitaṃ (syā. pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§346.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0256" /> mayhaṃ pūritaṃ kammaṃ, kusalaṃ sarase mune;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, puññaṃ upacitaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§347.</p>

```
‘‘‘Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā, vārayitvā anācaraṃ;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, sañcattaṃ jīvitaṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§348.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nekakoṭisahassāni<pb ed="T" n="2.0361" />, bhariyatthāyadāsi maṃ;
```

```
Na tattha vimanā homi, tuyhatthāya mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§349.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nekakoṭisahassāni, upakārāyadāsi maṃ;
```

```
Na tattha vimanā homi, tuyhatthāya mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§350.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nekakoṭisahassāni, bhojanatthāyadāsi maṃ;
```

```
Na tattha vimanā homi, tuyhatthāya mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§351.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nekakoṭisahassāni, jīvitāni pariccajiṃ;
```

```
Bhayamokkhaṃ karissanti, dadāmi mama jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§352.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṅgagate <note>aṅge evaṃ (ka.)</note> alaṅkāre, vatthe nānāvidhe bahū;
```

```
Itthimaṇḍe na gūhāmi, tuyhatthāya mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§353.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhanadhaññapariccāgaṃ<pb ed="P" n="2.0587" />, gāmāni nigamāni ca;
```

```
Khettaṃ puttā ca dhītā ca, pariccattā mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§354.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthī assā gavā cāpi, dāsiyo paricārikā;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, pariccattā asaṅkhiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§355.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yaṃ mayhaṃ paṭimantesi <note>patimantesi (sī.)</note>, dānaṃ dassāmi yācake;
```

```
Vimanaṃ me na passāmi, dadato dānamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§356.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nānāvidhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0268" /> bahuṃ dukkhaṃ, saṃsāre ca bahubbidhe;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, anubhuttaṃ asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§357.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sukhappattānumodāmi, na ca dukkhesu dummanā;
```

```
Sabbattha tulitā homi, tuyhatthāya mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§358.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anumaggena <pb ed="T" n="2.0362" /> sambuddho, yaṃ dhammaṃ abhinīhari;
```

```
Anubhotvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ, patto bodhiṃ mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§359.</p>

```
‘‘‘Brahmadevañca sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Aññesaṃ lokanāthānaṃ, saṅgamaṃ te bahuṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§360.</p>

```
‘‘‘Adhikāraṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0257" /> bahuṃ mayhaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmuni;
```

```
Gavesato buddhadhamme, ahaṃ te paricārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§361.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappe ca satasahasse, caturo ca asaṅkhiye;
```

```
Dīpaṅkaro mahāvīro, uppajji lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§362.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paccantadesavisaye, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Tassa āgamanaṃ maggaṃ, sodhenti tuṭṭhamānasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§363.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tena kālena so āsi, sumedho nāma brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Maggañca paṭiyādesi, āyato <note>āyataṃ (sī.)</note> sabbadassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§364.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tena kālenahaṃ āsiṃ, kaññā brāhmaṇasambhavā;
```

```
Sumittānāma nāmena, upagacchiṃ samāgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§365.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭha uppalahatthāni, pūjanatthāya satthuno;
```

```
Ādāya janasaṃmajjhe, addasaṃ isi muggataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§366.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cirānugataṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0588" /> dayitaṃ <note>cirānupari āsīnaṃ (sī.)</note>, atikkantaṃ manoharaṃ;
```

```
Disvā tadā amaññissaṃ, saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§367.</p>

```
‘‘‘Parakkamaṃ taṃ saphalaṃ, addasaṃ isino tadā;
```

```
Pubbakammena sambuddhe, cittañcāpi pasīdi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§368.</p>

```
‘‘‘Bhiyyo <pb ed="T" n="2.0363" /> cittaṃ pasādesiṃ, ise uggatamānase;
```

```
Deyyaṃ aññaṃ na passāmi, demi pupphāni te isi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§369.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pañcahatthā <pb ed="M" n="2.0269" /> tava hontu, tayo hontu mamaṃ ise;
```

```
Tena saddhiṃ samā hontu, bodhatthāya tavaṃ ise’.
```

Catutthaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

<p rend="hangnum">§370.</p>

```
‘‘Isi gahetvā pupphāni, āgacchantaṃ mahāyasaṃ;
```

```
Pūjesi janasaṃmajjhe, bodhatthāya mahāisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§371.</p>

```
‘‘Passitvā janasaṃmajjhe, dīpaṅkaro mahāmuni;
```

```
Viyākāsi mahāvīro, isi muggatamānasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§372.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, dīpaṅkaro mahāmuni;
```

```
Mama kammaṃ viyākāsi, ujubhāvaṃ mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§373.</p>

```
‘‘‘Samacittā <pb ed="V" n="2.0258" /> samakammā, samakārī bhavissati;
```

```
Piyā hessati kammena, tuyhatthāya mahāisi <note>mahāise (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§374.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sudassanā supiyā ca, manāpā piyavādinī;
```

```
Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, viharissati iddhikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§375.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yathāpi bhaṇḍasāmuggaṃ, anurakkhati sāmino;
```

```
Evaṃ kusaladhammānaṃ, anurakkhissate ayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§376.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa te <note>tassa taṃ (syā.)</note> anukampantī, pūrayissati pāramī;
```

```
Sīhova pañjaraṃ bhetvā <note>hitvā (syā.), hetvā (pī.)</note>, pāpuṇissati bodhiyaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§377.</p>

```
‘‘Aparimeyye <pb ed="T" n="2.0364" /> ito kappe, yaṃ maṃ buddho viyākarī;
```

```
Taṃ vācaṃ anumodentī, evaṃkārī bhaviṃ ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§378.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa <pb ed="P" n="2.0589" /> kammassa sukatassa, tattha cittaṃ pasādayiṃ;
```

```
Devamanussakaṃ yoniṃ, anubhotvā asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§379.</p>

```
‘‘Sukhadukkhenubhotvāhaṃ, devesu mānusesu ca;
```

```
Pacchime bhave sampatte, ajāyiṃ sākiye kule.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§380.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpavatī bhogavatī, yasasīlavatī tato;
```

```
Sabbaṅgasampadā homi, kulesu abhisakkatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§381.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0270" /> silokaṃ sakkāraṃ, lokadhammasamāgamaṃ;
```

```
Cittañca dukkhitaṃ natthi, vasāmi akutobhayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§382.</p>

```
‘‘Vuttañhetaṃ bhagavatā, rañño antepure tadā;
```

```
Khattiyānaṃ pure vīra, upakārañca niddisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§383.</p>

```
‘‘Upakārā ca yā nārī, yā ca nārī sukhe dukhe;
```

```
Atthakkhāyī ca yā nārī, yā ca nārīnukampikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§384.</p>

```
‘‘Pañcakoṭisatā buddhā, navakoṭisatāni ca;
```

```
Etesaṃ devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§385.</p>

```
‘‘Adhikāraṃ mahā <note>sadā (pī.) evamuparipi</note> mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me;
```

```
Ekādasakoṭisatā, buddhā dvādasa koṭiyo <note>honti lokagganāyakā (sī. syā.), paṇṇākoṭisatāni ca (pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§386.</p>

```
‘‘Etesaṃ devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§387.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vīsakoṭisatā <pb ed="T" n="2.0365" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0259" /> buddhā, tiṃsakoṭisatāni ca;
```

```
Etesaṃ devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§388.</p>

```
‘‘‘Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me;
```

```
Cattālīsakoṭisatā, paññāsa koṭisatāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§389.</p>

```
‘‘‘Etesaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0590" /> devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§390.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṭṭhikoṭisatā buddhā, sattatikoṭisatāni ca;
```

```
Etesaṃ devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§391.</p>

```
‘‘‘Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me;
```

```
Asītikoṭisatā buddhā, navutikoṭisatāni ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§392.</p>

```
‘‘‘Etesaṃ devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§393.</p>

```
‘‘‘Koṭisatasahassāni, honti lokagganāyakā;
```

```
Etesaṃ devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§394.</p>

```
‘‘‘Adhikāraṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0271" /> mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me;
```

```
Navakoṭisahassāni, apare lokanāyakā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§395.</p>

```
‘‘‘Etesaṃ devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§396.</p>

```
‘‘‘Koṭisatasahassāni, pañcāsītimahesinaṃ;
```

```
Pañcāsītikoṭisatā, sattatiṃsā ca koṭiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§397.</p>

```
‘‘‘Etesaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0366" /> devadevānaṃ, mahādānaṃ pavattayiṃ;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§398.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paccekabuddhā vītarāgā <note>dhutarāgā (pī. ka.)</note>, aṭṭhaṭṭhamakakoṭiyo <note>aṭṭhamattaka… (sī.), aṭṭhamatthaka… (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§399.</p>

```
‘‘‘Khīṇāsavā vītamalā, asaṅkhiyā buddhasāvakā;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ mahā mayhaṃ, dhammarāja suṇohi me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§400.</p>

```
‘‘‘Evaṃ dhamme suciṇṇānaṃ, sadā dhammassa cārinaṃ;
```

```
Dhammacārī sukhaṃ seti, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§401.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhammaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0260" /> care sucaritaṃ, na naṃ duccaritaṃ care;
```

```
Dhammacārī sukhaṃ seti, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§402.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nibbinditvāna saṃsāre, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Sahassaparivārena, pabbajitvā akiñcanā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§403.</p>

```
‘‘‘Agāraṃ vijahitvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Aḍḍhamāse asampatte, catusaccamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§404.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Upanenti bahū janā, sāgareyeva ūmiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§405.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§406.</p>

```
‘‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§407.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0367" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§408.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ, sampattī ca bahubbidhā;
```

```
Visuddhibhāvaṃ sampattā, labhāmi sabbasampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§409.</p>

```
‘‘Yā <pb ed="M" n="2.0272" /> dadāti sakattānaṃ, puññatthāya mahesino;
```

```
Sahāyasampadā honti, nibbānapadamasaṅkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§410.</p>

```
‘‘Parikkhīṇaṃ atītañca, paccuppannaṃ anāgataṃ;
```

```
Sabbakammaṃ mamaṃ khīṇaṃ, pāde vandāmi cakkhuma’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharā bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Yasodharātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Yasodharāpamukhadasabhikkhunīsahassaapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§411.</p>

```
‘‘Kappe <pb ed="P" n="2.0591" /> ca satasahasse, caturo ca asaṅkhiye;
```

```
Dīpaṅkaro nāma jino, uppajji lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§412.</p>

```
‘‘Dīpaṅkaro mahāvīro, viyākāsi vināyako;
```

```
Sumedhañca sumittañca, samānasukhadukkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§413.</p>

```
‘‘Sadevakañca <pb ed="V" n="2.0261" /> passanto, vicaranto sadevakaṃ;
```

```
Tesaṃ pakittane amhe, upagamma samāgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§414.</p>

```
‘‘Amhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0368" /> sabbapati hohi <note>sabbā patī honti (pī.)</note>, anāgatasamāgame;
```

```
Sabbāva tuyhaṃ bhariyā, manāpā piyavādikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§415.</p>

```
‘‘Dānaṃ sīlamayaṃ sabbaṃ, bhāvanā ca subhāvitā;
```

```
Dīgharattañca no <note>dīgharattamidaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> sabbaṃ, pariccattaṃ mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§416.</p>

```
‘‘Gandhaṃ vilepanaṃ mālaṃ, dīpañca ratanāmayaṃ;
```

```
Yaṃkiñci patthitaṃ sabbaṃ, pariccattaṃ mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§417.</p>

```
‘‘Aññaṃ vāpi kataṃ kammaṃ, paribhogañca mānusaṃ;
```

```
Dīgharattañhi no sabbaṃ, pariccattaṃ mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§418.</p>

```
‘‘Anekajātisaṃsāraṃ, bahuṃ puññampi no kataṃ;
```

```
Issaramanubhotvāna, saṃsaritvā bhavābhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§419.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="M" n="2.0273" /> bhave sampatte, sakyaputtanivesane;
```

```
Nānākulūpapannāyo, accharā kāmavaṇṇinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§420.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhaggena yasaṃ pattā, pūjitā sabbasakkatā;
```

```
Lābhiyo annapānānaṃ, sadā sammānitā mayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§421.</p>

```
‘‘Agāraṃ pajahitvāna, pabbajimhanagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Aḍḍhamāse asampatte, sabbā pattāmha nibbutiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§422.</p>

```
‘‘Lābhiyo annapānānaṃ, vatthasenāsanāni ca;
```

```
Upenti paccayā sabbe, sadā sakkatapūjitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§423.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0592" /> jhāpitā amhaṃ…pe… viharāma anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§424.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0369" /> vata no āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§425.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharāpamukhāni dasabhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Yasodharāpamukhadasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Yasodharāpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassaapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§426.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārasasahassāni<pb ed="V" n="2.0262" />, bhikkhunī sakyasambhavā;
```

```
Yasodharāpamukhāni, sambuddhaṃ upasaṅkamuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§427.</p>

```
‘‘Aṭṭhārasasahassāni, sabbā honti mahiddhikā;
```

```
Vandantī munino pāde, ārocenti yathābalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§428.</p>

```
‘‘‘Jāti khīṇā jarā byādhi, maraṇañca mahāmuni;
```

```
Anāsavaṃ padaṃ santaṃ, amataṃ yāma nāyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§429.</p>

```
‘‘‘Khalitañce pure atthi, sabbāsampi mahāmuni;
```

```
Aparādhamajānantī, khama amhaṃ vināyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§430.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iddhiñcāpi nidassetha, mama sāsanakārikā;
```

```
Parisānañca sabbāsaṃ, kaṅkhaṃ chindatha yāvatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§431.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasodharā <pb ed="M" n="2.0274" /> mahāvīra, manāpā piyadassanā;
```

```
Sabbā <pb ed="T" n="2.0370" /> tuyhaṃ mahāvīra, agārasmiṃ pajāpati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§432.</p>

```
‘‘‘Thīnaṃ satasahassānaṃ, navutīnaṃ chaduttari;
```

```
Agāre te mayaṃ vīra, pāmokkhā sabbā issarā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§433.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rūpācāraguṇūpetā, yobbanaṭṭhā piyaṃvadā;
```

```
Sabbā no apacāyanti, devatā viya mānusā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§434.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṭṭhārasasahassāni, sabbā sākiyasambhavā;
```

```
Yasodharāsahassāni, pāmokkhā issarā tadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§435.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kāmadhātumatikkamma<pb ed="P" n="2.0593" />, saṇṭhitā rūpadhātuyā;
```

```
Rūpena sadisā natthi, sahassānaṃ mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§436.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sambuddhaṃ abhivādetvā, iddhiṃ dassaṃsu satthuno;
```

```
