```
Nekā nānāvidhākārā, mahāiddhīpi dassayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§437.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cakkavāḷasamaṃ kāyaṃ, sīsaṃ uttarato kuru;
```

```
Ubho pakkhā duve dīpā, jambudīpaṃ sarīrato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§438.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dakkhiṇañca saraṃ piñchaṃ, nānāsākhā tu pattakā;
```

```
Candañca sūriyañcakkhi, merupabbatato sikhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§439.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cakkavāḷagiriṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0263" /> tuṇḍaṃ, jamburukkhaṃ samūlakaṃ;
```

```
Bījamānā upāgantvā, vandantī lokanāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§440.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthivaṇṇaṃ tathevassaṃ, pabbataṃ jaladhiṃ tathā;
```

```
Candañca sūriyaṃ meruṃ, sakkavaṇṇañca dassayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§441.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yasodharā <pb ed="T" n="2.0371" /> mayaṃ vīra, pāde vandāma cakkhuma;
```

```
Tava cirapabhāvena, nipphannā naranāyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§442.</p>

```
‘‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homa, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homa mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§443.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāma, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§444.</p>

```
‘‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ amhaṃ mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§445.</p>

```
‘‘‘Pubbānaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0275" /> lokanāthānaṃ, saṅgamaṃ no nidassitaṃ;
```

```
Adhikārā bahū amhaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§446.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yaṃ amhaṃ pūritaṃ kammaṃ, kusalaṃ sarase mune;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, puññānupacitāni no.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§447.</p>

```
‘‘‘Abhabbaṭṭhāne vajjetvā, vārayimha anācaraṃ;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, cattāni jīvitāni no <note>sañcattaṃ jīvitampi no (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§448.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nekakoṭisahassāni<pb ed="P" n="2.0594" />, bhariyatthāyadāsi no;
```

```
Na tattha vimanā homa, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§449.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nekakoṭisahassāni, upakārāyadāsi no;
```

```
Na tattha vimanā homa, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§450.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nekakoṭisahassāni, bhojanatthāyadāsi no;
```

```
Na tattha vimanā homa, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§451.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nekakoṭisahassāni<pb ed="T" n="2.0372" />, jīvitāni cajimhase <note>cajimha no (pī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Bhayamokkhaṃ karissāma, jīvitāni cajimhase.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§452.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aṅgagate alaṅkāre, vatthe nānāvidhe bahū;
```

```
Itthibhaṇḍe na gūhāma, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§453.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhanadhaññapariccāgaṃ<pb ed="V" n="2.0264" />, gāmāni nigamāni ca;
```

```
Khettaṃ puttā ca dhītā ca, pariccattā mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§454.</p>

```
‘‘‘Hatthī assā gavā cāpi, dāsiyo paricārikā;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, pariccattaṃ asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§455.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yaṃ amhe paṭimantesi, dānaṃ dassāma yācake;
```

```
Vimanaṃ no na passāma, dadato dānamuttamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§456.</p>

```
‘‘‘Nānāvidhaṃ bahuṃ dukkhaṃ, saṃsāre ca bahubbidhe;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, anubhuttaṃ asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§457.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sukhappattānumodāma, na ca dukkhesu dummanā;
```

```
Sabbattha tulitā homa, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§458.</p>

```
‘‘‘Anumaggena <pb ed="M" n="2.0276" /> sambuddho, yaṃ dhammaṃ abhinīhari;
```

```
Anubhotvā sukhaṃ dukkhaṃ, patto bodhiṃ mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§459.</p>

```
‘‘‘Brahmadevañca sambuddhaṃ, gotamaṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Aññesaṃ lokanāthānaṃ, saṅgamaṃ tehi no bahū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§460.</p>

```
‘‘‘Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ amhe, tuyhatthāya mahāmune;
```

```
Gavesato buddhadhamme, mayaṃ te paricārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§461.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kappe <pb ed="T" n="2.0373" /> ca satasahasse, caturo ca asaṅkhiye;
```

```
Dīpaṅkaro mahāvīro, uppajji lokanāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§462.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paccantadesavisaye, nimantetvā tathāgataṃ;
```

```
Tassa āgamanaṃ maggaṃ, sodhenti tuṭṭhamānasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§463.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tena <pb ed="P" n="2.0595" /> kālena so āsi, sumedho nāma brāhmaṇo;
```

```
Maggañca paṭiyādesi, āyato sabbadassino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§464.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tena kālena ahumha, sabbā brāhmaṇasambhavā;
```

```
Thalūdajāni pupphāni, āharimha samāgamaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§465.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tasmiṃ so samaye buddho, dīpaṅkaro mahāyaso;
```

```
Viyākāsi mahāvīro, isimuggatamānasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§466.</p>

```
‘‘‘Calatī ravatī puthavī, saṅkampati sadevake;
```

```
Tassa kammaṃ pakittente, isimuggatamānasaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§467.</p>

```
‘‘‘Devakaññā <pb ed="V" n="2.0265" /> manussā ca, mayañcāpi sadevakā;
```

```
Nānāpūjanīyaṃ bhaṇḍaṃ, pūjayitvāna patthayuṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§468.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tesaṃ buddho viyākāsi, jotidīpa sanāmako;
```

```
Ajja ye patthitā atthi, te bhavissanti sammukhā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§469.</p>

```
‘‘‘Aparimeyye ito kappe, yaṃ no buddho viyākari;
```

```
Taṃ vācamanumodentā, evaṃkārī ahumha no.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§470.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa kammassa sukatassa, tassa cittaṃ pasādayuṃ;
```

```
Devamānusikaṃ yoniṃ, anubhotvā asaṅkhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§471.</p>

```
‘‘‘Sukhadukkhenubhotvāna<pb ed="T" n="2.0374" />, devesu mānusesu ca;
```

```
Pacchime bhave sampatte, jātāmha sākiye kule.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§472.</p>

```
‘‘‘Rūpavatī <pb ed="M" n="2.0277" /> bhogavatī, yasasīlavatī tato;
```

```
Sabbaṅgasampadā homa, kulesu abhisakkatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§473.</p>

```
‘‘‘Lābhaṃ silokaṃ sakkāraṃ, lokadhammasamāgamaṃ;
```

```
Cittañca dukkhitaṃ natthi, vasāma akutobhayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§474.</p>

```
‘‘‘Vuttañhetaṃ bhagavatā, rañño antepure tadā;
```

```
Khattiyānaṃ pure vīra <note>tāsaṃ (syā.)</note>, upakārañca niddisi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§475.</p>

```
‘‘‘Upakārā ca yā nārī, yā ca nārī sukhe dukhe;
```

```
Atthakkhāyī ca yā nārī, yā ca nārīnukampikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§476.</p>

```
‘‘‘Dhammaṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0596" /> care sucaritaṃ, na naṃ duccaritaṃ care;
```

```
Dhammacārī sukhaṃ seti, asmiṃ loke paramhi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§477.</p>

```
‘‘‘Agāraṃ vijahitvāna, pabbajimhanagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Aḍḍhamāse asampatte, catusaccaṃ phusimha no.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§478.</p>

```
‘‘‘Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Upanenti bahū amhe, sāgarasseva ūmiyo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§479.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā amhaṃ <note>mayhaṃ (syā.), amhākaṃ (ka.)</note>, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāma anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§480.</p>

```
‘‘‘Svāgataṃ vata no āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§481.</p>

```
‘‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0375" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0266" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§482.</p>

```
‘‘Evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ dukkhaṃ, sampattī ca bahubbidhā;
```

```
Visuddhabhāvaṃ sampattā, labhāma sabbasampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§483.</p>

```
‘‘Yā dadanti sakattānaṃ, puññatthāya mahesino;
```

```
Sahāyasampadā honti, nibbānapadamasaṅkhataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§484.</p>

```
‘‘Parikkhīṇaṃ atītañca, paccuppannaṃ anāgataṃ;
```

```
Sabbakammampi no khīṇaṃ, pāde vandāma cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§485.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbānāya <pb ed="M" n="2.0278" /> vadantīnaṃ, kiṃ vo vakkhāma uttari;
```

```
Santasaṅkhatadosañhi, pappotha <note>santasaṅkhatadoso yo, pajjotaṃ (syā. pī. ka.)</note> amataṃ padaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasodharāpamukhāni aṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Yasodharāpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Kuṇḍalakesīvaggo tatiyo.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Kuṇḍalā gotamī ceva, dhammadinnā ca sakulā;
```

```
Varanandā ca soṇā ca, kāpilānī yasodharā.
```

```
Dasasahassabhikkhunī, aṭṭhārasasahassakā;
```

```
Gāthāsatāni cattāri, cha ca sattatimeva ca <note>aṭṭhasattatimeva ca (syā.)</note>.
```

### 4. Khattiyāvaggo

#### 1. Yasavatīpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassaapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§1.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavā <pb ed="T" n="2.0376" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0279" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0267" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0597" /> sabbe parikkhīṇā, bhavā santi vimocitā;
```

```
Sabbāsavā ca no natthi, ārocema mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§2.</p>

```
‘‘Purimaṃ kusalaṃ kammaṃ <note>parikammañca kusalaṃ (syā.)</note>, yaṃ kiñci sādhupatthitaṃ;
```

```
Paribhogamayaṃ dinnaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§3.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhapaccekabuddhānaṃ, sāvakānañca patthitaṃ <note>buddhānaṃ sāvakānañca (sī. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Paribhogamayaṃ dinnaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§4.</p>

```
‘‘Uccanīcamayaṃ kammaṃ, bhikkhūnaṃ sādhupatthitaṃ;
```

```
Uccākulaparikammaṃ, katametaṃ mahāmune <note>katamhehi mahāmune (syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§5.</p>

```
‘‘Teneva sukkamūlena, coditā kammasampadā;
```

```
Mānusikamatikkantā, jāyiṃsu khattiye kule.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§6.</p>

```
‘‘Uppatte ca kate kamme, jātiyā vāpi ekato;
```

```
Pacchime ekato jātā, khattiyā kulasambhavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§7.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpavatī bhogavatī, lābhasakkārapūjitā;
```

```
Antepure mahāvīra, devānaṃ viya nandane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§8.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbinditvā agāramhā, pabbajimhanagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Katipāhaṃ upādāya, sabbā pattāmha nibbutiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§9.</p>

```
‘‘Cīvaraṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0377" /> piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Upanenti bahū amhe, sadā sakkatapūjitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§10.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā amhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāma anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§11.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata no āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§12.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0280" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0268" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ yasavatīpamukhāni khattiyakaññābhikkhuniyo aṭṭhārasasahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Yasavatīpamukhaaṭṭhārasabhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ paṭhamaṃ.

#### 2. Caturāsītibhikkhunīsahassaapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§13.</p>

```
‘‘Cullāsītisahassāni<pb ed="P" n="2.0598" />, brāhmaññakulasambhavā <note>brāhmaṇakulasambhavā (syā. ka.)</note>;
```

```
Sukhumālahatthapādā, pure tuyhaṃ mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§14.</p>

```
‘‘Vessasuddakule jātā, devā nāgā ca kinnarā;
```

```
Cātuddīpā bahū kaññā, pure tuyhaṃ mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§15.</p>

```
‘‘Kāci pabbajitā atthi, sabbadassāvino <note>saccadassāvino (sī. pī.)</note> hū;
```

```
Devā ca kinnarā nāgā, phusissanti anāgate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§16.</p>

```
‘‘Anubhotvā yasaṃ sabbaṃ, patvāna sabbasampadā;
```

```
Tumhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0378" /> <note>tvayi (sī. pī.)</note> pasādaṃ paṭiladdhā, bujjhissanti anāgate.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§17.</p>

```
‘‘Amhe brāhmaṇadhītā tu, brāhmaññakulasambhavā;
```

```
Pekkhato no <note>lakkhaṇā ca (syā.)</note> mahāvīra, pāde vandāma cakkhuma.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§18.</p>

```
‘‘Upahatā bhavā sabbe, mūlataṇhā samūhatā;
```

```
Samucchinnā anusayā, puññasaṅkhāradālitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§19.</p>

```
‘‘Samādhigocarā sabbā, samāpattivasī katā;
```

```
Jhānena dhammaratiyā, viharissāma no sadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§20.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavanetti avijjā ca, saṅkhārāpi ca khepitā;
```

```
Sududdasaṃ padaṃ gantvā, anujānātha <note>anujānimha (syā. pī. ka.)</note> nāyaka.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§21.</p>

```
‘‘Upakārā mamaṃ tumhe, dīgharattaṃ katāvino;
```

```
Catunnaṃ saṃsayaṃ chetvā, sabbā gacchantu nibbutiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§22.</p>

```
‘‘Vanditvā <pb ed="M" n="2.0281" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0269" /> munino pāde, katvā iddhivikubbanaṃ;
```

```
Kāci dassenti ālokaṃ, andhakāramathāparā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§23.</p>

```
‘‘Dassenti candasūriye, sāgarañca samacchakaṃ;
```

```
Sineruṃ paribhaṇḍañca, dassenti pārichattakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§24.</p>

```
‘‘Tāvatiṃsañca bhavanaṃ, yāmaṃ dassenti iddhiyā;
```

```
Tusitaṃ nimmite deve, vasavattī mahissare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§25.</p>

```
‘‘Brahmāno kāci dassenti, caṅkamañca mahārahaṃ;
```

```
Brahmavaṇṇañca māpetvā, dhammaṃ desenti suññataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§26.</p>

```
‘‘Nānāvikubbanaṃ katvā, iddhiṃ dassiya satthuno;
```

```
Dassayiṃsu <pb ed="T" n="2.0379" /> balaṃ sabbā, pāde vandiṃsu satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§27.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="P" n="2.0599" /> ca vasī homa, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homa mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§28.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāma, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§29.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ amhaṃ mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§30.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbānaṃ lokanāthānaṃ, saṅgamaṃ no nidassitaṃ;
```

```
Adhikāraṃ bahuṃ amhaṃ, tuyhatthāya mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§31.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ amhehi kataṃ kammaṃ, kusalaṃ sara taṃ mune;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, puññānupacitāni no.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§32.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, padumuttaro mahāmuni;
```

```
Puraṃ haṃsavatī nāma, sambuddhassa kulāsayaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§33.</p>

```
‘‘Dvārena haṃsavatiyā, gaṅgā sandati sabbadā;
```

```
Ubbaḷhā nadiyā bhikkhū, gamanaṃ na labhanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§34.</p>

```
‘‘Divasaṃ dve tayo ceva, sattāhaṃ māsikaṃ tato;
```

```
Catumāsampi sampuṇṇaṃ, gamanaṃ na labhanti te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§35.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā ahu sattasāro, jaṭilo nāma raṭṭhiko;
```

```
Oruddhe <note>oratīre (syā.)</note> bhikkhavo disvā, setuṃ gaṅgāya kārayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§36.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="T" n="2.0380" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0282" /><pb ed="V" n="2.0270" /> satasahassehi, setuṃ gaṅgāya kārayi;
```

```
Saṅghassa orime tīre, vihārañca akārayi.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§37.</p>

```
‘‘Itthiyo purisā ceva, uccanīcakulāni ca;
```

```
Tassa setuṃ vihārañca <note>tesu setuvihāresu (sī.), tassa setū vihāre ca (pī.)</note>, samabhāgaṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§38.</p>

```
‘‘Amhe aññe ca mānujā, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, nagare janapadesu ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§39.</p>

```
‘‘Itthī pumā kumārā ca, bahū ceva kumārikā;
```

```
Setuno ca vihārassa, vālukā ākiriṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§40.</p>

```
‘‘Vīthiṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0600" /> sammajjanaṃ katvā, kadalīpuṇṇaghaṭe dhaje;
```

```
Dhūpaṃ cuṇṇañca mālañca, kāraṃ katvāna satthuno.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§41.</p>

```
‘‘Setuvihāre kāretvā, nimantetvā vināyakaṃ;
```

```
Mahādānaṃ daditvāna, sambodhiṃ abhipatthayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§42.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro mahāvīro, tārako sabbapāṇinaṃ;
```

```
Anumodanīyaṃkāsi, jaṭilassa mahāmuni <note>katvā, viyākāsi mahāmuni (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§43.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassātikkante, kappo hessati bhaddako;
```

```
Bhavābhavenubhotvāna, pāpuṇissati bodhiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§44.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kāci hatthaparikammaṃ, katāvī naranāriyo;
```

```
Anāgatamhi addhāne, sabbā hessanti sammukhā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§45.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammavipākena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Uppannā devabhavanaṃ, tuyhaṃ tā paricārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§46.</p>

```
‘‘Dibbasukhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0381" /> asaṅkhiyaṃ, mānusañca asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Tuyhaṃ te paricārema, saṃsarimha bhavābhave.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§47.</p>

```
‘‘Satasahassito kappe, sukataṃ kammasampadaṃ;
```

```
Sukhumālī manussānaṃ, atho devapure vare.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§48.</p>

```
‘‘Rūpabhogayase ceva, atho kittiñca sakkataṃ <note>kittisukhaṃ piyaṃ (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Labhāma satataṃ sabbaṃ, sukataṃ kammasampadaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§49.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="M" n="2.0283" /> bhave sampatte, jātāmha brāhmaṇe kule;
```

```
Sukhumālahatthapādā, sakyaputtanivesane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§50.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbakālampi <pb ed="V" n="2.0271" /> pathaviṃ, na passāma na laṅkataṃ;
```

```
Cikkhallabhūmimasuciṃ <note>cikkhallaṃ bhūmiṃ gamanaṃ (syā.)</note>, na passāma mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§51.</p>

```
‘‘Agāraṃ vasante amhe, sakkāraṃ sabbakālikaṃ;
```

```
Upanenti sadā sabbaṃ, pubbakammaphalena no <note>pubbakammaphalaṃ tato (sī. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§52.</p>

```
‘‘Agāraṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0601" /> pajahitvāna, pabbajitvānagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Saṃsārapathanitthiṇṇā, vītarāgā bhavāmase <note>natthi dāni punabbhavo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§53.</p>

```
‘‘Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Upanenti sadā amhe, sahassāni tato tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§54.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā amhaṃ…pe… viharāma anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§55.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0382" /> vata no āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§56.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ caturāsītibrāhmaṇakaññābhikkhunīsahassāni bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Caturāsītibhikkhunīsahassāpadānaṃ dutiyaṃ.

#### 3. Uppaladāyikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§57.</p>

```
‘‘Nagare aruṇavatiyā, aruṇo nāma khattiyo;
```

```
Tassa rañño ahuṃ bhariyā, ekajjhaṃ cārayāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§58.</p>

```
‘‘Rahogatā nisīditvā, evaṃ cintesahaṃ tadā;
```

```
‘Kusalaṃ me kataṃ natthi, ādāya gamiyaṃ mama.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§59.</p>

```
‘‘‘Mahābhitāpaṃ kaṭukaṃ, ghorarūpaṃ sudāruṇaṃ;
```

```
Nirayaṃ nūna gacchāmi, ettha me natthi saṃsayo’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§60.</p>

```
‘‘Evāhaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0284" /> cintayitvāna, pahaṃsetvāna mānasaṃ;
```

```
Rājānaṃ upagantvāna, idaṃ vacanamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§61.</p>

```
‘‘‘Itthī nāma mayaṃ deva, purisānittarā ahu <note>purisānugatā sadā (sī.), purisā na bhavāma no (syā.), purisānaṃ bharā mayaṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Ekaṃ me samaṇaṃ dehi, bhojayissāmi khattiya’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§62.</p>

```
‘‘Adāsi <pb ed="V" n="2.0272" /> me tadā rājā, samaṇaṃ bhāvitindriyaṃ;
```

```
Tassa pattaṃ gahetvāna, paramannena pūrayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§63.</p>

```
‘‘Pūretvā <pb ed="T" n="2.0383" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0602" /> paramaṃ annaṃ, saha sugandhalepanaṃ;
```

```
Mahācelena chāditvā, adāsiṃ tuṭṭhamānasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§64.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§65.</p>

```
‘‘Sahassadevarājūnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Sahassacakkavattīnaṃ, mahesittamakārayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§66.</p>

```
‘‘Padesarajjaṃ vipulaṃ, gaṇanāto asaṅkhiyaṃ;
```

```
Nānāvidhaṃ bahuṃ aññaṃ, tassa kammaphalaṃ tato.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§67.</p>

```
‘‘Uppalasseva me vaṇṇo, abhirūpā sudassanā;
```

```
Itthisabbaṅgasampannā, abhijātā jutindharā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§68.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, ajāyiṃ sākiye kule;
```

```
Nārīsahassapāmokkhā, suddhodanasutassahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§69.</p>

```
‘‘Nibbinditvā agārehaṃ, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Sattamīrattisampattā <note>sattamiṃrattimapattā (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, catusaccamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§70.</p>

```
‘‘Cīvaraṃ piṇḍapātañca, paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ;
```

```
Parimetuṃ na sakkomi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§71.</p>

```
‘‘Yaṃ mayhaṃ pūritaṃ kammaṃ, kusalaṃ sarase muni;
```

```
Tuyhatthāya mahāvīra, paricattaṃ bahuṃ mayā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§72.</p>

```
‘‘Ekattiṃse ito kappe, yaṃ dānamadadiṃ tadā;
```

```
Duggatiṃ nābhijānāmi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§73.</p>

```
‘‘Dve <pb ed="T" n="2.0384" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0285" /> gatiyo pajānāmi, devattaṃ atha mānusaṃ;
```

```
Aññaṃ gatiṃ na jānāmi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§74.</p>

```
‘‘Ucce kule pajāyāmi, mahāsāle <note>tayo sāla (ka.)</note> mahaddhane;
```

```
Aññe kule na jāyāmi, piṇḍapātassidaṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§75.</p>

```
‘‘Bhavābhave saṃsaritvā, sukkamūlena coditā;
```

```
Amanāpaṃ na passāmi, somanassakataṃ phalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§76.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="V" n="2.0273" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0603" /> ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§77.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§78.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§79.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§80.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§81.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ uppaladāyikā bhikkhunī bhagavato sammukhā imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Uppaladāyikātheriyāpadānaṃ tatiyaṃ.

#### 4. Siṅgālamātutherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§82.</p>

```
‘‘Padumuttaro <pb ed="T" n="2.0385" /> nāma jino, sabbadhammāna pāragū;
```

```
Ito satasahassamhi, kappe uppajji nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§83.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ haṃsavatiyaṃ, jātāmaccakule ahuṃ;
```

```
Nānāratanapajjote, iddhe phīte mahaddhane.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§84.</p>

```
‘‘Pitunā saha gantvāna, mahājanapurakkhatā;
```

```
Dhammaṃ buddhassa sutvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§85.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvāna <pb ed="M" n="2.0286" /> kāyena, pāpakammaṃ vivajjayiṃ;
```

```
Vacīduccaritaṃ hitvā, ājīvaṃ parisodhayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§86.</p>

```
‘‘Buddhe pasannā dhamme ca, saṅghe ca tibbagāravā;
```

```
Saddhammassavane yuttā, buddhadassanalālasā <note>buddhadassanasālayā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§87.</p>

```
‘‘Aggaṃ saddhādhimuttānaṃ, assosiṃ bhikkhuniṃ tadā;
```

```
Taṃ ṭhānaṃ patthayitvāna, tisso sikkhā apūrayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§88.</p>

```
‘‘Tato <pb ed="V" n="2.0274" /> maṃ sugato āha, karuṇānugatāsayo;
```

```
‘Yassa saddhā tathāgate, acalā suppatiṭṭhitā;
```

```
Sīlañca <pb ed="P" n="2.0604" /> yassa kalyāṇaṃ, ariyakantaṃ pasaṃsitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§89.</p>

```
‘‘‘Saṅghe pasādo yassatthi, ujubhūtañca dassanaṃ;
```

```
Adaliddoti taṃ āhu, amoghaṃ tassa jīvitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§90.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tasmā saddhañca sīlañca, pasādaṃ dhammadassanaṃ;
```

```
Anuyuñjetha <pb ed="T" n="2.0386" /> medhāvī, saraṃ buddhāna <note>buddhānusāsanaṃ (sī.), buddhānaṃ sāsanaṃ (syā.)</note> sāsanaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§91.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvāhaṃ pamuditā, apucchiṃ paṇidhiṃ mama;
```

```
Tadā anomo amito, byākarittha vināyako;
```

```
‘Buddhe pasannā kalyāṇī, lacchase taṃ supatthitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§92.</p>

```
‘‘‘Satasahassito kappe, okkākakulasambhavo;
```

```
Gotamo nāma gottena, satthā loke bhavissati.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§93.</p>

```
‘‘‘Tassa dhammesu dāyādā, orasā dhammanimmitā;
```

```
Siṅgālakassa <note>sigālakassa (sī. pī.)</note> mātāti, hessati satthu sāvikā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§94.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ sutvā muditā hutvā, yāvajīvaṃ tadā jinaṃ;
```

```
Mettacittā paricariṃ, paṭipattīhi nāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§95.</p>

```
‘‘Tena kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§96.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, giribbajapuruttame;
```

```
Jātā seṭṭhikule phīte, mahāratanasañcaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§97.</p>

```
‘‘Putto <pb ed="M" n="2.0287" /> siṅgālako nāma, mamāsi vipathe rato;
```

```
Diṭṭhigahanapakkhando, disāpūjanatapparo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§98.</p>

```
‘‘Nānādisā namassantaṃ <note>namassati (syā.)</note>, piṇḍāya nagaraṃ vajaṃ;
```

```
Taṃ disvā ovadī buddho, magge ṭhatvā vināyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§99.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa desayato dhammaṃ, panādo vimhayo ahu;
```

```
Dvekoṭinaranārīnaṃ, dhammābhisamayo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§100.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0387" /> parisaṃ gantvā, sutvā sugatabhāsitaṃ;
```

```
Sotāpattiphalaṃ pattā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§101.</p>

```
‘‘Na <pb ed="V" n="2.0275" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0605" /> cireneva kālena, buddhadassanalālasā;
```

```
Anussatiṃ taṃ bhāvetvā, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§102.</p>

```
‘‘Dassanatthāya buddhassa, sabbadā ca vajāmahaṃ;
```

```
Atittāyeva passāmi, rūpaṃ nayananandanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§103.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbapāramisambhūtaṃ, lakkhīnilayanaṃ varaṃ;
```

```
Rūpaṃ sabbasubhākiṇṇaṃ, atittā viharāmahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§104.</p>

```
‘‘Jino tasmiṃ guṇe tuṭṭho, etadagge ṭhapesi maṃ;
```

```
Siṅgālakassa yā mātā, aggā saddhādhimuttikā <note>saṃghavimuttikā (pī.), mamādhimuttikā (ka.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§105.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmuni.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§106.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§107.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§108.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§109.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§110.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="T" n="2.0388" /> catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ siṅgālamātā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Siṅgālamātutheriyāpadānaṃ catutthaṃ.

#### 5. Sukkātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§111.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito <pb ed="M" n="2.0288" /> kappe, vipassī nāma nāyako;
```

```
Uppajji cārudassano, sabbadhammavipassako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§112.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ bandhumatiyaṃ, jātā aññatare kule;
```

```
Dhammaṃ sutvāna munino, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§113.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussutā <pb ed="V" n="2.0276" /> dhammadharā, paṭibhānavatī tathā;
```

```
Vicittakathikā cāpi, jinasāsanakārikā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§114.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="P" n="2.0606" /> dhammakathaṃ katvā, hitāya janataṃ bahuṃ <note>janatāya hitaṃ bahuṃ (sī.) … sadā (syā.), hitāya janasaṃsariṃ (pī.)</note>;
```

```
Tato cutāhaṃ tusitaṃ, upapannā yasassinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§115.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, sikhī viya sikhī jino;
```

```
Tapanto yasasā loke <note>lokaṃ (syā. pī.)</note>, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§116.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāpi pabbajitvāna, buddhasāsanakovidā;
```

```
Jotetvā jinavākyāni, tatopi tidivaṃ gatā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§117.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃseva kappamhi, vessabhū nāma nāyako;
```

```
Uppajjittha mahāñāṇī, tadāpi ca tathevahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§118.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvā <pb ed="T" n="2.0389" /> dhammadharā, jotayiṃ jinasāsanaṃ;
```

```
Gantvā marupuraṃ rammaṃ, anubhosiṃ mahāsukhaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§119.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, kakusandho jinuttamo;
```

```
Uppajji narasaraṇo <note>narasaddūlo (sī. syā. pī.)</note>, tadāpi ca tathevahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§120.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvā munimataṃ, jotayitvā yathāyukaṃ;
```

```
Tato cutāhaṃ tidivaṃ, agaṃ sabhavanaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§121.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva kappamhi, koṇāgamananāyako;
```

```
Uppajji lokasaraṇo, araṇo amataṅgato <note>vadataṃ varo, sabbasattānamuttamo (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§122.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāpi pabbajitvāna, sāsane tassa tādino;
```

```
Bahussutā dhammadharā, jotayiṃ jinasāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§123.</p>

```
‘‘Imasmiṃyeva <pb ed="M" n="2.0289" /> kappamhi, kassapo munimuttamo;
```

```
Uppajji lokasaraṇo, araṇo maraṇantagū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§124.</p>

```
‘‘Tassāpi naravīrassa, pabbajitvāna sāsane;
```

```
Pariyāpuṭasaddhammā, paripucchāvisāradā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§125.</p>

```
‘‘Susīlā lajjinī ceva, tīsu sikkhāsu kovidā;
```

```
Bahuṃ dhammakathaṃ katvā, yāvajīvaṃ mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§126.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="P" n="2.0607" /> kammavipākena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§127.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="V" n="2.0277" /> ca bhave dāni, giribbajapuruttame;
```

```
Jātā seṭṭhikule phīte, mahāratanasañcaye.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§128.</p>

```
‘‘Yadā <pb ed="T" n="2.0390" /> bhikkhusahassena, parivuto lokanāyako;
```

```
Upāgami rājagahaṃ, sahassakkhena vaṇṇito.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§129.</p>

```
‘‘‘Danto dantehi saha purāṇajaṭilehi, vippamutto vippamuttehi;
```

```
Siṅgīnikkhasavaṇṇo, rājagahaṃ pāvisi bhagavā’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§130.</p>

```
‘‘Disvā buddhānubhāvaṃ taṃ, sutvāva guṇasañcayaṃ;
```

```
Buddhe cittaṃ pasādetvā, pūjayiṃ taṃ yathābalaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§131.</p>

```
‘‘Aparena ca kālena, dhammadinnāya santike;
```

```
Agārā nikkhamitvāna, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§132.</p>

```
‘‘Kesesu chijjamānesu, kilese jhāpayiṃ ahaṃ;
```

```
Uggahiṃ sāsanaṃ sabbaṃ, pabbajitvācirenahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§133.</p>

```
‘‘Tato dhammamadesesiṃ, mahājanasamāgame;
```

```
Dhamme desiyamānamhi, dhammābhisamayo ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§134.</p>

```
‘‘Nekapāṇasahassānaṃ, taṃ viditvātivimhito;
```

```
Abhippasanno me yakkho, bhamitvāna giribbajaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§135.</p>

```
‘‘Kiṃ me katā rājagahe manussā, madhuṃ pītāva acchare;
```

```
Ye sukkaṃ na upāsanti, desentiṃ amataṃ padaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§136.</p>

```
‘‘Tañca <pb ed="M" n="2.0290" /> appaṭivānīyaṃ, asecanakamojavaṃ;
```

```
Pivanti maññe sappaññā, valāhakamivaddhagū.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§137.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="T" n="2.0391" /> ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§138.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§139.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu<pb ed="P" n="2.0608" />, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§140.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0278" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§141.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§142.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ sukkā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Sukkātheriyāpadānaṃ pañcamaṃ.

Pañcamaṃ bhāṇavāraṃ.

#### 6. Abhirūpanandātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§143.</p>

```
‘‘Ekanavutito kappe, vipassī nāma nāyako;
```

```
Uppajji cārudassano, sabbadhammesu cakkhumā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§144.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ bandhumatiyaṃ, iddhe phīte mahākule;
```

```
Jātā <pb ed="T" n="2.0392" /> surūpā dayitā, pūjanīyā janassa ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§145.</p>

```
‘‘Upagantvā mahāvīraṃ, vipassiṃ lokanāyakaṃ;
```

```
Dhammaṃ suṇitvā saraṇaṃ, upesiṃ naranāyakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§146.</p>

```
‘‘Sīlesu saṃvutā hutvā, nibbute ca naruttame;
```

```
Dhātuthūpassa upari, soṇṇacchattamapūjayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§147.</p>

```
‘‘Muttacāgā sīlavatī, yāvajīvaṃ tato cutā;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsūpagā ahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§148.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="M" n="2.0291" /> dasahi ṭhānehi, adhibhotvāna sesake <note>adhibhotvā asesato (syā.)</note>;
```

```
Rūpasaddehi gandhehi, rasehi phusanehi ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§149.</p>

```
‘‘Āyunāpi ca vaṇṇena, sukhena yasasāpi ca;
```

```
Tathevādhipateyyena, adhigayha virocahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§150.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime ca bhave dāni, jātāhaṃ kapilavhaye;
```

```
Dhītā khemakasakkassa, nandā nāmāti vissutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§151.</p>

```
‘‘Abhirūpasampadampi <note>abhirupaṃ upapadaṃ (sī.), abhirupaṃ uppādaṃ (pī.)</note>, ahu me kantisūcakaṃ;
```

```
Yadāhaṃ yobbanappattā, rūpalāvaññabhūsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§152.</p>

```
‘‘Tadā <pb ed="V" n="2.0279" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0609" /> <note>tadā mamatthaṃ (sī.), idha mamatte (syā. ka.)</note> matthe sakyānaṃ, vivādo sumahā ahu;
```

```
Pabbājesi tato tāto, mā sakyā vinassiṃsuti.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§153.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvā tathāgataṃ, rūpadessiṃ naruttamaṃ;
```

```
Sutvāna nopagacchāmi, mama rūpena gabbitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§154.</p>

```
‘‘Ovādampi <pb ed="T" n="2.0393" /> na gacchāmi, buddhadassanabhīrutā;
```

```
Tadā jino upāyena, upanetvā sasantikaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§155.</p>

```
‘‘Tissitthiyo <note>tisso thīyo (sī. pī.)</note> nidassesi, iddhiyā maggakovido;
```

```
Accharārūpasadisaṃ, taruṇiṃ jaritaṃ <note>jarikaṃ (syā. ka.)</note> mataṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§156.</p>

```
‘‘Tāyo disvā susaṃviggā, virattāse kaḷevare;
```

```
Aṭṭhāsiṃ bhavanibbindā, tadā maṃ āha nāyako.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§157.</p>

```
‘‘‘Āturaṃ asuciṃ pūtiṃ, passa nande samussayaṃ;
```

```
Uggharantaṃ paggharantaṃ, bālānaṃ abhinanditaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§158.</p>

```
‘‘‘Asubhāya cittaṃ bhāvehi, ekaggaṃ susamāhitaṃ;
```

```
Yathā idaṃ tathā etaṃ, yathā etaṃ tathā idaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§159.</p>

```
‘‘‘Evametaṃ avekkhantī, rattindivamatanditā;
```

```
Tato sakāya paññāya, abhinibbijjha vacchasi’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§160.</p>

```
‘‘Tassā <pb ed="M" n="2.0292" /> me appamattāya, vicarantiyā <note>vicarantvādha (sī.), vicinantīdha (syā. pī.)</note> yoniso;
```

```
Yathābhūtaṃ ayaṃ kāyo, diṭṭho santarabāhiro.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§161.</p>

```
‘‘Atha nibbindahaṃ kāye, ajjhattañca virajjahaṃ;
```

```
Appamattā visaṃyuttā, upasantāmhi nibbutā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§162.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§163.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā<pb ed="T" n="2.0394" />, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§164.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§165.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0280" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0610" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§166.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§167.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ abhirūpanandā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Abhirūpanandātheriyāpadānaṃ chaṭṭhaṃ.

#### 7. Aḍḍhakāsitherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§168.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§169.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāhaṃ pabbajitvāna, tassa buddhassa sāsane;
```

```
Saṃvutā pātimokkhamhi, indriyesu ca pañcasu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§170.</p>

```
‘‘Mattaññunī ca asane, yuttā jāgariyepi ca;
```

```
Vasantī yuttayogāhaṃ, bhikkhuniṃ vigatāsavaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§171.</p>

```
‘‘Akkosiṃ duṭṭhacittāhaṃ, gaṇiketi bhaṇiṃ tadā;
```

```
Tena pāpena kammena, nirayamhi apaccisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§172.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="T" n="2.0395" /><pb ed="M" n="2.0293" /> kammāvasesena, ajāyiṃ gaṇikākule;
```

```
Bahusova parādhīnā, pacchimāya ca jātiyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§173.</p>

```
‘‘Kāsīsu seṭṭhikulajā, brahmacārībalenahaṃ;
```

```
Accharā viya devesu, ahosiṃ rūpasampadā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§174.</p>

```
‘‘Disvāna dassanīyaṃ maṃ, giribbajapuruttame;
```

```
Gaṇikatte nivesesuṃ, akkosanabalena me.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§175.</p>

```
‘‘Sāhaṃ sutvāna saddhammaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhena desitaṃ;
```

```
Pubbavāsanasampannā, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§176.</p>

```
‘‘Tadūpasampadatthāya, gacchantī jinasantikaṃ;
```

```
Magge dhutte ṭhite sutvā, labhiṃ dūtopasampadaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§177.</p>

```
‘‘Sabbakammaṃ <pb ed="V" n="2.0281" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0611" /> parikkhīṇaṃ, puññaṃ pāpaṃ tatheva ca;
```

```
Sabbasaṃsāramuttiṇṇā, gaṇikattañca khepitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§178.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§179.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§180.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ mama mahāvīra, uppannaṃ tava santike.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§181.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§182.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0396" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§183.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ aḍḍhakāsi bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Aḍḍhakāsitheriyāpadānaṃ sattamaṃ.

#### 8. Puṇṇikātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§184.</p>

```
‘‘Vipassino bhagavato, sikhino vessabhussa ca;
```

```
Kakusandhassa munino, koṇāgamanatādino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§185.</p>

```
‘‘Kassapassa <pb ed="M" n="2.0294" /> ca buddhassa, pabbajitvāna sāsane;
```

```
Bhikkhunī sīlasampannā, nipakā saṃvutindriyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§186.</p>

```
‘‘Bahussutā dhammadharā, dhammatthapaṭipucchikā;
```

```
Uggahetā ca dhammānaṃ, sotā payirupāsitā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§187.</p>

```
‘‘Desentī janamajjhehaṃ, ahosiṃ jinasāsane;
```

```
Bāhusaccena tenāhaṃ, pesalā atimaññisaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§188.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="V" n="2.0282" /> ca bhave dāni, sāvatthiyaṃ puruttame;
```

```
Anāthapiṇḍino gehe, jātāhaṃ kumbhadāsiyā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§189.</p>

```
‘‘Gatā udakahāriyaṃ, sotthiyaṃ dijamaddasaṃ;
```

```
Sītaṭṭaṃ toyamajjhamhi, taṃ disvā idamabraviṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§190.</p>

```
‘‘‘Udahārī <pb ed="T" n="2.0397" /><pb ed="P" n="2.0612" /> ahaṃ sīte, sadā udakamotariṃ;
```

```
Ayyānaṃ daṇḍabhayabhītā, vācādosabhayaṭṭitā <note>vācārosabhayaṭṭitā (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§191.</p>

```
‘‘‘Kassa brāhmaṇa tvaṃ bhīto, sadā udakamotari;
```

```
Vedhamānehi gattehi, sītaṃ vedayase bhusaṃ’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§192.</p>

```
‘‘‘Jānantī vata maṃ bhoti, puṇṇike paripucchasi;
```

```
Karontaṃ kusalaṃ kammaṃ, rundhantaṃ <note>niddhantaṃ (sī. pī.), nudantaṃ (syā.)</note> katapāpakaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§193.</p>

```
‘‘‘Yo ce vuḍḍho daharo vā, pāpakammaṃ pakubbati;
```

```
Dakābhisiñcanā sopi <note>bhoti (sī. ka.) therīgā. 239</note>, pāpakammā pamuccati’.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§194.</p>

```
‘‘Uttarantassa akkhāsiṃ, dhammatthasaṃhitaṃ padaṃ;
```

```
Tañca sutvā sa saṃviggo <note>susaṃviggo (syā.)</note>, pabbajitvārahā ahu.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§195.</p>

```
‘‘Pūrentī ūnakasataṃ, jātā dāsikule yato;
```

```
Tato puṇṇāti nāmaṃ me, bhujissaṃ maṃ akaṃsu te.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§196.</p>

```
‘‘Seṭṭhiṃ tatonujānetvā <note>tato anumodetvā (sī. syā.), tato anumānetvā (pī.)</note>, pabbajiṃ anagāriyaṃ;
```

```
Na cireneva kālena, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§197.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu <pb ed="M" n="2.0295" /> ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§198.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§199.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0398" /> me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§200.</p>

```
‘‘Bhāvanāya mahāpaññā, suteneva sutāvinī;
```

```
Mānena nīcakulajā, na hi kammaṃ vinassati <note>panassati (syā.)</note>.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§201.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="V" n="2.0283" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§202.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§203.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ puṇṇikā bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Puṇṇikātheriyāpadānaṃ aṭṭhamaṃ.

#### 9. Ambapālitherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§204.</p>

```
‘‘Yo <pb ed="P" n="2.0613" /> raṃsiphusitāveḷo, phusso nāma mahāmuni;
```

```
Tassāhaṃ bhaginī āsiṃ, ajāyiṃ khattiye kule.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§205.</p>

```
‘‘Tassa dhammaṃ suṇitvāhaṃ, vippasannena cetasā;
```

```
Mahādānaṃ daditvāna, patthayiṃ rūpasampadaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§206.</p>

```
‘‘Ekatiṃse ito kappe, sikhī lokagganāyako;
```

```
Uppanno lokapajjoto, tilokasaraṇo jino.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§207.</p>

```
‘‘Tadāruṇapure ramme, brāhmaññakulasambhavā;
```

```
Vimuttacittaṃ kupitā, bhikkhuniṃ abhisāpayiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§208.</p>

```
‘‘Vesikāva <pb ed="T" n="2.0399" /> anācārā, jinasāsanadūsikā;
```

```
Evaṃ akkosayitvāna, tena pāpena kammunā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§209.</p>

```
‘‘Dāruṇaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0296" /> nirayaṃ gantvā, mahādukkhasamappitā;
```

```
Tato cutā manussesu, upapannā tapassinī.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§210.</p>

```
‘‘Dasajātisahassāni, gaṇikattamakārayiṃ;
```

```
Tamhā pāpā na muccissaṃ, bhutvā duṭṭhavisaṃ yathā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§211.</p>

```
‘‘Brahmacariyamasevissaṃ <note>brahmavesamasevissaṃ (syā.), brahmaceramasevissaṃ (pī.)</note>, kassape jinasāsane;
```

```
Tena kammavipākena, ajāyiṃ tidase pure.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§212.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime bhave sampatte, ahosiṃ opapātikā;
```

```
Ambasākhantare jātā, ambapālīti tenahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§213.</p>

```
‘‘Parivutā <pb ed="V" n="2.0284" /> pāṇakoṭīhi, pabbajiṃ jinasāsane;
```

```
Pattāhaṃ acalaṃ ṭhānaṃ, dhītā buddhassa orasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§214.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, sotadhātuvisuddhiyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§215.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§216.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§217.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā <pb ed="P" n="2.0614" /> jhāpitā mayhaṃ…pe… viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§218.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="T" n="2.0400" /> vata me āsi…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§219.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā catasso…pe… kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ ambapāli bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo

Abhāsitthāti.

Ambapālitheriyāpadānaṃ navamaṃ.

#### 10. Pesalātherīapadānaṃ

<p rend="hangnum">§220.</p>

```
‘‘Imamhi bhaddake kappe, brahmabandhu mahāyaso;
```

```
Kassapo nāma gottena, uppajji vadataṃ varo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§221.</p>

```
‘‘Sāvatthiyaṃ <pb ed="M" n="2.0297" /> pure vare, upāsakakule ahaṃ;
```

```
Pasūtā taṃ <note>naṃ (syā.)</note> jinavaraṃ, disvā sutvā ca desanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§222.</p>

```
‘‘Taṃ vīraṃ saraṇaṃ gantvā, sīlāni ca samādiyiṃ;
```

```
Kadāci so mahāvīro, mahājanasamāgame.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§223.</p>

```
‘‘Attano abhisambodhiṃ, pakāsesi narāsabho;
```

```
Ananussutadhammesu, pubbe dukkhādikesu ca.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§224.</p>

```
‘‘Cakkhu ñāṇañca paññā ca, vijjāloko ca āsi me;
```

```
Taṃ sutvā uggahetvāna, paripucchiñca bhikkhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§225.</p>

```
‘‘Tena <pb ed="V" n="2.0285" /> kammena sukatena, cetanāpaṇidhīhi ca;
```

```
Jahitvā mānusaṃ dehaṃ, tāvatiṃsamagacchahaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§226.</p>

```
‘‘Pacchime <pb ed="T" n="2.0401" /> ca bhave dāni, jātā seṭṭhimahākule;
```

```
Upecca buddhaṃ saddhammaṃ, sutvā saccūpasaṃhitaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§227.</p>

```
‘‘Pabbajitvācireneva, saccatthāni <note>sabbatthāni (syā. ka.)</note> vicintayaṃ;
```

```
Khepetvā āsave sabbe, arahattamapāpuṇiṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§228.</p>

```
‘‘Iddhīsu ca vasī homi, dibbāya sotadhātuyā;
```

```
Cetopariyañāṇassa, vasī homi mahāmune.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§229.</p>

```
‘‘Pubbenivāsaṃ jānāmi, dibbacakkhu visodhitaṃ;
```

```
Sabbāsavaparikkhīṇā, natthi dāni punabbhavo.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§230.</p>

```
‘‘Atthadhammaniruttīsu, paṭibhāne tatheva ca;
```

```
Ñāṇaṃ me vimalaṃ suddhaṃ, buddhaseṭṭhassa vāhasā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§231.</p>

```
‘‘Kilesā jhāpitā mayhaṃ, bhavā sabbe samūhatā;
```

```
Nāgīva bandhanaṃ chetvā, viharāmi anāsavā.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§232.</p>

```
‘‘Svāgataṃ <pb ed="P" n="2.0615" /> vata me āsi, mama buddhassa santike;
```

```
Tisso vijjā anuppattā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ.
```

<p rend="hangnum">§233.</p>

```
‘‘Paṭisambhidā <pb ed="M" n="2.0298" /> catasso, vimokkhāpi ca aṭṭhime;
```

```
Chaḷabhiññā sacchikatā, kataṃ buddhassa sāsanaṃ’’.
```

Itthaṃ sudaṃ pesalā <note>selā (syā. pī.)</note> bhikkhunī imā gāthāyo abhāsitthāti.

Pesalātheriyāpadānaṃ dasamaṃ.

<trailer rend="centre">Khattiyāvaggo catuttho.</trailer>

Tassuddānaṃ –

```
Khattiyā <pb ed="T" n="2.0402" /> brāhmaṇī ceva, tathā uppaladāyikā;
```

```
Siṅgālamātā sukkā ca, abhirūpā aḍḍhakāsikā.
```

```
Puṇṇā ca ambapālī ca, pesalāti ca tā dasa;
```

```
Gāthāyo dvisatānettha, dvicattālīsa cuttari.
```

Atha <pb ed="V" n="2.0286" /> vagguddānaṃ –

```
Sumedhā ekūposathā, kuṇḍalakesī khattiyā;
```

```
Sahassaṃ tisatā gāthā, sattatālīsa piṇḍitā.
```

```
Saha uddānagāthāhi, gaṇitāyo vibhāvibhi;
```

```
Sahassaṃ tisataṃ gāthā, sattapaññāsameva cāti.
```

<trailer rend="centre">Therikāpadānaṃ samattaṃ.</trailer>

Apadānapāḷi samattā.
